Chapter 902: Nameless Sword Cultivators

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, several of my senior brothers and sisters have long wanted to meet you. Would it be convenient for you?”

“Sure, let’s go meet them then.” Lu Yang smiled, sheathing the Qingfeng Sword and casually hanging it at his waist.

Previously, Lu Yang had tried not to reveal the Qingfeng Sword. As it was an immortal blade refined by Wu Yao, he was worried it would be recognized by Great Yu cultivators, thereby inviting trouble.

For instance, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord attacked the Dao-Seeking Sect after recognizing the Qingfeng Sword and deducing that the sect possessed the immortal treasure left behind by Wu Yao.

Now, Lu Yang had no such concerns. Everyone who knew the Qingfeng Sword’s origin was imprisoned at Incarceration Peak; no one in the outside world could recognize it.

Yun Mengmeng gazed at the Qingfeng Sword, a thoughtful expression on her visage.

“Miss Yun, what are you thinking?” Lu Yang noticed her reaction.

“Do you remember that sister I mentioned earlier?”

“The one incredibly formidable at fighting?”

“Yes. She actually likes swords quite a bit. She secretly practiced for a while and studied plenty of theory. However, she never achieved much, not even grasping the fundamentals. Eventually, she gave up.”

Lu Yang chuckled. “That’s just how the Sword Dao is. Effort alone doesn’t guarantee success; talent and comprehension are both integral. It suggests that your sister’s sword talent is pretty average.

“That said, since she’s interested in Sword Dao, I could offer some guidance. I’m not trying to boast, but I have some talent in Sword Dao. Among the younger generation of the cultivation world, few surpass me.”

Hearing this, Mingtai smiled too. “Senior Brother Lu Yang is being modest. Among the younger generation, I doubt anyone’s talent in Sword Dao exceeds yours.

“Perhaps that Young Creed Leader Lu comes close, but he’s from the ancient era; strictly speaking, he’s not from our generation.”

“That’s wonderful then.” Yun Mengmeng was happy for her good friend. According to her, she also belongs to the younger generation, so her talent definitely falls short of Lu Yang’s. This is a perfect chance for Lu Yang to teach her.

Little Zhi always brings gifts home; this time, I’m reciprocating by finding her a shifu.

~~~

The Sword Tower had eighteen floors altogether. The first eight were open to visitors; sword cultivators attending the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony could choose rooms here to stay for a few days, with cultivation resources provided by the Sword Tower.

Floors nine to twelve were for inner and true lineage disciples. As the Sword Tower’s core area, they were not easily accessible to outsiders.

Mingtai brought Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng to the twelfth floor.

“Who are those two? Why can they go up?”

Sword cultivators exchanging insights on the eighth floor were astonished. From Mingtai’s clothing, he was clearly an inner disciple, but Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng were obviously outsiders.

“Why does one of them look like Lu Yang?”

“He’s Lu Yang? Right, I’ve seen his portrait—that is Lu Yang!”

“I heard that when he was at the East Sea, he had already comprehended Sword Dao to the point where all things could become a sword. He even used people as swords to execute One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords!”

“He was only at the Nascent Soul Stage then, wasn’t he? To perform One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords at that level is truly terrifying.”

Those eligible to attend the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony were all prodigies of their respective regions and unmatched in Sword Dao, inevitably carrying some pride. Yet compared to Lu Yang, they were like novices showing off before a master, unable to muster even the will to compete with him.

A nameless sword cultivator sitting in a corner curled his lips into an enigmatic smile. “Lu Yang, eh? I wonder if he’s worthy to test my sword.”

In another corner, another nameless cultivator’s eyes were fixed on Lu Yang until the latter vanished up the stairs. “Looks like he’s nothing special.”

The former nameless cultivator took offense. “Hey, watch your words. Lu Yang is the opponent I’ve chosen. Are you saying my test subject is mediocre?”

The latter nameless sword cultivator sneered coldly. “And what if I am?!”

The two nameless sword cultivators glared fiercely at each other, their right hands silently gripping their sword hilts, poised to draw their swords at any moment.

Just then, an outer Sword Tower disciple led an elder to the eighth floor, pointing at the two nameless cultivators in the corner. “Elder, it’s these two. When registering at the entrance, they refused to give their names and sneaked into our Sword Tower!”

The elder looked down at them imperiously. “So you two entered without registering. Shall I escort you out, or will you leave on your own?”

One nameless cultivator smirked disdainfully at the elder. “Chase me out? Is this the Sword Tower’s hospitality? Do you know who I am...”

Without another word, the elder opened a window and tossed them both out.

“Lunatics. You wouldn’t give your names during registration, and now you want to? Too late.”

~~~

“Senior Sister Little Mi, Senior Brother Yu...look who I’ve brought.”

Mingtai led Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng to a stone chamber on the twelfth floor, where six people gathered. Apart from Mingtai, they were the most talented disciples of the Sword Tower.

“Greetings, fellow Daoists. I am Lu Yang.” Lu Yang inverted the Qingfeng Sword and cupped his hands in salute.

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, your reputation precedes you.” The six Sword Tower prodigies rose and returned the salute, genuinely elated to meet him.

“This is Miss Yun. She’s traveling with me for now.”

“Greetings, Miss Yun.”

“Hello.” Yun Mengmeng stood quietly to the side. I know little of the outside world; speaking too much may make me a laughingstock.

“Come, come, come, let me introduce them to you, Senior Brother Lu Yang. This is Senior Sister Mi Li[1]—everyone likes to call her Senior Sister Little Mi.”

Lu Yang noticed that Mi Li’s aura fluctuated, rising and falling unstably, indicating she was at the Void Refinement Stage.

“This is Senior Brother Yue Chuan, the Tower Leader’s closed-left-door disciple.”

Yue Chuan resembled a libertine, openly embracing a woman in public without any sense of impropriety.

“This is Senior Brother Li Tang, the Tower Leader’s closed-right-door disciple.”

Li Tang was reticent, cradling a sword, his hair tied in a high ponytail. He merely nodded to Lu Yang without speaking, exuding the aura of a sword cultivator.

Yun Mengmeng couldn’t help but ask, “What are a ‘closed-left-door disciple’ and a ‘closed-right-door disciple?’”

“When the Tower Leader decided to take only one person as his closed-door disciple, both senior brothers were excellent, and it was hard to choose, so he accepted both.

“The Tower Leader said that since closing a gate requires closing two doors, taking in two disciples was perfectly normal.

“Senior Brother Li Tang is shy and unwilling to speak. Please don’t mind, Senior Brother Lu Yang.”

After a round of introductions, Mingtai still hadn’t introduced the woman in Yue Chuan’s arms, which Lu Yang found odd.

“And this is?”

“Oh, I forgot to introduce. This is a sword spirit nurtured by Senior Brother Yue Chuan—truly remarkable. Senior Brother Yue Chuan is strengthening his communion with the sword spirit. He’s the only disciple of our generation with a sword spirit.”

1. “Mili” literally means rice grain. ☜

Chapter 903: Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony

It was Lu Yang’s first time seeing a bona fide sword spirit—a far cry from the counterfeit one residing in the Qingfeng Sword.

Yue Chuan’s sword spirit was undoubtedly of a high caliber; otherwise, Lu Yang wouldn’t have been able to perceive its uniqueness.

Yue Chuan smiled, unable to conceal his pride. “In the early days of my cultivation, I was fortunate to obtain a sword with a perfect spiritual nature. By nurturing it with my heart, I gradually cultivated A’Lan.”

His personal sword was called the Lanyan Sword, so the spirit named herself A’Lan.

To deepen their bond, he embraced A’Lan during the day and used sword-nurturing techniques to take care of her body at night. Countless people envied him.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t bear seeing Lu Yang being outshone. “As if no one else has a sword spirit! Xiao Yangzi, show them to me and broaden their horizons!”

Our Great Dou Dynasty is vast, rich with resources, and sparsely populated. As a pillar minister and future Dou Emperor, how could Xiao Yangzi lack a sword with a sword spirit?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that she was quite a competent emperor. I serve as Xiao Yangzi’s second nascent soul, and now I’m his sword spirit for appearances. Surely no emperor in history has been so attentive to a minister.

“No, no, please don’t! Immortal Fairy, just rest and recuperate in the Qingfeng Sword,” Lu Yang hastily dissuaded her. If she reveals herself, and others ask how I communicate and bond with my sword spirit, wouldn’t everything be exposed?

Mi Li and the others discussed Sword Dao with Lu Yang, feeling that they had met too late. His unique insights left them with a sudden sense of enlightenment.

A day passed in a flash.

“Let’s go. The Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony is about to begin.” Mi Li led the group downstairs.

The venue was temporarily constructed beside the Sword Tower, adjacent to the sword vault.

According to Mingtai, the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony was the same as in previous years, divided into three segments. The first was the tower leader’s address. The second was the Sword Seeking segment itself; it wasn’t a competition of cultivation level but pure comprehension of the Sword Dao. The third was visiting the sword vault to resonate with spirit swords.

For attending sword cultivators, the second segment was the main draw. It was a chance to prove their Sword Dao comprehension to the world, representing absolute honor.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest had once claimed first at a Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony, then advanced rapidly and defeated the Sword Tower Leader, earning the title of number one in Sword Dao.

“Take my sword!”

“Kunlun Sword Art!”

“Heaven-Earth Single Sword!”

“Peacock Display Sword Art!”

Many sword cultivators seized the brief time before the ceremony to spar, swords clashing at the venue.

Some executed majestic strikes that could rip space, while others demonstrated sword techniques resembling peacock displays, hiding true attacks among countless feints. There was even an octopus that wielded eight swords and spun like an iron top, preventing anyone from approaching.

Previously, Lu Yang had only encountered rogue cultivators here and there, so it didn’t leave much of an impression on him. Now, with the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony formally underway and sword cultivators from across the world gathered here, he was awed by the overwhelming sword intent in the air.

Aside from exceptions like the Taciturn Daoist Priest, most sword cultivators appeared aloof and taciturn because their hearts were wholly devoted to the sword, leaving no common ground with others.

At the Sword Tower, these sword cultivators finally found kindred spirits and came together in small groups. Most hadn’t known each other before, yet a few words engendered friendships.

This was another reason the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony drew this much attention from sword cultivators.

Every sword cultivator possessed a unique intent. When these intents gathered, they would automatically coalesce into a soaring sword intent that dispersed the clouds without employing a single trace of power, revealing a clear sky above.

Lu Yang gazed at the blazing sun overhead. Couldn’t you at least leave me a patch of cloud? Back in my previous life, even our drill instructors during military training had the decency to pick a shaded spot for us to stand at attention.

If not for the inappropriate setting, Lu Yang would have executed One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords to block out the sun.

The Sword Tower Leader stood at the highest point and addressed the crowd. Lu Yang couldn’t make out the words because Mingtai kept transmitting him auditory messages, introducing key sword cultivators to pay attention to.

“That tall, thin one in green is Duan Changqing from the Demon Region, a bamboo that turned into a demon spirit. He carved a section of his own body into a bamboo sword, using himself as a weapon.”

It was challenging for spirit plants to gain sentience, but once they did, they would be endowed with talents blessed by the heavens. Among spirit plants that became demon spirits, the one with the highest attainment was none other than the Epoch Immortal.

Though he was now reincarnated as Li Haoran and constantly on Su Yiren’s mind.

“That androgynous one is Kun Qiu of the Hundun Tribe. It’s said that he is highly regarded by their tribe’s Transcendent Tribulation ancestor and has been confirmed as the next tribe chieftain.”

Lu Yang stole a couple more glances at Kun Qiu. He had encountered Hundun Tribe prodigies in the Demon Region’s Creation Ancient Domain, but he was too busy fighting back then to note their race.

Kun Qiu wasn’t among those Hundun Tribe prodigies he had met. Lu Yang estimated that the other party’s age and cultivation level exceeded his own, though he couldn’t tell by how much.

Hundun’s gender was fluid, shifting between male and female, often appearing androgynous. This caused others to keep their distance.

Kun Qiu sensed Lu Yang’s gaze. When he turned to look at Lu Yang, the latter hurriedly snapped his head back.

“Kun Qiu, what’s wrong?” a large black dog beside him asked.

He was a prodigy from the Heavenly Dog Tribe and held a sword in his mouth. As he had practiced the sword in his original form since childhood, he still preferred it even after learning to shapeshift.

Kun Qiu muttered, “I felt someone watching me. It was probably my imagination.”

“Maybe they’re guessing your gender again.” The large black dog chuckled slyly. In the Demon Region, demons often speculated about Kun Qiu’s gender. freewebnovel.com

Kun Qiu shot the dog a sidelong glance. “Shut up. You’re drooling.”

Holding a sword in one’s mouth had one major drawback—the tendency to drool.

“That’s Xuan Xuan of the East Sea’s Xuanwu Tribe. They’re known for defense, yet he’s abandoned it and become obsessed with the sword. It’s said that even his peers’ turtle shells can’t withstand his blade.”

Xuan Xuan was dark and burly, carrying a broadsword on his back, with a small turtle he had drawn on the hilt.

At the Old Dragon Emperor’s birthday banquet, Lu Yang had seen the Xuanwu Tribe’s Transcendent Tribulation chieftain, but not its younger generation.

Seeing that the Sword Tower Leader was still speaking, Yun Mengmeng opened some oil paper, took out two pastries, and ate them stealthily. Lu Yang had bought them for her on the way to the Sword Tower.

Finally, the Sword Tower Leader announced the much-anticipated segment. “Next, we’ll proceed to the second segment—the Sword Seeking!”

Lu Yang revealed a confident yet restrained smile. He hoped to avoid fighting demons during the Sword Seeking segment. As Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi’s senior brother, engaging in battle with younger demons would undermine my status.

Chapter 904: Sword Heart

After announcing the commencement of the second segment, the Sword Tower Leader continued, “A sword cultivator is not merely a cultivator who uses a sword as a weapon. If that were the case, who in this world wouldn’t be a sword cultivator?”

Lu Yang nodded inwardly. What the Sword Tower Leader said is right. Which cultivator hasn’t dreamed of being a sword immortal? They simply tried to use the sword as a weapon but found it unsuitable, so they gave up.

“Then does a sword cultivator refer to someone talented in Sword Dao? Not entirely either.

“A true sword cultivator not only possesses talent beyond ordinary people in Sword Dao, but also harbors a Sword Heart—that is, your attitude toward your sword!”

“There’s such a theory as Sword Heart?” Lu Yang was puzzled. I’ve never heard Shifu or Big Senior Sister mention it.

He felt that he really should attend more sword cultivator gatherings. I may not get to see Shifu even once a year, and after the Foundation Establishment Stage, Big Senior Sister has stopped teaching me sword techniques. As for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it goes without saying that she knows nothing about the Sword Dao.

“The Sword Seeking is divided into two parts: seeking the sword through the heart and seeking the sword through the intent.”

“Seeking the sword through the heart tests one’s Sword Heart.”

After hearing the Sword Tower Leader’s words, Lu Yang felt somewhat uneasy. If it were a competition of sword intent, I’d fear no one. But I’m hearing this “Sword Heart” thing for the first time. What should I do?

An array appeared beneath every sword cultivator’s feet, shooting a curtain of light upward and enveloping them.

“This is the Heart-Seeking Array. Within it, one cannot lie when answering any question concerning the ‘sword.’“

This was one of the Sword Tower’s heritage, an array that the Sword Tower Supreme Lord had unintentionally comprehended while ruminating on Sword Dao. It greatly aided one’s Sword Heart.

Lu Yang felt that this array shared some similarities with his Clear Heart True Nature Mantra, though it was more mysterious and profound.

The Heart-Seeking Array could distinguish truth from falsehood, but couldn’t initiate questions. The Sword Tower had twelve elders and one tower leader—thirteen in total—who personally stepped forward to test all the sword cultivators.

Among them, none drew more attention than the Sword Tower Leader. The sword cultivators he chose to test signified that he regarded them favorably to some extent.

The Sword Tower Leader first approached the bamboo demon spirit Duan Changqing. “Duan Changqing, do you cultivate the Heartful Sword Dao or the Heartless Sword Dao?”

“The Heartless Sword Dao.”

“If your sword breaks, would you be sad?”

Duan Changqing replied coldly, “If the sword breaks, I’ll just forge another. Why would I be sad?”

“Then do you like the Sword Dao?”

“Of course, I like it.”

The array beneath Duan Changqing’s feet blazed with glaring red light, indicating he lied.

The Sword Tower Leader spoke sternly, his eyes like swords seeming to pierce through Duan Changqing. “Say the truth.”

Unable to withstand the pressure, Duan Changqing confessed honestly. “I became a sword cultivator only because a sword cultivator’s offensive power is very strong.”

The Sword Tower Leader sighed. “Your sword was forged from part of your body. This certainly aids your mastery of the sword, but you feel no emotion for the Sword Dao. This will block your future path.”

He then approached his closed-left-gate disciple, Yue Chuan. The latter took out the Lanyan Sword, its sword spirit A’Lan nestled in his arms.

He knew Yue Chuan well, so there was no need to ask which Sword Dao he cultivated.

“Yue Chuan, can you live and die together with your sword?”

Looking at A’Lan in his arms, Yue Chuan declared firmly, “I can!”

“Then what is your relationship with your sword?”

Yue Chuan replied without hesitation, “I want to marry A’Lan!”

The Sword Tower Leader pressed a hand to his forehead. Asking Yue Chuan was just a formality. How could I not know what my eldest disciple is like? If it weren’t for the Great Xia’s laws not recognizing sword spirits as marriageable entities, the two would have wed long ago.

“Mingtai, can you live and die together with your sword?” The Sword Tower Leader’s tone was genial. In terms of seniority, unless the Sword Tower Supreme Lord revived, even if all past tower leaders were dug out, none would outrank Mingtai.

“I can!” Mingtai held the Hanguang Sword—the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s personal sword and Mingtai’s original form. If anything happened to it, he wouldn’t survive.

“What is your relationship with your sword?”

“We are one entity.”

An uproar broke out from the crowd. The array showed no reaction, indicating that Mingtai hadn’t lied. Hearing his answer, countless cultivators felt ashamed. Although their feelings for their swords were sincere, compared to Mingtai’s, they still fell far short.

“Greetings, Tower Leader Guan.” Seeing him approach, Lu Yang hastily bowed.

The Sword Tower Leader’s name was Guan Yi.

“So you are Lu Yang? This is our first meeting.” The Sword Tower Leader smiled at Lu Yang.

Although he had conflicts with the Taciturn Daoist Priest, those were matters between seniors and unrelated to the younger generation. As the Sword Tower Leader, nothing delighted him more than seeing talented young sword cultivators grow.

With Lu Yang currently in the spotlight, the Sword Tower Leader’s words immediately attracted everyone’s attention.

“He really is Lu Yang.”

“I wonder what Lu Yang’s Sword Heart is like.”

“With Mingtai setting the bar, even if his Sword Heart is excellent, it can’t surpass Mingtai’s, right?”

Tower Leader Guan asked, “Your shifu cultivates the Heartless Sword Dao. What about you, Lu Yang? Do you cultivate the Heartful Sword Dao or the Heartless Sword Dao?”

Lu Yang hesitated. This was his first time hearing that the Sword Dao was divided into heartful and heartless paths. “May I first ask what the Heartful Sword Dao and the Heartless Sword Dao are?”

“Your shifu didn’t even tell you this?” Tower Leader Guan was somewhat displeased with the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Too irresponsible. Nevertheless, he began to explain.

“A sword cultivator certainly loves their sword, but that love can be categorized.

“The Heartful Sword Dao refers to treating the sword as a person and loving it like a beloved. Everyone in our Sword Tower cultivates this path.

“On the other hand, the Heartless Sword Dao refers to treating the sword as an object, simply loving it as a thing. The most famous practitioner of this path is your shifu.”

Lu Yang pondered over it. Although the Qingfeng Sword is a gift from Big Senior Sister and I like it, I ultimately regard it as an object, with no special feelings.

“In that case, I’m probably cultivating the Heartless Sword Dao.”

Hearing that, Tower Leader Guan was slightly unhappy. So it really is the case, huh? Lu Yang is such a promising seedling, yet that old Taciturn scoundrel has taught him the Heartless Sword Dao.

But then, the array beneath Lu Yang flashed red.

“Hmm? Did you just lie?” Tower Leader Guan’s face lit up with joy. Doesn’t this mean that Lu Yang is actually cultivating the Heartful Sword Dao?

“I lied?” Lu Yang was equally surprised. By Tower Leader Guan’s definition, I clearly fit the Heartless Sword Dao.

Tower Leader Guan guided him patiently and gently. “Do you like your sword?”

Lu Yang nodded. I do like the Qingfeng Sword.

“Do you treat your sword as a person?”

Lu Yang was about to shake his head when he suddenly realized the issue—there was a person inside the Qingfeng Sword!

Lu Yang could only nod again.

Tower Leader Guan clapped his hands, concluding on Lu Yang’s behalf. “Isn’t that it then?! You like your sword and treat it as a person—that is the Heartful Sword Dao!

“Suppose your sword broke or vanished. Would you be sad and weep bitterly?”

Lu Yang considered the scenario. If the Everlasting Immortal Fairy vanished, I would indeed be sad and probably even cry.

He could only nod again.

“See? This isn’t just the Heartful Sword Dao—you’ve reached the profound realm of entrusting your emotions to the sword!”

Inside the Qingfeng Sword, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy giggled foolishly. She was unsure why, but his answers made her elated.

“Then are you willing to live and die together with your sword?”

Within the Heartful Sword Dao, a small subset of sword cultivators, such as Yue Chuan and Mingtai, held extreme feelings for their swords, advocating ‘sword exists, I exist; sword perishes, I perish.’ Sword cultivators had historically revered such extreme emotions.

Hearing this question, Lu Yang’s expression turned peculiar, uncertain how to respond. “It’s not about living and dying together. Even if I die, my sword cannot die.”

Given the Everlasting Dao Fruit’s heaven-defying nature, it’ll be hard for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to die even if she wants to.

Tower Leader Guan praised Lu Yang’s answer effusively. “Fantastic! Protecting your sword with your life, preventing your sword from suffering any harm, even at the expense of your life!”

Everyone turned their gazes to Lu Yang with respect. Only sword cultivators could grasp what his answer meant. This surpassed even “sword exists, I exist; sword perishes, I perish.”

“As expected of Lu Yang! With such devotion, which sword cultivator today can match him?”

“Earlier, I thought he only had talent in Sword Dao, with no feelings for his sword. I was mistaken!”

“No wonder he could perform One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords and One Person Into Ten Thousand Persons at the Nascent Soul Stage. Apart from his talent in Sword Dao, his feelings for the sword surely played a pivotal role!”

Tower Leader Guan threw out his final question. “Then what is your relationship with your sword?”

Lu Yang felt that telling the truth would be embarrassing, but the array would detect falsehood, so he could only answer honestly. “The sword is the sovereign, I am the subject.”

Another uproar erupted from the crowd, even louder than when it was Mingtai’s turn. Faces were filled with utter disbelief as they stared at Lu Yang.

“Treating the sword as the sovereign—this is the legendary realm of Person and Sword as One and Body Moves With Sword!”

“No one in history has ever reached this level, right?!”

Sword cultivators were proud. No matter how well they treated their swords, they simply placed them on equal footing, never above themselves.

To set aside a sword cultivator’s pride for the sword—what a Sword Heart!

The more Tower Leader Guan looked at Lu Yang, the more pleasing to the eye he found him. The sword foremost, and the cultivator secondary; not even the Sword Tower Supreme Lord had cultivated the Heartful Sword Dao to this level!

Chapter 905: Sword Seeking Through the Intent

Mingtai gazed at Lu Yang with even more reverence. My Sword Heart is already rare in this world, yet Senior Brother Lu Yang’s feelings for his sword surpass even my own.

Throughout history—even in the enigmatic ancient era, and including the ancient Qin Sword Venerable—perhaps none had ever been like Senior Brother Lu Yang.

The only uncertainty is the Qilin Immortal. It’s said that he used a sword, but it is unknown whether he merely wielded it as a weapon or was a sword cultivator. If the Qilin Immortal were a sword cultivator, it would be unclear whose Sword Heart would be superior—his or Senior Brother Lu Yang’s.

Cultivating to reach immortality required unique insights into Sword Dao and Sword Heart.

“This Sword Heart is number one throughout the ages,” someone murmured, and many others immediately echoed.

“Lu Yang’s Sword Heart is number one throughout the ages!”

“Sword as the sovereign, Lu Yang as the subject—his Sword Heart is number one throughout the ages!”

Even the Sword Tower elders cast approving glances at Lu Yang, feeling that with his sword cultivation alone, he was worthy of having his name resound throughout the ages, serving as a role model for all future sword cultivators.

The slogans varied but shared the same essence, rising into a thunderous chorus like crashing waves. Embarrassed, Lu Yang lowered his head, curling his toes within his shoes.

It feels like everyone is calling me the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s subject.

Lu Yang regretted attending the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony. I shouldn’t have insisted on finding an excuse to travel; staying at the Dao-Seeking Sect would have been fine.

Yun Mengmeng didn’t understand Sword Dao well, but from everyone’s reactions, she could tell that Lu Yang’s Sword Heart was extraordinary.

She felt somewhat proud. “I’ve found a good teacher for Little Zhi. Granny even worried that I'd encounter accidents outside. With my luck, how could anything happen?”

With Lu Yang hailed as possessing the number one Sword Heart throughout the ages, any other sword cultivator’s answers truly couldn’t compare.

“See? It’s all thanks to this immortal that your Sword Heart is so amazing, Xiao Yangzi.”

Lu Yang ignored his sword spirit’s shameless claim.

“The sword seeking through the heart segment has concluded. I believe I don’t need to say whose Sword Heart is the most admirable.” Tower Leader Guan smiled, his gaze inadvertently falling on Lu Yang. If he could beat the Taciturn Daoist Priest, he would want to steal Lu Yang as his own disciple.

But come to think of it, it’s said that Yun Zhi cherishes this little junior brother dearly. Even if I could beat the Taciturn Daoist Priest, I probably can’t beat her.

Forget it. Lu Yang is fine staying in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Next, we’ll begin the sword seeking through the intent segment.”

The Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony was held once in a century. If it were one-on-one battles of sword techniques, those who had cultivated the longest would surely win, rendering the contest meaningless. Thus, the Sword Tower Supreme Lord proposed suppressing everyone’s cultivation to the same level, competing purely through sword intent.

Lu Yang felt a frightening pressure. It swept across the entire venue, suppressing everyone to the Golden Core Stage. Then, the earth trembled as eighteen platforms burst forth, encircling the Sword Tower.

Tower Leader Guan explained, “These eighteen platforms were forged by the first tower leader. You only need to place a strand of sword qi on them, and it will manifest as a sword-intent avatar, which you can control in battle.”

“These are the legendary sword intent arena platforms?” The sword cultivators’ eyes gleamed at the sight of the eighteen platforms that were as smooth as mirrors.

These were supreme treasures left by the Sword Tower Supreme Lord. Prolonged cultivation atop them could hone one’s sword intent, making it sharper.

It was Lu Yang’s first time seeing these, but he could grasp their significance by hearing the discussions in his surroundings.

After drawing lots, Lu Yang was assigned to the second group and would have to wait for the first group’s matches to finish before it was his turn.

He recalled the key cultivators Mingtai had mentioned—among the first group was Xuan Xuan of the Xuanwu Tribe.

Xuan Xuan carried a heavy, broad black sword on his back, with a small turtle drawn on its hilt. When he walked, it felt as though the ground quaked and the mountains shook.

Lu Yang also recognized Xuan Xuan’s opponent. It was the octopus with eight swords coiled in its tentacles.

“Wu’er, I didn’t expect to meet you here.” Xuan Xuan grinned, revealing eight white teeth.

Both he and the octopus were sword cultivators from the East Sea. They had heard of each other’s reputation before, but never exchanged blows.

“Xuan Xuan, they all say my Sword Dao is inferior to yours. I never found the chance, but today, I’ll dispel that rumor!”

“What rumor? They’re simply speaking the truth. How could you compare to me?”

Wu’er attacked first. Tentacles coiled around eight swords, spinning wildly without an opening. Those who had sparred with him before the ceremony couldn’t strike his main body.

Xuan Xuan yelled and hefted his black sword, swinging it at Wu’er.

Clang!

Such a strike would trouble any sword cultivator, but upon reaching Wu’er, the sword was deflected by the rapidly spinning eight swords.

“There’s indeed some substance.” Xuan Xuan grew intrigued. Sword cultivators were known for offense, yet Wu’er adopted the opposite approach—defense.

“Isn’t it just spinning? Anyone can do that!” Xuan Xuan reverted to his original form—a black turtle with a serpent’s body.

He flipped over, resting on his raised shell. Head tucked into the shell, he gripped the sword hilt with his mouth and used his tail to push off the ground, sending himself whirling.

As his tail struck the ground with increasing speed and force, Xuan Xuan spun increasingly faster until his head and tail blurred into one. Using his tail to accelerate and steer, he charged at Wu’er, knocking him over.

Wu’er also grew furious. This move has never failed. It’s my first time getting knocked down.

“You think I fear you?!”

The two seafolk spun and collided like iron tops. Whoever was sent flying would muster strength to slam back into their opponent.

Lu Yang watched Xuan Xuan and Wu’er with admiration, surprised to witness such fusion battle techniques here. But these two seafolk were even more impressive; they could spin individually, which was far more convenient.

Observing that the two iron tops were unlikely to decide a victor anytime soon, Lu Yang circled the Sword Tower to observe other arena platforms.

“Little Feng! Why...why are you here?!” One sword cultivator looked terrified upon seeing his opponent’s face and name.

The one named Little Feng smiled stiffly. “Brother Lin, I told you we’d meet again. Did you think I wouldn’t be able to find you just because you changed your name? I knew you’d definitely attend this centennial Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony!

“Blood debts must be repaid in blood. Let’s settle this with our life and death on this arena platform today!”

~~~

“Big Senior Brother! I never thought we’d meet on this arena platform. Do you remember our pact? The winner gets to confess to Little Junior Sister!”

“Second Junior Brother, who Little Junior Sister likes is her own affair. Don’t let the result of our duel decide her marriage!”

“Enough talk! Let’s fight!”

~~~

“Big Brother, you stole my spirit root and pushed me off a cliff twenty years ago. You never thought I’d survive, did you?!”

“So what if you’re still alive? You’re nothing but worthless trash without a spirit root. There’s no way you can beat me!”

“Kekeke. You’ll probably never understand the meaning of ‘break to rebuild.’”

“...” Lu Yang. Sword Tower, you didn’t rig the draw for the matchups, did you?

Chapter 906: A Tenacious Opponent

Tower Leader Guan fell into deep contemplation at the sight.

How can we possibly investigate every sword cultivator’s background? The Sword Tower lacks an intelligence department like the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Great Mission Hall; we can’t check them all. Besides, such situations had never arisen in any past Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony.

Strange. A Sword Tower elder sensed something unusual about this year’s ceremony and secretly transmitted an auditory message to Tower Leader Guan. “Tower Leader, this may be an ill omen. Should we make some preparations?”

Tower Leader Guan nodded, agreeing with the elder’s assessment. Matters at this year’s ceremony have exceeded the Sword Tower’s capabilities. “It’s indeed an ill omen. Notify the authorities first and have them send more personnel, lest they lack manpower to make arrests.”

The Sword Tower isn’t one of the Five Great Immortal Sects; we lack enforcement authority.

~~~

Aside from the numerous irreconcilable conflicts among the respective sword cultivators, the first group’s matches had nothing else noteworthy.

Xuan Xuan and Wu’er’s iron top duel attracted many eyeballs. As the two seafolk clashed to their limits, Wu’er activated his hidden bloodline, and an ancestor’s phantom appeared overhead, granting him new strength and giving him the upper hand. Next, Xuan Xuan also activated his hidden bloodline, summoning his ancestor’s phantom, turning the tide, and gaining the advantage.

In the end, Xuan Xuan’s last strike prevailed, securing victory.

With that, the first group’s matches concluded.

Since everyone had fought using sword-intent avatars, even if they killed their opponent, it merely caused their sword intent to collapse and didn’t pose a danger to their lives.

Of course, if they sought revenge in private afterward, that couldn’t be helped.

Compared to the first group, the second group’s matches drew more interest. It featured Mingtai and Lu Yang, two widely acclaimed young Sword Dao rising stars. People had only heard legends, and this would be their first glimpse of them in action.

However, the most conspicuous was Yue Chuan, who brought his sword spirit A’Lan directly onto the arena. As sword spirits were considered part of the sword, this didn’t violate the rules.

Lu Yang didn’t let his sword spirit—the Everlasting Immortal Fairy—make an appearance. If she does, forget the sword cultivators participating this year, even all sword cultivators from past ceremonies combined wouldn’t be enough to take her on.

I, Lu Yang, am upright and aboveboard; I don’t rely on superficial external forces.

Lu Yang’s opponent was a somewhat oddly dressed cultivator, pale-faced and frail-looking, carrying an ice sword engraved with snowflake patterns.

He remembered Mingtai mentioning this person, a cultivator named Xue Shilou who was somewhat famous in the Extreme North. To be noted by Mingtai, he naturally had merits. However, compared to Lu Yang, he ultimately fell far short.

“Poor Xue Shilou, meeting Lu Yang in the first match.”

“Can’t help it; he’s too unlucky.”

“I wonder how much power he could force Lu Yang to display.”

“I hope the fight lasts longer. The more of Lu Yang’s trump cards he reveals, the better for us.”

Despite hearing the murmurs below the platform, Xue Shilou’s gaze remained exceptionally resolved. So what if Lu Yang’s talent is great? I can bridge the gap through effort. My decades of sword practice—tears, sweat, and scars—are countless.

Throughout my journey, how many strong foes have I faced? How many people said I couldn’t win? Yet reality slapped them in the face and proved them all wrong.

On the arena platform, dozens of blows were exchanged in a flash. Living up to his reputation as a Sword Dao genius honed by years in the Extreme North, Xue Shilou’s sword intent style carried a tinge of chill and decisiveness.

It was Lu Yang’s first time fighting with a sword-intent avatar, and he found it quite novel.

Now that I’ve experienced what it feels like to fight a sword-intent avatar, it’s time to get serious.

As Lu Yang’s sword moves changed, Xue Shilou felt mounting pressure, as if Lu Yang wielded not a sword but a giant hammer capable of shaking heaven and earth. Each clash numbed his wrist.

Is this Lu Yang’s true strength? Had he merely been warming up just now?

Cold sweat formed on Xue Shilou’s forehead. Both of us are using sword-intent avatars, which have nothing to do with our cultivation. This also signifies that Lu Yang’s sword intent far surpasses mine.

Lu Yang’s moves were heavy and swift, seemingly piercing Xue Shilou’s moves. Each sword strike was aimed at his weakness, forcing him to passively defend without the chance to counter.

The spectating sword cultivators could also tell that Xue Shilou’s resistance was futile and that his defeat was a matter of time. However, none of them could imagine faring better than Xue Shilou if they were in his place.

“How about you just admit defeat?” Lu Yang suggested sincerely, hoping to finish early and observe other matches before they ended.

“No!” Xue Shilou said firmly. Though he was at a disadvantage, his gaze remained resolute, unshaken by the gulf in their abilities.

Lu Yang was stunned, then realized his attitude was wrong. As a sword cultivator, one should fight to the last moment; how could I suggest surrender? My words were an insult and a slap to Xue Shilou’s face.

He said earnestly, “Apologies. In return, I’ll use my full power to defeat you.”

Sensing Lu Yang’s increasingly heavy and rapid assaults, Xue Shilou sweated profusely, feeling like his blood was boiling.

So the gap between me and a true Sword Dao genius is this vast? Is this as far as I’ll go?

Xue Shilou was momentarily dazed as his memories were pulled back to his childhood.

~~~

Amidst swirling snow, Xue Shilou stood on a wooden stake, holding a broken iron sword. The north wind howled, snowflakes stinging his face.

“Shifu, I can't hold on much longer,” Xue Shilou said through gritted teeth, afraid to open his mouth wide lest snow fly in.

His shifu, hunched and leaning on a cane, seemed utterly oblivious to Xue Shilou’s wavering form.

“Persevere. You must adapt to this kind of environment and withstand the blizzard. One day, you'll understand the meaning of today's training.”

~~~

“Shifu, so you had foreseen this day long ago?” Xue Shilou mumbled. Lu Yang's attacks resembled the fierce snowstorm in the Extreme North.

He slowly reined in his moves, narrowing his defense range and adjusting his posture. He assumed a peculiar stance—stake-standing meditation.[1]

Gradually, he recalled his shifu’s guidance and the memories of his sword practice. Previously unrelated moves now connected, transforming into new moves.

“Stake-Standing Meditation Sword Form!”

This is a sword form that can withstand blizzards—one that even Shifu couldn't complete!

“Slash.”

With a soft mutter from Lu Yang, sword qi turned into a moon and pierced the Stake-Standing Meditation Sword Form, hurling Xue Shilou to the platform’s edge, knocking him unconscious.

“Junior Brother Xue has passed out. This is bad.” A sword cultivator below the platform grew anxious upon seeing Xue Shilou collapse.

“Fellow Daoist, what happens when Xue Shilou loses consciousness?”

That person sighed. “Xue Shilou is my junior brother. Shifu found him as an orphan, and he demonstrated remarkable talent in Sword Dao when he was young, so Shifu regarded him as his successor.

“Just as Shifu thought he had gained a fine disciple, an accident happened. Junior Brother Xue fell unconscious, and another consciousness took over his body, making him cruel and powerful. That was how Shifu’s leg got broken.

“Later, when Junior Brother Xue awoke, he remembered nothing. Shifu and I never mentioned the incident.

“Shifu suspected that before Junior Brother Xue was found, he had encountered some trauma, resulting in his split personality.”

Sure enough, after Xue Shilou passed out, he stood again, his entire aura completely transformed.

“Why did this trash faint again? As I thought, he still has to count on me.” As “Xue Shilou” looked at Lu Yang, his lips curled into a ruthless smile.

“Slash.”

Just like before, with a soft mutter from Lu Yang, Xue Shilou’s alternate personality was knocked unconscious too.

~~~

Within Xue Shilou’s mental world stood two Xue Shilous—one bright and one dark.

“So I was the one who broke Shifu’s leg?” The bright Xue Shilou clutched his head and wept. “No, it was you! You hurt Shifu!”

The dark Xue Shilou sneered. “So what if I did? Isn't it because your bloodline's power was too strong and uncontrollable that I split off as an alternate personality?

“Without me, you would have frozen to death before Shifu found you.”

Seeing the bright Xue Shilou still crying, the dark Xue Shilou was frustrated. “Cry, keep crying—what’s the use? Can crying let you defeat your opponent?!”

“Then what should I do?!” the bright Xue Shilou demanded between sobs.

The dark Xue Shilou showed a complicated smile. “When you comprehended the Stake-Standing Meditation Sword Form, it elevated your cultivation realm. You just lack a little bit of help to fully adapt to your bloodline.”

“A little bit of help?” The bright Xue Shilou was taken aback.

Without any explanation, the dark Xue Shilou hugged the bright Xue Shilou, his form slowly dissipating.

“You still lack our fusion. I hope that after I vanish, you're no longer that crybaby who weeps at the slightest difficulty.”

“Little Dark!” The bright Xue Shilou yelled, desperately grasping for his other self, but he only managed to catch a shimmer of light.

~~~

In the real world, the fallen Xue Shilou slowly rose again, his gaze sorrowful yet unwavering. He raised his sword toward Lu Yang, speaking as if he were one person, yet also as though two selves were speaking in unison.

“Lu Yang, I will defeat you!”

“This aura—he possesses the legendary Snow Emperor Bloodline!” a sword cultivator from the Extreme North exclaimed.

“Why are you not done yet? Slash!” Lu Yang roared in rage, swinging his sword vigorously.

Xue Shilou tumbled off the arena platform.

1. You may refer to this article for more information on the zhanzhuang stance. ☜

Chapter 907: The Sword as the Body, the Body as the Sword

“Finally done.”

For some reason, after battling Xue Shilou, Lu Yang inexplicably felt exhausted, as if he had fought three people. He had originally planned to finish early and watch the other matches in the second group. Now, he just wanted to sit and rest for a while.

“By the way, Immortal Fairy, did someone below the platform shout something about a Snow Emperor Bloodline? Do you know what that is?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “Never heard of it. It’s probably not any impressive figure; didn’t you just defeat his descendant?”

Lu Yang felt that Xue Shilou was a rather tough nut to crack. He is the first opponent to withstand three consecutive Slashing Word Mantras.

Oh, that isn’t exactly accurate. I should say that he’s the first opponent of the same level to withstand three Slashing Word Mantras.

After all, my opponents include the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, the Heaven Mandate Immortal, the Qilin Immortal, and so on. Three Slashing Word Mantras would be nothing to them.

Lu Yang felt embarrassed to ask the cultivators from the Extreme North what the Snow Emperor Bloodline was. Judging by their reactions, it must be terrifying and perhaps highly revered among cultivators there.

Having just defeated Xue Shilou, if I were to ask, “What’s the Snow Emperor? Is he really that impressive?” wouldn’t that be outright mockery?

Even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wouldn’t do something so foolish.

“Hey, why not just ask those sword cultivators from the Extreme North? Then wouldn’t you know what the Snow Emperor Bloodline is?!” As Lu Yang’s golden finger cheat and strategist, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy proposed a great solution.

Lu Yang, “...”

“Congratulations on your victory.” Yun Mengmeng approached with a beaming smile.

“A piece of cake.” In front of a Golden Core cultivator, Lu Yang had to maintain his image and not show any fatigue.

Seeing Lu Yang descend from the platform, the crowd instinctively parted, making way for him.

Those three Slashing Word Mantras were a sword cultivator’s most basic sword forms, yet they seemed to have undergone a complete transformation in Lu Yang’s hands, their power incomparable to the Slashing Word Mantra they knew.

Few could even withstand one strike.

To hone the most fundamental sword forms to such an extent, one could imagine how diligently Lu Yang trained.

Extraordinary talent in Sword Dao is one thing, but even his effort surpasses ours. How are we supposed to compete?

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, you’re done too?” Mingtai came over to look for Lu Yang after finishing his match.

“Just finished fighting Xue Shilou from the Extreme North. What about you?”

“Just finished fighting a large black dog from the Demon Region.” Recalling the battle, Mingtai shifted uncomfortably; he wanted a bath. “When that dog fought me with a sword in its mouth, saliva flew everywhere and all over me.”

The large black dog’s offensive power was average, but the psychological impact was immense. Demon Region sword cultivators all knew its fighting style, and none of them wanted to be matched against him.

Fortunately for them, Mingtai became the unlucky one.

After the second group’s matches ended, the third, fourth...up to the thirty-second groups all concluded smoothly. The order was reshuffled, and lots were drawn again.

Next, Lu Yang faced a woman disguised as a man, seeking to prove that women could also become supreme sword cultivators.

“Slash.”

Next, he faced a daughter attending the Sword-Seeking Grand ceremony in place of her bedridden father.

“Slash.”

Next, he faced a female sword cultivator who came to challenge the strong, believing only the strongest could be her husband.

“Mingtai, let’s swap opponents.”

“Ah? Oh.”

~~~

“Xiao Yangzi, Xiao Yangzi, let me have a go!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy saw Yue Chuan and his sword spirit A’Lan fight together like husband and wife, sweeping through matches until they were ultimately defeated by Lu Yang. Although they lost, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy found the sight of a sword cultivator and a sword spirit fighting together so cool that she was tempted to try it herself.

“Ah? Immortal Fairy, you want to fight?” Lu Yang wondered, Should I resurrect and tie up the Sword Tower Supreme Lord and the Qin Sword Venerable Lord for you?

“Aiya, I won’t show my face.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy giggled, understanding that she must keep a low profile and not appear in public. “Just hold on tight to the Qingfeng Sword.”

Clueless as to how she planned to fight, Lu Yang felt uneasy, but since it was her request, he had to accept.

~~~

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, I never expected to exchange blows with you at this Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony.”

This time, Lu Yang’s opponent was Kun Qiu of the Hundun Tribe.

Lu Yang had watched Kun Qiu’s matches. His style was indeed unique, emphasizing yin-yang fusion and balancing hardness with softness. The transitions between his sword moves were so fluid that his opponents couldn’t react.

“I never expected the Hundun Tribe to have such a Sword Dao expert like you. It’s really a pity that I didn’t spar with you during my visit to the Demon Region.”

Yin-yang fusion and balancing hardness with softness were reminiscent of the Nine-Layers Immortal’s Dao Fruit. Lu Yang felt that adapting a simpler version now would prepare him for the Nine-Layers Immortal yin-yang torture in the future.

The moment the battle began, the Qingfeng Sword lunged toward Kun Qiu, dragging Lu Yang along, startling both him and Kun Qiu.

Lu Yang hadn’t expected such a fighting style from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy; Kun Qiu hadn’t expected such a fighting style from Lu Yang.

Kun Qiu’s fighting style was known for unpredictability and surprise; he never imagined Lu Yang would seize the initiative first.

“As I thought, he’s a tough opponent. One move, and he’s disrupted my rhythm!

“Right, only such opponents are challenging!

“Lu Yang, come fight!”

“Xiao Yangzi, let’s charge!” Within the Qingfeng Sword, the sword spirit shouted, her voice only heard by Lu Yang. She bolted like a wild horse loose from its reins. Had Lu Yang not held tight, he would have been flung off.

~~~

Tower Leader Guan watched Lu Yang gravely, commenting to the elders beside him.

“Juniors are redoubtable indeed. Have you noticed? Every time, the Qingfeng Sword moves first, then Lu Yang follows.

“What does this mean? It means that Lu Yang has reached a legendary variant of the realm Person as Sword as One. His thoughts transmit to the sword first, then to his body!

“The sword as the sovereign and he as the subject—so that’s what it means.

“Remarkable.”

One elder couldn’t help but ask, “Setting aside Lu Yang’s matter, after Mingtai defeated that female sword cultivator, she’s been clamoring to marry him. What should we do?”

Another elder grew anxious. “Absolutely not! We mustn’t let Mingtai betray the Supreme Lord!”

~~~

On the arena platform, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had comprehended a new realm of Person and Sword as One, flinging Lu Yang about and using him to ram Kun Qiu.

“Heyah!”

Without any other choice, Lu Yang could only envelop himself in sword qi and kick Kun Qiu.

No matter how renowned Kun Qiu was for his versatile sword moves, he couldn’t have anticipated such a fighting style. He was stunned anew; every one of Lu Yang’s attacks defied his expectations.

“Could this be the legendary ‘the sword as the body, the body as the sword?’”

“Chain Sword-Qi Kick!” Lu Yang bellowed.

His legwork was formidable. His feet moved in a blur, each kick imbued with sword qi and striking Kun Qiu’s chest. Attacks rained down like a tempest, leaving Kun Qiu no time to react as he was sent tumbling off the platform!

Chapter 908: Incipient Sword Dao Field

“What kind of sword technique is that?”

Having witnessed the entire battle between Lu Yang and Kun Qiu, the crowd of sword cultivators was astonished, gathering to discuss. They had seen many humans wielding swords, but this was their first time seeing a sword wielding a human.

As Lu Yang’s sword intent dissipated, he coughed dryly. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s antics had exhausted him. “It’s a sword technique I just improvised. I haven’t thought of a name yet.”

His words caused an even greater uproar.

“An improvised sword technique? That’s so impressive.”

“I wondered why Fellow Daoist Lu Yang’s sword technique seemed somewhat crude and needed polishing—so it’s because it was newly created!”

“To think a sword technique comprehended on the spot is so powerful.”

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, please give this sword technique a name.”

Lu Yang froze at the sudden request. What should I call it?

“Then let’s call it the Dou Emperor Sword Technique.”

After all, this sword technique isn’t considered mine but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s—it’s better to credit her. Lu Yang was good at putting himself in others’ shoes, and he was confident the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would name it the same.

“Dope Emperor Sword Technique?[1] What a domineering name!”

“Uh, it’s the ‘dou’ as in doufu,” Lu Yang clarified.

The crowd was slightly surprised. Although Fellow Daoist Lu Yang’s sword technique is stellar, his naming sense is...a different story.

“Xiao Yangzi, your naming sense is terrible! Calling it the Everlasting Sword Technique would be so much better!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. When it comes to naming, it’s still up to me; Xiao Yangzi can’t be counted on.

The cultural gap between minister and emperor is reflected in such minor details.

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, since when was your naming sense so good?

But the name is already set; it’s too late to change it now.

~~~

Lu Yang’s match with Kun Qiu was part of the semifinals. Having defeated Kun Qiu, Lu Yang naturally advanced to the much-anticipated final.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, just as I thought, we are the last two standing.” Mingtai stood on the arena platform with the Hanguang Sword in his hand, exuding the aura of a Sword Dao grandmaster. No one could discern his earlier discomfiture before that female sword cultivator.

The Hanguang Sword was both Mingtai’s original form and an immortal treasure forged by the Sword Tower Supreme Lord, half a step from becoming an immortal artifact. It was worthy of being called an immortal sword.

In terms of quality, only Lu Yang’s Qingfeng Sword could surpass it; even the Seven Stars Sword Set paled in comparison.

“I thought so too.” Lu Yang smiled, unsurprised that Mingtai had reached the final.

Mingtai was the sword spirit of the Sword Tower Supreme Lord, the strongest sword cultivator in history. A sword spirit nurtured through countless battles alongside such a figure would naturally be terrifyingly powerful.

Meeting Lu Yang’s gaze, Mingtai felt inexplicably uneasy, as if Lu Yang had seen through his true origin.

Be it the sword cultivators below or the Sword Tower’s higher-ups above, all watched intently, eager to find out who would prevail.

On the platform, the two genius sword cultivators raised their immortal swords, the gleaming tips aimed at each other, and their smiles gradually faded.

Below the platform, sword cultivators held their breath, determined to observe this battle closely. With a flash and a clang, the two geniuses vanished from their spots, appearing at the center of the arena platform.

None of them could even see who struck first, or perhaps the two had moved simultaneously.

“Slash!”

Abandoning any preliminary probing, Lu Yang decisively employed the Slashing Word Mantra. Previously, he reserved the Slashing Word Mantra for the final, decisive blow, but Mingtai was clearly unlike any prior opponent.

“Vast Wave Sword Technique!”

Behind Mingtai, sword qi coalesced into raging waves, shrouding the arena in mist and oceanic spray. The Hanguang Sword sliced through the air, leaving countless afterimages in its wake. Its speed was so extreme that the phantom images seemed almost real.

“This is the sword technique created by the Sword Tower Supreme Lord!” Kun Qiu remarked gravely.

Legend had it that the Vast Wave Sword Technique was long lost, and even Sword Tower possessed mere fragments. But judging by Mingtai’s unceasing display, it hardly seemed like a fragmented technique.

This is the complete Vast Wave Sword Technique!

“Rumor has it that Mingtai obtained the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s legacy—so it is true.”

In the ten thousand years after the Sword Tower Supreme Lord perished, numerous Sword Tower geniuses had failed the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s trial. Since Mingtai emerged, rumors claimed that he had succeeded in obtaining the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s legacy.

But these were only rumors; Mingtai had never demonstrated the lost sword techniques.

Now, in his battle with Lu Yang, he had confirmed that he had obtained the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s legacy.

“Slash!”

“Break!”

“Point!”

Lu Yang executed only fundamental sword moves. I have no other choice. I also want to use flashy sword techniques, but no one has taught me.

Although they were basic sword moves, Mingtai dared not underestimate them. In Lu Yang’s hands, these moves had transformed, unfolding with limitless variations according to his will.

Perhaps even Senior Brother Lu Yang himself doesn’t realize that his basic sword moves have undergone a complete transformation and are already considered self-created sword techniques.

The Qingfeng Sword possessed the might to split the heavens, cleaving through the vast waves of sword qi. The sword rays blazed fiercely, erupting in volcanic pillars of light.

With a flick of his wrist, Mingtai changed his moves, resembling a great peng, a phoenix, and a true dragon. Suddenly, countless phantoms of ancient, savage demon beasts appeared on the platform.

“This is the Demon Sword Technique, created by the Sword Tower Supreme Lord based on the folk art of Animal Form Fist!” Kun Qiu’s expression grew solemn. Even from below, he could sense the terror of the sword technique.

The Demon Sword Technique, also known as the Demon-Slaying Sword Technique, was created through battles between the Sword Tower Supreme Lord and the old ancestors of various demon tribes. Countless demon tribes’ old ancestors had fallen to it.

Mingtai tossed the Hanguang Sword upward, and it suddenly vanished. Neither the naked eye nor one’s spiritual consciousness could detect it.

However, as his opponent, Lu Yang knew the Hanguang Sword remained on the platform and under Mingtai’s control, just that it had turned invisible.

“That’s the Hanguang Sword—invisible when observed, imperceptible when deployed!”

All the sword cultivators were stunned. They had only heard that the Hanguang Sword was the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s personal sword, but none had seen it. Now, as Mingtai unleashed its true power, they finally realized that he was wielding the Hanguang Sword!

Sensing danger, Lu Yang shifted, barely evading the invisible Hanguang Sword’s strike.

He already bore multiple sword marks from the blade. None were fatal, but if this continued, defeat was certain.

As the Hanguang Sword was undetectable, Lu Yang had dodged through his keen perception of sword qi, but this method wasn’t foolproof. Moreover, he still had to deal with various demons formed from its sword qi, which was quite troublesome.

“Then it’s time I get serious. One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords!”

Lu Yang thrust the Qingfeng Sword into the platform. Countless sword replicas spread beneath his feet, while the sky above darkened with inverted replicas.

“This is...a Sword Dao field?” The Sword Tower’s higher-ups were visibly shaken, eyes wide with disbelief. They knew that Lu Yang had mastered One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords, but never expected him to have pushed it further, developing it into a Sword Dao field.

“No, it’s still in its incipient form,” Tower Leader Guan said calmly.

Even an incipient Sword Dao field was remarkable. This was something Advanced Divine Transfiguration cultivators had a slim chance of comprehending, and only with guidance.

From Lu Yang’s display, Tower Leader Guan suspected that the Taciturn Daoist Priest hadn’t taught Lu Yang any sword techniques and that Lu Yang had learned everything on his own.

He probably figured this out by himself.

“Was that old Taciturn scoundrel too lazy to teach Lu Yang? Or did he feel that he was incapable of teaching him, worried about leading him astray, so he might as well let Lu Yang comprehend things on his own?” Tower Leader Guan eyed Lu Yang within his incipient field suspiciously, surmising that even the Taciturn Daoist Priest dared to offer only vague directions out of fear that he would misguide Lu Yang.

Lu Yang’s talent in Sword Dao leaves even me awestruck. It can be said that such talent is number one in all of history.

1. Although both “dou” sound the same, the first “豆” means bean, while the second “斗” means battle or fight. I used “dope” with its vernacular meaning here because it sounds closer to “dou” in English. ☜

Chapter 909: Sword Seeking Number One

Lu Yang couldn’t hear Tower Leader Guan’s murmurs, so he didn’t know that he was manifesting an incipient Sword Dao field. He had merely witnessed the Unbeatable Nascent Soul perform it and thought he could too.

Upon trying, he found it indeed worked.

Furthermore, he could now deploy the incipient Sword Dao field on the ground and in the sky simultaneously.

The Qingfeng Sword replicas rose from the earth one after another. Lu Yang’s sword qi filled the entire space, sharpening his senses and allowing him to vaguely sense the Hanguang Sword’s position.

If Sword Tower’s higher-ups were already stunned from witnessing Lu Yang’s incipient Sword Dao field, much less needed to be said for the sword cultivators below.

The large black dog’s jaw dropped in astonishment, not even noticing that its saliva-covered sword had fallen to the ground.

Kun Qiu stared dumbfounded. Her true cultivation was at the Advanced Divine Transfiguration Stage, yet she had only just touched the threshold of a Sword Dao field, let alone an incipient form. She didn’t expect Lu Yang to beat her to it.[1]

“Lu Yang, I will definitely catch up to you!” Unshaken by the massive gulf between them, Kun Qiu’s gaze grew more resolute. As a sword cultivator, one must be indomitable and forge ahead with relentless drive.

“Here!” Lu Yang suddenly raised his right hand.

A clang could be heard, as if something had been struck away.

Mingtai caught the Hanguang Sword, also surprised that Lu Yang had comprehended an incipient Sword Dao field.

He had accompanied the Sword Tower Supreme Lord through the Immortal Ascension Tribulation, suffering severe damage and losing most of his memories. It was only twenty years ago that he awoke and had to start everything anew.

Otherwise, he too could manifest an incipient Sword Dao field.

The Hanguang Sword remained invisible, yet Lu Yang could anticipate the sword's moves through Mingtai’s wrist movements. To true Sword Dao experts, the Hanguang Sword might as well not be hidden.

This puzzled Lu Yang. Mingtai surely knows that I can predict his moves, so why is he still gripping the Hanguang Sword?

Lu Yang diverted part of his attention, sending most of the Qingfeng Sword replicas to battle the sword-qi demons while he confronted Mingtai directly.

Mingtai employed the Vast Wave Sword Technique again. Sword qi surged like an ocean toward Lu Yang, seeking to shatter this stubborn stone.

Lu Yang had grasped a measure of Xue Shilou’s Stake-Standing Meditation Sword Technique. Though waves came from all sides, he stood unmoved.

Below the platform, Xue Shilou looked as if he had seen a ghost. Didn’t I just perform a few moves of the Stake-Standing Meditation Sword Technique? Yet Lu Yang can already mimic them?

Mingtai hid within the ocean of sword qi. With Lu Yang’s Stake-Standing Meditation stance, ambushing from any direction was futile; Mingtai could only reveal himself to fight.

Barely ten exchanges in, Lu Yang’s cheek was suddenly cut.

Had I misjudged?

No, that’s not right.

“What happened? Didn’t Lu Yang block the Hanguang Sword? Why was he still cut?”

“Did another hidden Hanguang Sword ambush Lu Yang?”

“Didn’t the Sword Tower Supreme Lord always use a single-handed sword?”

The sword cultivators below discussed fervently, baffled by how Lu Yang got injured.

Lu Yang temporarily pulled away. Pondering briefly, he figured it out. “I see. The Hanguang Sword can not only turn invisible but also control its blade length.”

I could predict the Hanguang Sword’s position, but not its length!

“As expected of Senior Brother Lu Yang.” Mingtai was astonished. I didn’t expect Senior Brother Lu Yang to discern the Hanguang Sword’s other function so quickly.

Since Lu Yang couldn’t predict the Hanguang Sword’s length, he realized that close combat would be disadvantageous to him.

With a violent tremor of his arm, a surge of sword qi shot skyward, forming a cascading waterfall and a vast expanse of white, crashing down like a mountain flood with a deafening rumble.

Since I can’t defeat him in close combat, I’ll fight from a distance with sword qi!

Mingtai had anticipated this. Wielding the Hanguang Sword, he knew none of his peers could surpass him in close quarters.

The Hanguang Sword hummed, and sword qi reached the heavens, as if it were the center of the world, with great stars and suns revolving around it.

Two distinct masses of sword qi collided, unleashing terrifying power.

The sword qi shattered on contact, its fragments cutting the two. However, they ignored the pain, swinging their swords again and severing everything with domineering auras.

Below the platform, the sword cultivators reflected, discerning that the two possessed the spirit, the will, and the conviction in being the strongest at their level—only sword cultivators with such an aura could hack through thorns, charge ahead valiantly, and break through bottlenecks!

This is the true meaning of sword seeking through the intent!

Neither held back. Every sword qi encompassed their full strength, seeking to overpower the other, yet each clash ended with both forces shattering.

Their sword qi was equally matched with no victor in sight!

“Person and Sword as One!” Mingtai yelled, merging with the Hanguang Sword and returning to his original form. The power of his sword qi surged again.

“In that case...” An idea seemed to have struck Lu Yang, and he decided to attempt it.

He abandoned using his incipient Sword Dao field to battle the sword-qi demons, letting them ravage him, leaving himself riddled with wounds.

Qingfeng Sword replicas from the sky and beneath his feet trembled. They flew forth, transformed into sword light, and resonated with one another, coalescing into the sword qi that Lu Yang was accumulating.

The sword qi that had hit its limit somehow grew severalfold!

“This is...Ten Thousand Swords Return to One!” Tower Leader Guan vaguely identified the move Lu Yang displayed.

With his experience, he should have recognized it instantly, but Lu Yang’s version was too ambiguous. It’s completely unlike anything learned through proper channels!

Tower Leader Guan’s guess was correct—Lu Yang had never learned Ten Thousand Swords Return to One at all. He had merely seen the Taciturn Daoist Priest use it once against the Heartless Creed. Based on that memory and his own comprehension of the Sword Dao, Lu Yang mimicked it on the spot!

It was only natural that it differed greatly from the proper version.

Lu Yang had no other option. I can’t use Sword into Tiger, Sword into Phoenix, Sword into Dragon, or the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array in public.

That leaves me with no choice but to attempt new moves.

The two combatants’ sword qi swelled unceasingly. The sword cultivators below couldn’t discern which was stronger. Swallowing nervously, they stared unblinkingly, fearing they would miss details.

The answer would soon be revealed.

Boom!

As if the heavens had collapsed, the two dragon-like sword qi collided, erupting in a brilliant sword rain that produced thunderous clangs.

The two were blasted backward by the impact’s immense energy.

Mingtai was like a kite with a broken string, tumbling off the arena platform!

Lu Yang also stumbled backward uncontrollably, continuously deflecting the force from the shockwaves. With a shout, he thrust the Qingfeng Sword into the ground with his right arm, finally anchoring himself on the platform.

Tower Leader Guan flew above the arena platform, surveying the crowd solemnly. His gaze finally settled on Lu Yang with approval, and he announced loudly.

“Lu Yang’s Sword Heart—witnessed by heaven and earth, unprecedented in history.

“Lu Yang’s Sword Intent—luminous and pure, lofty and soaring to the sky.

“Sword-Seeking Segment, Lu Yang is number one!”

The sword cultivators below cheered. Having witnessed Lu Yang’s might, they all yelled, “Lu Yang number one!”

The collective volume of their voices shook the heavens as it reverberated throughout the Sword Tower.

Lu Yang’s gaze grew hazy as he swayed. The battle had drained all his energy.

“You people...have time to call me number one...yet not a single soul can come to support me...”

Thud.

He toppled over.

1. Kun Qiu’s pronoun changed here, so I’ll be following the author, since it was also previously mentioned that Kun Qiu is androgynous. ☜

Chapter 910: Portable Small World

Lu Yang slowly stirred awake, finding himself lying on the ground with Yun Mengmeng looking at him with concern.

“How long was I unconscious?”

“About ten breaths.” Yun Mengmeng led a carefree lifestyle, never sensitive to time.

“Lu Yang, take this pill.” A Sword Tower elder hurried over and presented a sublime pill to help Lu Yang recover.

The pill felt refreshing as it touched his tongue. After it slid into his stomach, he felt as if his whole body was immersed in water, cool and comfortable.

Lu Yang regained clarity. Yun Mengmeng helped him up, and he sat in meditation, circulating his cultivation technique and adjusting his breathing. Soon, he could move freely.

His mental power was comparable to the Fusion Stage and quickly returned to normal after being depleted.

As the sword spirit of an immortal sword, Mingtai also recovered swiftly.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, I’m in awe.” Mingtai approached. In that battle, he had used all his trump cards yet still lost to Lu Yang. It was a defeat he accepted wholeheartedly.

This was the nature of all sword cultivators—forthright. A win was a win, and a loss was a loss; there was nothing shameful in admitting it.

“Not at all. I merely got lucky.” Lu Yang was modest. His final Ten Thousand Swords Return to One was simply an attempt with a fifty-fifty chance of success or failure.

After witnessing that battle, many sword cultivators gained insights to varying degrees and dared not delay, sitting down on the spot to meditate. Fortuitous opportunities were hard to come by.

The planned visit to the sword vault after the Sword Seeking segment was postponed. The Sword Tower elders stepped in, setting up arrays to shield the cultivators from external disturbances, enabling them to gain as much insight as possible.

With all the sword cultivators going into seclusion, Lu Yang became the most idle person.

“Come to think of it, Mingtai’s Hanguang Sword can turn invisible; doesn’t my Qingfeng Sword have other functions?”

Lu Yang examined the Qingfeng Sword carefully. The Hanguang Sword is just an immortal treasure, while my Qingfeng Sword is a bona fide immortal artifact and Wu Yao’s personal sword. Logically, aside from its high quality, it should possess some special ability.

“It does. Isn’t it quite spacious inside? Other swords don’t have this,” the Qingfeng Sword’s sword spirit remarked.

“What do you mean... Wait, Immortal Fairy, are you saying the Qingfeng Sword contains another space?” Lu Yang caught on.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rolled her eyes. “Where else do you think I reside?”

Lu Yang replied inwardly, Immortal Fairy, with your amazing abilities, I truly thought you had attached yourself to the sword.

So you actually moved in.

“Hold on, I will pull you in."

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy thought, Xiao Yangzi is rather dull-witted; he doesn’t even know how to enter. Oh well, let me just drag him in myself.

Lu Yang vanished on the spot, and the Qingfeng Sword clanged to the ground.

~~~

“Is this the Qingfeng Sword’s internal space?” Lu Yang spun around in surprise, surveying his surroundings.

“More accurately, this is a self-contained small world within the Qingfeng Sword.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy employed more technical terminology.

Within this small world, spirit qi abounded. Towering mountains and flowing waters created a picturesque paradise isolated from the world.

Lu Yang stood on a bamboo raft, drifting downstream, while the mountains receded like filmstrips.

The bamboo raft was crafted by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy when she was bored during her time as a sword spirit, for which she had chopped down a great many trees.

“How is it?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy preened, though it was unclear whether she was flaunting this small world or her handiwork.

“That Wu Yao fellow had some skill, making the Qingfeng Sword’s interior quite presentable.”

“Has this small space always existed?” Lu Yang was astonished. To think I’ve always underestimated the Qingfeng Sword.

“It has indeed always existed, but it was previously sealed, so you couldn’t enter. Only after your cultivation reached a certain level did the seal open.”

Lu Yang felt somewhat comforted. It wasn’t that I failed to recognize its value, but that the seal was still unbroken. “When was the seal opened?”

“When you were at the Nascent Soul Stage.”

Lu Yang, “...”

He gazed at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with a profound look, the implication in his eyes self-evident.

Embarrassed by her pillar minister’s stare, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy chuckled sheepishly. “Xiao Yangzi, I thought you knew about the space inside the Qingfeng Sword and simply couldn’t be bothered to enter. After all, aside from the nice scenery, there’s nothing much fun here.”

Lu Yang pondered. True. Besides, I have no need for a portable small world anyway.

If I had one in my previous life, every flower and grass here would be spirit herbs, and even one of them sold outside would bring unimaginable wealth.

Or perhaps I could farm inside the small world. With the abundant spirit qi, seeds would surely mutate, and I can bring them out to amaze everyone.

Unfortunately, I didn’t have a portable small world in my previous life; acquiring it only after transmigrating to a cultivation world is rather pointless.

Lu Yang took a turn inside the Qingfeng Sword before departing.

~~~

About half a day later, the sword cultivators gradually concluded their seclusion and exchanged insights, feeling greatly enlightened.

Attending this Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony was well worth it. A single session of comprehension surpassed years of comprehension. Lu Yang and Mingtai’s battle showed them the future path of Sword Dao.

The sword cultivators sought out Lu Yang and Mingtai to express gratitude, and Xue Shilou and Kun Qiu were among them.

After the last cultivator’s seclusion finished, Tower Leader Guan announced the ceremony’s third and final segment.

“I believe everyone has heard that our Sword Tower’s sword vault houses spirit swords left by past sages. Upon entering, if fate allows, a spirit sword may choose to follow you and acknowledge you as its master. We will absolutely not interfere.

“When your affinity ends, we will naturally reclaim the spirit sword.

“If there is no affinity, please do not force it. I know some of you possess innate divine strength and could wrench a spirit sword through sheer force. Should you provoke the collective wrath of the spirit swords and an accident occur, the Sword Tower will bear no responsibility.”

The sword cultivators praised the Sword Tower’s magnanimity. Even though other sword sects possessed spirit swords, they would rather let their spiritual nature fade than allow outsiders to use them.

“If there are no objections, please follow me.”

Tower Leader Guan led the way, guiding them beneath the Sword Tower.

All the sword cultivators were nervous. A spirit sword acknowledging a master depended on affinity, unrelated to cultivation realm or talent. History offered many examples; an unremarkable cultivator was chosen by a spirit sword of great origin, thereafter becoming an unremarkable sword cultivator.

The sword vault was a massive cavity, as if someone had carved out a space beneath the Sword Tower with a sword. It was undecorated and quite primitive. Only a top-grade luminous pearl glowing for ten thousand years provided light.

Manifold spirit swords were casually inserted throughout, some in the ground and some on the walls. This wasn’t due to the Sword Tower’s indifference. The spirit swords themselves preferred such arrangements.

“I wonder how many spirit swords will acknowledge masters this time,” an elder commented.

Beside him, Tower Leader Guan said, “Perhaps not even one.”

“Ah? Why?” The elder was bewildered.

Watching Mingtai enter the sword vault, Tower Leader Guan said meaningfully, “Don’t forget Mingtai’s identity—the Supreme Lord’s personal sword and big brother to all spirit swords. The sword vault is like his harem.”

Chapter 911: Please Advise, Junior Brother Mingtai

What was Mingtai’s identity? He was the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s personal sword—all the spirit swords in the sword vault were his juniors.

However, there was no seniority among swords, as that was a human construct. Between spirit swords, only strength mattered, and the weak submitted to the strong.

From this perspective, Mingtai was like a big brother to all the spirit swords in the sword vault. As long as he wished, they would all submit to him and follow him out.

Mingtai was aware that his status in the sword vault was like that of an emperor. If he entered, there would be nothing left for others. Hence, he tactfully moved to the back of the line, planning to enter last and give others a chance.

He also stopped Lu Yang. “Senior Brother Lu Yang, would you like to enter last with me? I can’t tell you some things, but I guarantee that if you fancy any sword, I have a way to make it follow you.”

Lu Yang could roughly guess where Mingtai’s confidence stemmed from. Since he offered help, refusing would make us seem distant.

“Sure, then thank you in advance, Junior Brother Mingtai.”

Mingtai smiled, eager to show off before Lu Yang.

On Lu Yang’s account, Yun Mengmeng was allowed to tour the sword vault. The Sword Tower agreed that if fate allowed, she too could take a sword.

“This sword is rather pretty.” In a corner of the sword vault, Yun Mengmeng squatted down and examined an exquisitely crafted sword with ornate patterns and gems on its hilt.

Only its hilt was visible; the blade was buried in the earth. She poked the slender sword, but received no response, which meant it had no affinity with her.
