“Come out and let me see your blade.” She prodded the slender sword again.

The sword emitted a rather rude thought. Let this lass called Yun Mengmeng scram, or I will teach her a lesson if she keeps pestering.

No one had scolded Yun Mengmeng like this before. She grew displeased and reached out, effortlessly pulling the slender sword from the earth.

Enraged, the slender sword vibrated violently, trying to break free and teach Yun Mengmeng a lesson.

“Stop shaking.” Yun Mengmeng flicked the sword, making it hum.

Seeing her bully the slender sword, nearby spirit swords stirred, preparing to burst forth from the earth.

Sensing the movement, Yun Mengmeng glared at them, frightening them into keeping their necks down.

The slender sword also realized that Yun Mengmeng hadn’t relied on innate divine strength, but on overwhelming power to pull it out. Its ire vanished as it froze in terror.

Finding the blade bare and unappealing, Yun Mengmeng lost interest and casually reinserted it into the ground.

“I was thinking of gifting you to Little Zhi, but you’re not pretty enough. Forget it.” Yun Mengmeng selected swords not for quality; they just had to look good.

~~~

“Brother Sword, follow me from now on! Let’s work hard together and reach the pinnacle of Sword Dao!” Someone painted grand visions, attempting to lure a spirit sword out.

“If you follow me, I guarantee you’ll evolve into a sword spirit.”

“Look at how our colors match—we’re destined to be a pair! Come on out!”

Other sword cultivators sat silently, resonating with the spirit swords, wishing to move them with sincerity.

However, whether it was grand promises or heartfelt resonance, all the spirit swords remained motionless, utterly ignoring the sword cultivators.

“Why aren’t you going over to resonate with the swords?” Kun Qiu saw the large black dog crouched at the entrance like a watchdog.

Before the dog could answer, Kun Qiu noticed the saliva-covered sword in its mouth.

“Never mind, no need to explain. I understand.” Kun Qiu looked at the large black dog with pity. With such usage of the sword, no spirit sword would choose it.

Entering the sword vault, Kun Qiu continuously communicated with the spirit swords through her spiritual consciousness, hoping one would follow her.

Alas, all spirit swords were set on following Mingtai and ignored her.

After a full round, a sword was finally moved by her sincerity. It trembled and emerged from the ground.

Kun Qiu gripped it joyfully. The blade divided into black and white from the middle, encompassing the dao of yin-yang hundun chaos—perfect for her.

Mingtai and Lu Yang entered the sword vault together.

During the ten thousand years after the Sword Tower Supreme Lord perished, Mingtai had remained here. He couldn’t be more familiar with the place and every spirit sword within.

His mere presence caused many spirit swords to grow restless, eager to rush into his arms and call him “gege.”

Other sword cultivators noticed the movement and looked to the entrance in astonishment.

“Mingtai resonates with all these swords?!”

Everyone was shocked. This was unprecedented in previous Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremonies.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, do you know how to choose a sword you desire?” Mingtai asked.

“I’d like to hear the details.”

Mingtai was an expert on this. “A desired sword is a sword that resonates with you. From what I see, you likely wish to possess another sword alongside your current one?”

Lu Yang nodded.

Mingtai added, “In that case, the sword you choose must resonate with you and your current personal sword. Otherwise, conflict may arise between the two swords.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, you can try raising your current personal sword and releasing your aura and its aura. Swords that match you will stir, and the one that reacts most strongly will be the sword that resonates with you best.”

Completely ignorant here, Lu Yang could only comply.

At the entrance, he raised the Qingfeng Sword. Divine Transfiguration aura surged, and the Qingfeng Sword trembled slightly, spreading sword qi like ripples.

“It also has to resonate with the Qingfeng Sword?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy listened intently to Mingtai’s theory. “Since this immortal is now the sword spirit, any sword Xiao Yangzi chooses must resonate with me, too, right?”

At this thought, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stealthily released a wisp of immortal charm. This aura was perceptible only to spirit swords, not sword cultivators.

The spirit swords sensed Lu Yang’s spirit root, the immortal sword’s presence, and the sword spirit within containing eternal power—this combination was the supreme existence they all pursued!

One after another, the spirit swords vibrated violently in ecstasy. The entire sword vault shook as if there was an earthquake.

Mingtai was dumbstruck, wondering if some accident had caused the chaos in the sword vault. He desperately issued commands to pacify the spirit swords, but they completely ignored him!

Witnessing this, Sword Tower’s higher-ups were even more bewildered. What's happening? Even the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s presence shouldn’t cause such an unusual phenomenon!

Countless spirit swords burst forth from the earth and walls, leaving their positions to form neat rows. Even the Hundun Yin-Yang Sword that Kun Qiu had painstakingly obtained flew from her grasp to join the formation of spirit swords in the air.

The spirit swords were perfectly aligned like an army awaiting inspection. Wherever Lu Yang’s gaze landed, the respective swords would stir, hoping to be selected.

Lu Yang turned to Mingtai, somewhat embarrassed. “It’s my first time doing this, so I don’t have much experience. I’m not sure which sword resonates best with me. Please advise, Junior Brother Mingtai.”

Chapter 912: An Immortal’s Successor

Mingtai shuddered, unable to utter a single word.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy acted cautiously, understanding that her existence was a secret. She deliberately controlled herself, merely spreading her immortal charm to every spirit sword, which was imperceptible to Mingtai and the others.

However, she had overlooked one thing—Mingtai could sense the changes to the spirit swords.

He could sense the spirit swords’ cheers, excitement, and desire to submit to Lu Yang, who possessed a sword spirit root, an immortal sword, and its sword spirit! If they followed him, they might have a chance to become immortal swords and give birth to immortal-level sword spirits!

This was a massive, fortuitous opportunity for every spirit sword!

Mingtai stared at Lu Yang in disbelief. Lu Yang possesses an immortal-level sword spirit?!

How did he achieve this? Has there been such a sword spirit in history?

If he hadn’t already taken human form, he would also want to become Lu Yang’s sword!

~~~

Tower Leader Guan and the others couldn’t perceive the sword’s thoughts as clearly as Mingtai.

“How is this possible? Why is Lu Yang so popular?”

They were utterly flummoxed. The reason couldn’t be something as simple as possessing a sword spirit root.

Back when the Taciturn Daoist Priest attended the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony, he had only gained recognition from a small fraction of the spirit swords. He had caused quite an uproar then, but compared to Lu Yang now, it was totally incomparable.

Other sword cultivators stood frozen on the spot, gazing blankly at Lu Yang. The latter stood at the entrance, with his back facing the light, resembling a deity.

They had exhausted every effort without gaining the recognition of a single spirit sword. Yet Lu Yang merely had to stand there and release his aura, and every spirit sword in the sword vault would flock to him.

Xue Shilou’s expression was vacant as he mechanically mumbled, “Wasn’t it said that choosing a sword depends on fate?”

Is Lu Yang so fated with every spirit sword here?

Although Lu Yang was selecting a sword in the sword vault for the first time, seeing this army of spirit swords and Mingtai’s reaction, he knew something was amiss.

This situation likely has little to do with me. It must have been caused by the fake sword spirit, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy said in delight, “Xiao Yangzi, Xiao Yangzi! Quickly take them all! We now have a use for the souls of those prisoners on Incarceration Peak!”

She still hadn’t forgotten about the prisoners.

“Don’t worry if your identity jade tablet can’t store all of them. We have the Qingfeng Sword’s small world. That will be enough.” She had thought it through, even considering how to transport the spirit swords.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was naturally elated. Xiao Yangzi is a pillar minister of the Great Dou Dynasty. These spirit swords are his subordinates and thus rightful possessions of the Great Dou Dynasty.

When it came to matters of the Great Dou Dynasty, she was always quick-witted.

Lu Yang. “...”

Immortal Fairy, your consideration is thorough, but have you considered the Sword Tower’s reaction?

Just as Lu Yang ruminated on which sword he should choose, Mingtai suddenly gasped.

“That sword is reacting, too?!”

Lu Yang snapped back to his senses and followed Mingtai’s gaze. A single sword remained embedded in the ground, sticking out among the airborne swords. Yet it also trembled continuously, clearly also reacting to Lu Yang.

“Is that sword very impressive?” Lu Yang asked in puzzlement.

Mingtai’s expression was grave. “I can control every spirit sword in the sword vault, except that one.

“That sword didn’t originate from the Sword Tower, but was acquired by Mast...the first Tower Leader by chance. Its grade is not below that of my Hanguang Sword, and it is worthy of being called an immortal sword.

“The first Tower Leader’s Sword Dao was unparalleled, yet he never gained that sword’s recognition. Without a choice, he stored it here, hoping a fated person would one day claim it. freewebnovel.com

“This is also the origin of the sword vault.”

Gazing at the nameless immortal sword shaking incessantly and preparing to burst forth from the earth, Mingtai continued slowly, “Yet for ten thousand years, that sword has remained like this, unresponsive to any sword cultivator’s call—until you appeared, Senior Brother Lu Yang.”

Lu Yang was astonished to learn that it was also an immortal sword.

“Eh, why does this sword look familiar?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy studied the nameless sword with only its hilt visible, gradually matching it with one in her memory.

“I remember! Isn’t this Liu Ningxuan’s Chengying[1] Sword?!”

The name sounded familiar to Lu Yang.

Suddenly, it clicked. Liu Ningxuan, who possessed peerless talent in Sword Dao, was hailed as number one in antiquity. He was a master of both qin and sword, creating the move Person and Sword as One. In his battle against the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, he had pushed himself to sublimation, merging with his sword and becoming inseparable from it.

Nowadays, when people mention the strongest sword cultivators, they often name Liu Ningxuan alongside the Sword Tower Supreme Lord.

The Seven Stars Sword Set I obtained from the Creation Secret Domain was once used by Liu Ningxuan!

At this thought, Lu Yang had a bad feeling.

Just as he was about to question the Everlasting Immortal Fairy further, the Chengying Sword shot skyward, radiating an aura that caused hearts to palpitate and scattering the orderly formation of the spirit swords.

A figure emerged from the sword, and it was none other than Liu Ningxuan himself!

Clad in ancient garb, Liu Ningxuan appeared before everyone as an immortal sword’s sword spirit, sweeping his furious gaze across the crowd before locking his eyes onto Lu Yang with a hostile expression.

“So you were the one who released the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s aura just now!”

“Heaven Mandate Immortal?” Lu Yang hadn’t expected that to be Liu Ningxuan’s first question.

Liu Ningxuan sneered, his gaze growing frosty. “Still trying to deceive me? Back then, the Heaven Mandate Immortal forced me to use Person and Sword as One just to escape, reducing me to this state that is neither human nor ghost! How could I mistake his aura?!”

Lu Yang understood—Liu Ningxuan’s memories had also been altered. The mastermind behind the scenes had made him believe that his final battle was against the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

Although Ao Ling’s and Jiang Lianyi’s memories had also been erased, their deep bond with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy made her feel familiar the moment they saw her.

The same applied to Liu Ningxuan. How could his life-and-death enmity with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy be completely forgotten?

For various reasons, he had mistaken her aura for the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s. “If my guess is correct, kid, you must be the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s successor.”

Lu Yang felt that Liu Ningxuan had a rather significant misunderstanding about him.

But to onlookers, it was an entirely different matter. If Liu Ningxuan said that Lu Yang was the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s successor, how could it be false?

“No wonder Lu Yang is so formidable! So it’s because he has inherited the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s legacy!”

“An immortal’s successor—terrifying...”

The people from the Sword Tower nodded, finding explanations for all of Lu Yang’s actions.

“No wonder Lu Yang could fight Young Creed Leader Lu to a draw. So it’s because both are successors of immortals.”

“Hmm, kid, you are a sword spirit turned human?” Liu Ningxuan’s murderous intent flared as he noticed Mingtai beside Lu Yang.

After being grievously wounded by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, he had executed Person and Sword as One to flee, which left the Chengying Sword damaged, reduced to little more than a discarded piece of metal. He had remained unconscious as the sword passed through various hands—forging masters and Sword Dao experts—who recognized its extraordinary nature and gradually restored it. Eventually, he awoke.

By then, it was the Great Yu era.

It was because Liu Ningxuan had become a sword spirit, an external existence, that he had survived to this day.

Unlike Mingtai, an innate sword spirit, Liu Ningxuan was an acquired sword spirit.

Innate sword spirits could take human form, while acquired ones couldn’t, forever bound to their swords.

Hence, he particularly despised innate sword spirits.

1. Shadow-Bearing ☜

Chapter 913: Sword Tower Supreme Lord

“What did he just say? Mingtai is a sword spirit turned human?”

The sword cultivators stared at Mingtai incredulously. Lu Yang is the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s successor, and Mingtai is a sword spirit turned human—hold on, with how special your identities are, aren’t we too ordinary when compared to you two?

Originally, the sword cultivators thought that with the upcoming Battle of the Great Era, it was their time to shine.

In the end, they realized that they had been utterly defeated in terms of status alone.

Having a special identity wasn’t necessarily a problem. Throughout history, there were plenty of cultivators who trained diligently and defeated foes with special backgrounds. Their deeds were then passed down as tales.

But the problem is, even after such training, we still can’t defeat them both.

What the hell are we still contending for in the Great Era?

The expressions of the Sword Tower’s higher-ups shifted. They hadn’t expected this ancient nameless sword spirit to expose Mingtai’s identity outright, and they didn’t know whether this was a blessing or a calamity.

Yun Mengmeng quietly drew closer to Lu Yang, sensing something amiss with Liu Ningxuan’s demeanor. The faint aura he emitted made her very uncomfortable. If Yun Mengmeng had spent more time in the outside world, she would have recognized this as a murderous aura.

Liu Ningxuan fixed his gaze on Mingtai, revealing a cruel, dangerous smile as he spoke slowly. “Innate sword spirits have it so good—they can even take human form. Unlike me, I can only stay confined within the sword.”

Lu Yang’s expression changed, and he stepped before Mingtai. “What are you planning?!”

Liu Ningxuan found his gesture laughable. “Kid, don’t think I fear you just because you inherited the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s legacy. Let me guess—you’ve only obtained his legacy and seen his projections, but never seen the true Heaven Mandate Immortal!”

Seeing Lu Yang’s expression, Liu Ningxuan grew more certain. “The Heaven Mandate Immortal hasn’t appeared in ages. He might be long dead.”

With how much the ostentatious Heaven Mandate Immortal liked to flaunt, how could he have gone silent for over a hundred thousand years? Something must be wrong.

I have a life-and-death enmity with the Heaven Mandate Immortal. If it hadn't been for the fear that he could still be alive, I would have killed Lu Yang, too!

Over ten thousand years ago, the Sword Tower Supreme Lord obtained the Chengying Sword. Liu Ningxuan feared that he'd be discovered within it, so he remained in slumber since then.

Upon awakening, he first saw his mortal enemy’s successor, then an innate sword spirit in human form. How could he not kill them to vent his fury?

Liu Ningxuan manipulated the Chengying Sword, unleashing invisible sword qi. It erupted brilliantly, surpassing the top-grade luminous pearl on the sword vault’s ceiling. Such power made the sword vault tremble. The tower above even swayed, unable to withstand it.

The invisible sword qi locked onto Mingtai, intent on killing him in one strike!

The sword cultivators shuddered in fear at the sight. Even an ordinary Transcendent Tribulation cultivator could probably not withstand something like that!

“Protect Mingtai!” Tower Leader Guan hastily hollered. Together with the twelve elders, they positioned themselves before Mingtai.

Golden runes burst forth. They encompassed some supreme principle, interweaving to form the Great Sword Dao Cosmic Loop Array.

Boom!

The invisible sword qi descended, raging upon contacting the array. After three breaths of stalemate, both the invisible sword qi and the great array shattered at the same time!

“Ah—” Tower Leader Guan and the others were flung back by the shockwaves. It was unclear how many ribs they broke, and blood trickled from their lips.

Liu Ningxuan sneered. “Is this all you’ve got?

“You should be grateful that I haven’t fought in tens of thousands of years and have gotten rusty. Otherwise, that strike would have annihilated you all!

“This time, I wonder what you will use to defend yourselves?”

Liu Ningxuan condensed another invisible sword qi, even more powerful than the one before!

Tower Leader Guan and the elders paled. They had exhausted their full strength to block the first strike. How were they supposed to withstand this?

Right then, the top-grade luminous pearl on the sword vault’s ceiling blazed with unprecedented radiance. A graceful figure emerged from the nine-colored divine light.

“I’d like to see who dares harm Mingtai!”

All eyes were fixed on the silhouette within the nine-colored divine light, wondering which exalted figure had appeared.

Mingtai’s eyes lit up at the familiar figure. He couldn’t help but cry out, “Master!”

Master?

Hearing Mingtai’s form of address, Tower Leader Guan realized who she was. “Unworthy disciple of the Sword Tower pays respects to the Supreme Lord!”

The top-grade luminous pearl shattered, and the nine-colored divine light faded, revealing the graceful figure’s true form—a woman of peerless elegance. She appeared delicate, like a sheltered young miss.

Few knew that the Sword Tower Supreme Lord was actually a woman.

“Sword Tower Supreme Lord?” Liu Ningxuan narrowed his eyes, remaining calm. This is definitely not her true body.

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord acted as if she hadn’t seen Liu Ningxuan, flying down and patting Mingtai’s head dotingly. “As I thought, you have chosen the path of taking on human form.”

“Master!” Mingtai clung to her, weeping bitterly. He had thought he would never see her again.

“Alright, that’s enough, don’t cry. Am I not perfectly fine?” the Sword Tower Supreme Lord comforted him softly.

Then she turned her head to look at Liu Ningxuan above. “So he’s the one bullying you? Watch your jiejie teach him a lesson!”

Taking the Hanguang Sword, the Sword Tower Supreme Lord flew up to confront Liu Ningxuan. The air itself seemed to congeal.

Liu Ningxuan showed no fear, sneering contemptuously. “You have the face to say you’re perfectly fine? You are nothing but a remnant soul hidden within that luminous pearl. I suppose you only emerge when the Sword Tower faces catastrophe. freewebnovel.com

“How much of your original power can this remnant soul wield?” One can’t survive after failing the Immortal Ascension Tribulation. The fact that she could leave a remnant soul is already an impossibility made possible.

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord replied, “Back then, I already suspected that this sword was the Chengying Sword. Unfortunately, I never had proof, and even the Taixue Imperial Academy couldn’t confirm.

“Who would have thought? The world claims that you have vanished, yet here you are, skulking in the Chengying Sword and barely clinging to life without dignity.”

She pointed her sword at Liu Ningxuan, her brows furrowing. “How dare you harm my Mingtai?! You must be tired of living!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also observed the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s state. “Impressive. To leave a remnant soul from the Immortal Ascension Tribulation—could she have the Soul Incipient Dao Fruit?”

Apart from the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit, only the Soul Incipient Dao Fruit could achieve this.

“Immortal Fairy, what’s Liu Ningxuan’s cultivation level?” Lu Yang asked stealthily.

“Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage.”

“Only at the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage?” Lu Yang remarked inwardly, I thought Liu Ningxuan would be a half-immortal.

Then he realized something was off. When did I start thinking that Transcendent Tribulation cultivators are nothing special?

“Back then, we both wanted to condense the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit. He overestimated himself and challenged me. During the battle, he used Person and Sword as One to flee.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy huffed indignantly.

“It’s a pity that he became a sword spirit; sword spirits can’t possess Incipient Dao Fruits. Oh, except me.

“If he hadn’t become a sword spirit, he might have had some chance to condense the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit.”

Lu Yang hadn’t expected the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s assessment of Liu Ningxuan to be this high. But then again, that makes sense. Without some skill, who would dare challenge the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

Chapter 914: Who Are You?!

Within the sword vault, sword qi clashed fiercely. The Sword Tower Supreme Lord commanded myriad swords, sweeping across the field, while Liu Ningxuan, in the Person and Sword as One state, pressed forward with unstoppable momentum.

A cacophony of noises erupted as countless spirit swords collided in an instant. The deafening sounds inadvertently formed sonic attacks that posed a danger even to onlookers.

“Run!” Kun Qiu hollered and turned on her heels. She couldn’t be bothered that her Hundun Yin-Yang Sword had abandoned her.

If I still dare to remain in the sword vault now, I probably won’t even know how I died!

Other sword cultivators also realized the gravity of the situation and fled.

The sword vault had become a battlefield for two great sword cultivators; there was no place for mortals. Even Tower Leader Guan and the elders could only watch helplessly.

Both sword cultivators were in an incomplete state. Liu Ningxuan had become a sword spirit after executing Person and Sword as One, no longer human, while the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s true body had long perished, now nothing more than a remnant soul relying on the Soul Incipient Dao Fruit.

Despite the two being far from their peak condition, their battle was not something Fusion cultivators could interfere in; even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators would think twice before getting involved.

Liu Ningxuan was worthy to be the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s opponent and was qualified to possess the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit. It could be said that he was the number one sword cultivator of the ancient era.

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s cultivation was even higher. The fact that she could attempt the Immortal Ascension Tribulation signified that she had fully comprehended her Soul Incipient Dao Fruit and was on the same level as Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi; the next step would be immortality. Setting aside Yun Zhi, she was the person with the highest cultivation since Great Xia’s founding.

In a sense, their Sword Dao contest could be viewed as a part of the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony.

This was the most impressive Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony ever.

“Vast Wave Sword Technique.”

Sword qi surged, transforming the entire sword vault into an ocean of sword qi. It was as if the water from the East Sea’s depths had been relocated here, carrying terrifying weight and pressure. Numerous sword-qi demons roamed, frenziedly attacking Liu Ningxuan and biting him.

The Hanguang Sword vanished. It transformed into the ocean’s most ferocious demon, seeking to sever Liu Ningxuan’s Chengying Sword.

“Silent Annihilation Sword Technique!”

The Chengying Sword blackened to the hue of ink, thick and viscous, radiating a destructive aura as if it were the very source of calamity—a truly chilling sight.

This had already touched the edge of the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit, an extremely terrifying feat. With this move, he had once pierced through a xuanwu at the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage with a single sword strike. Despite the Xuanwu being renowned for defense, it was as fragile as paper before this technique!

Xuan Xuan felt that even their Transcendent Tribulation old ancestor had to evade this strike, lest the sword shatter their vital defenses.

Before this move, the sword-qi seafolk demons scattered into lawless sword qi, absorbed by the Chengying Sword’s emitted aura before they could even touch the sword.

Clang!

All the sword qi was devoured by the Chengying Sword. Only the Hanguang Sword, which was also an immortal sword, remained unaffected, clashing with the Chengying Sword.

The collision of the two great immortal swords spanned the past and present, shaking the earth. The whole sword vault teetered, and the Sword Tower’s foundation destabilized, threatening to collapse at any moment.

The two unparalleled sword cultivators ignored this as they unleashed their Sword Dao, seeking to overwhelm the other party. As their Sword Dao fields expanded, neither appeared as majestic as everyone had imagined.

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s field teemed with ghost phantoms. These were all powerful foes she had slain, replicated by her Soul Incipient Dao Fruit and restored within the field.

Liu Ningxuan’s field resembled the world’s end. It was dark red, with the sun sinking and stars shattering. Any living being entering would inexplicably die, as if struck by inevitable karmic death.

Even with Lu Yang’s talent in Sword Dao, he couldn’t understand these two Sword Dao fields, let alone the others.

Much less needed to be said for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy; all her understanding of Sword Dao came from Lu Yang.

The Sword Dao fields expanded rapidly, scouring every inch of space. Space itself grew unstable, cracks continuously forming as if on the verge of shattering!

Boom! Boom! Boom!

Under the collision of the Sword Dao fields, the Sword Tower above finally succumbed, collapsing into ruins that threatened to bury the sword vault.

Yet the Sword Dao fields hurled the Sword Tower’s debris aside, leaving the two unaffected.

Both panted, staring intently at each other. They were supreme Sword Dao experts of their respective eras. Despite having met comparable opponents, they had never encountered one to rival them in Sword Dao alone.

“Immortal Fairy, who will win?” Lu Yang asked anxiously.

Although the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was unfamiliar with strength, she could discern differences in strength.

“Tsk, with how they’re fighting, it will probably take at least a day or two for an outcome. However, that Sword Tower girl’s foundation is too weak; she can’t last that long.”

“Ah?” Lu Yang grew concerned for the Sword Tower Supreme Lord on Mingtai’s behalf.

Liu Ningxuan had noticed this too. Although he was a sword spirit and couldn’t revert to human form, his foundation was solid, unlike the Sword Tower Supreme Lord, who was like a flickering candle soon to be snuffed out.

Then the Everlasting Immortal Fairy added, “But with a third party’s intervention, Liu Ningxuan could be dealt with quickly.”

“A third party’s intervention?”

Just as Lu Yang was puzzled about where a third party could come from, he saw a familiar figure soar up high, joining the Sword Tower Supreme Lord.

“Fellow Daoist, I’m here to help you.”

“Yun Mengmeng?!”

“Miss Yun?”

Recognizing that figure, Lu Yang was stunned. Yun Mengmeng has been freeloading off me on meals all this time. How did she suddenly become a third party capable of fighting alongside the Sword Tower Supreme Lord?

Tower Leader Guan and the others hadn’t expected Lu Yang’s acquaintance to be so formidable. freewebnovel.com

“Her Golden Core cultivation was a disguise!” Lu Yang figured it out. This Yun Mengmeng hasn’t been honest, huh?

“Wait, Immortal Fairy, why didn’t you tell me?” I can’t see through her, but surely the Immortal Fairy could!

He frantically recalled their conversations. I don’t think I’ve said anything terribly rude to Senior Yun Mengmeng.

The only potential problem is her good sister's identity. I had apparently offered to teach her swordplay.

For some reason, Lu Yang grew restless as a sense of foreboding swelled within him.

“I saw you were getting along well with her. I was worried that if I had told you her cultivation, you'd hold back and spoil the fun.” With that, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy made a face at him and turned away, ignoring him.

“Who are you?!” Liu Ningxuan was startled by Yun Mengmeng’s appearance. He and the Sword Tower Supreme Lord were in a delicate balance; the slightest shift could tip the scales of victory.

Yun Mengmeng initially wanted to introduce herself, but reconsidered. There’s already an immortal named Yun Mengmeng, but I’m not an immortal; if I use that name, won't it bring disgrace to the name?

“My name is Yun Zhi.”

Lu Yang’s legs turned to jelly, and he almost wanted to drop to his knees.

I’m toast. The Immortal Fairy doomed me.

Chapter 915: Hard Counter

“So it’s Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi.” Liu Ningxuan eyed Yun Mengmeng warily. For her to dare intervene in our battle, she must be confident.

“Many thanks for your assistance, Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi. The Sword Tower will definitely repay you generously!” the Sword Tower Supreme Lord declared.

Both Liu Ningxuan and the Sword Tower Supreme Lord were from the ancient era and had never heard of Yun Zhi.

Coincidentally, everyone present except them had heard of the name.

The Sword Tower’s higher-ups cast peculiar glances at Yun Mengmeng. Not only had they heard of Yun Zhi, but they had also met her many times.

You’re clearly not her.

However, Tower Leader Guan offered a different view. “No, perhaps she truly is Yun Zhi.”

“How so?”

“Think about it. She claims to be Yun Zhi and is familiar with Lu Yang. Moreover, Yun Zhi has always kept a low profile and dislikes showing herself in public. It’s perfectly normal for her to disguise herself.”

“That makes sense.”

No wonder he’s the Tower Leader; he thinks a step ahead of us.

The sword cultivators attending the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony had only heard of the name Yun Zhi and never seen her before.

“Yun Zhi? I recall she’s the Big Senior Sister of the Dao-Seeking Sect. It’s just that she rarely makes a move. It’s hard to gauge her strength.”

“It shouldn’t be a problem. I heard our sect leader say that Yun Zhi is at least at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and may even be a half-immortal; she’s extremely strong.” A sword cultivator of extraordinary background shared more secrets.

Only Lu Yang wore a bitter expression. Miss Yun, I treated you well. How could you sabotage me like this?

“Heaven-Earth Single Sword!” Liu Ningxuan shouted, taking the initiative. Eliminating Yun Mengmeng first would restore the balance between him and the Sword Tower Supreme Lord.

Yun Mengmeng sensed the destructive intent from the Chengying Sword but reacted too late. She was sent flying by the strike and got embedded in the sword vault’s wall.

“I thought you had some skill. It turns out you’re just a little lass who has just advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.” Liu Ningxuan laughed out loud. All that nervousness was for nothing. A mere Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator isn’t significant enough to tip the scales.

“Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi!” The Sword Tower Supreme Lord was shocked. How is she gone before the fight has even started?

On the other hand, Lu Yang was surprised by Yun Mengmeng’s cultivation realm. If she and Big Senior Sister are sisters, their ages should be close. Senior Brother Dai Bufan is similar in age to Big Senior Sister and is only at the Intermediate Fusion Stage, yet Yun Mengmeng is already at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?

This cultivation talent could be called terrifying.

“Scared me to death.” Yun Mengmeng emerged from the wall, still shaken. She rarely exchanged blows with others, much less fight with her life on the line. Her journey to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage had been smooth sailing. Liu Ningxuan’s sudden sword strike had genuinely caught her off guard.

“You didn’t even warn me before attacking. I thought I was done for.” Despite the lingering fear, Yun Mengmeng felt that the move was nothing special.

Liu Ningxuan scrunched up his brows. This sword strike was enough to pierce a Basic Transcendent Tribulation xuanwu. Why is she completely unscathed?

My judgment about her cultivation realm can’t be wrong.

Strange.

“Again, again! This time, I won’t let you hit me!” Yun Mengmeng giggled.

“Silent Annihilation Sword Technique!” Liu Ningxuan swung his sword again, even faster than before. The speed exceeded the reaction limits of a Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator!

Boom!

Yun Mengmeng was struck again and sent flying away.

Liu Ningxuan stared at her in disbelief. She’s still completely unscathed!

“I refuse to believe this!” Just as Liu Ningxuan prepared a more powerful strike, a surge of ferocious sword qi rushed at him.

“Am I invisible to you?!” the Sword Tower Supreme Lord yelled, hope rising as she witnessed Yun Mengmeng’s mysterious resilience. It seemed that Yun Mengmeng wasn’t as weak as she had appeared.

“Soul Sword Dao Field!”

“Silent Annihilation Sword Dao Field!”

Both fields manifested once more, covering the sky and ground. Yun Mengmeng mounted a demon phantom and charged at Liu Ningxuan.

Liu Ningxuan sneered. Fool. Any living being entering my Silent Annihilation Sword Dao Field will be shredded by destructive intent. There are no exceptions!

Sure enough, as the fierce demon mount stepped into the field, it was instantly annihilated.

However, Yun Mengmeng dismounted and continued forward unscathed.

“This is impossible!”

She gently extended her palm.

“Falling Cloud Palm.”

As she delivered the strike, white clouds appeared behind her, undulating like the ocean, soft enough to lull one to sleep. The clouds condensed in her palm, forming a seal that struck the Chengying Sword’s hilt, sending it tumbling through the air.

None present understood why Yun Mengmeng was completely unaffected by the Silent Annihilation Sword Dao Field. Even the Sword Tower Supreme Lord could only ram it with her field, not daring to enter personally.

Only Lu Yang roughly deduced the reason.

“She has an Incipient Dao Fruit!”

Yun Mengmeng’s cultivation was indeed at the Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage, but a Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator could also possess an Incipient Dao Fruit!

She’s not a Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator but a half-immortal!

“Unharmed by attacks and unaffected by the Silent Annihilation Sword Dao Field. Her Incipient Dao Fruit should be related to defense, like the Vajra or Immovable Incipient Dao Fruits, or perhaps she possesses an Incipient Dao Fruit of an Everlasting nature?!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s face was wreathed in smiles. “You guessed it right. She has an Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit.”

Everlasting—constant, unchanging, and eternal—was the antithesis of Silent Annihilation.

Liu Ningxuan’s proud Silent Annihilation intent had zero effect on Yun Mengmeng!

Unless he possessed the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit!

But a sword spirit couldn’t possess one!

Lu Yang figured it out. No wonder the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said a third party’s intervention could shift things. She hard-counters Liu Ningxuan.

“It’s just that this little lass’s combat experience is lacking. She’s clumsy in her movements, and with her limited cultivation, her offensive power is insufficient.”

How could the sword cultivators be aware of all this? When they saw that Yun Mengmeng seemed to be possessed by a divine being, resembling the golden arhat from the legends and impervious to all spells, they were instantly dumbstruck. Yun Zhi is indeed utterly terrifying. To think she can suppress Liu Ningxuan!

Yun Mengmeng stood at the forefront. No sword technique Liu Ningxuan employed could injure her.

“Stay away!” Liu Ningxuan cried out as Yun Mengmeng approached again. If he weren’t a sword spirit, he would be sweating profusely right now.

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord followed close behind, raising the Hanguang Sword with a shout. “Sever!”

The runes on the sword flashed, merging into the blade with resonant clangs as it descended with the might to sweep across the world.

This strike chipped the Chengying Sword. Liu Ningxuan’s form flickered; his foundation was finally damaged.

Just as the Sword Tower Supreme Lord and Yun Mengmeng were prepared to shatter the Chengying Sword together, the sky suddenly darkened, shrouded in an ominous gloom.

A figure slowly appeared above the ruins of the sword vault with a cold expression, holding a broken bowl. As the bowl was tossed upward, it enveloped the entire Sword Tower.

Gazing at the Hanguang Sword and the Chengying Sword, he revealed a sliver of a smile.

“I happen to lack some materials for forging immortal swords—you all will suffice.”

Seeing that figure, Lu Yang’s expression shifted.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal!

Chapter 916: The Bizarre Heaven Mandate Immortal

“Who goes there?!” the Sword Tower Supreme Lord hollered, lifting her head to gaze at that immortal figure, feeling like a formidable foe was upon her.

The aura he casually emits is far stronger than mine before I faced the Immortal Ascension Tribulation.

An immortal! He’s definitely an immortal!

As Liu Ningxuan stared at that arrogant figure, various unpleasant memories surged forth. Through gritted teeth, he slowly uttered three words. “Heaven Mandate Immortal...”

He had heard clearly. The Heaven Mandate Immortal intended to use them to forge immortal swords. If Chengying Sword gets refined, can I even survive then?

Stupid mouth! Who told you to say that something had likely happened to the Heaven Mandate Immortal?!

Great, now he’s appeared.

“What? He’s the legendary Heaven Mandate Immortal, one of the Four Ancient Immortals?!”

Liu Ningxuan’s voice wasn’t loud, but after the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s entrance, a deathly silence had draped over the entire venue. His words reached everyone clearly, causing blood to drain from their faces.

They could distinctly sense the malice emanating from the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

He comes with hostile intentions!

The Four Ancient Immortals were the most primordial immortals. As their ages were too distant in the past, many legends had become veiled in myth, making the Four Ancient Immortals seem all the more terrifying.

“Immortal Fairy, is that the Heaven Mandate Immortal?” Lu Yang’s brow clouded with worry. I can’t help but feel that this figure’s demeanor seems vastly different from the Heaven Mandate Immortal I encountered in the heavenly tribulation.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy remained silent, lost in thought.

Realizing that matters had spiraled beyond control, Lu Yang urgently tried summoning Yun Zhi, but to no avail.

After appearing, the Heaven Mandate Immortal had tossed a broken bowl, enclosing Sword Tower. Lu Yang felt that this bowl had severed all connection to the outside world, preventing him from contacting Yun Zhi.

“Immortal Fairy, what is this bowl?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy knitted her brows as she pointed out the broken bowl’s origin. “It looks like a Cosmos Cover refined by the Heaven Mandate Immortal, though it seems cruder than the one in my memory, as if it is newly forged. No one can escape this place, and neither can messages be transmitted outside. It can temporarily fool the national fortune’s detection, creating an illusion of normalcy. He’s probably worried that those two from the Jiang and Meng families would discover him.” She also sensed something off about the Heaven Mandate Immortal and refrained from rashly revealing herself to him.

Seeming to have made up her mind, she said seriously, “Xiao Yangzi, rest assured, this immortal is here. You’ll be safe.”

Hearing Liu Ningxuan call out his title, the Heaven Mandate Immortal showed mild surprise. “Oh, interesting. Who would have thought a mere sword spirit would recognize me?”

Bafflement flashed through Lu Yang’s mind. The Heaven Mandate Immortal doesn’t know Liu Ningxuan?

He hurriedly asked, “Immortal Fairy, had the Heaven Mandate Immortal and Liu Ningxuan ever met before in the ancient era?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was equally puzzled. She wished to scrutinize the Heaven Mandate Immortal with her immortal consciousness, but feared being discovered and putting Lu Yang in danger. “Of course, they’ve met. They even clashed many times.”

Lu Yang was perplexed. “So has the Heaven Mandate Immortal lost his memory? Or is that not the real Heaven Mandate Immortal but some entity possessing his body?”

This Heaven Mandate Immortal who suddenly popped up is absolutely bizarre. Everything smells fishy.

Apart from this, Lu Yang had another doubt.

In the three hundred thousand years since the Great Qian Dynasty, the Heaven Mandate Immortal had never appeared, yet this is the first time he’s showing himself?

If so, the timing is too coincidental.

If not, then why had there been no news of his previous appearances...?

Lu Yang’s forehead broke out in a cold sweat. I hope this is Heaven Mandate Immortal’s first appearance; otherwise, it would mean that matters are far worse.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal acted as if he were utterly oblivious to Liu Ningxuan and the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s wariness, remarking casually, “Will you hand over these two swords willingly, or must I fetch them myself?”

“In your dreams!”

“Wishful thinking!”

Neither Liu Ningxuan nor the Sword Tower Supreme Lord would surrender their swords. For Liu Ningxuan, the Chengying Sword was his foundation, and for the Sword Tower Supreme Lord, Mingtai’s life depended on it.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal thought nothing of their defiance and burst out laughing. However, his laughter didn’t dispel the ominous atmosphere; instead, it made the area seem even more eerie.

“Just like this, just like this—it’s only interesting when there’s resistance.”

Scanning the sword cultivators below, he grew even more pleased. “It seems that I have a pretty good luck today. I sensed two swords here that could be used for forging immortal swords, but I never expected there to be so many sword cultivators as well.

“Perfect! Refining all of you into a single soul might just suffice as my immortal sword’s sword spirit!”

The “immortal sword” he spoke of wasn’t an immortal treasure like the Chengying Sword but an immortal artifact on par with the Qingfeng Sword—a bona fide immortal sword! Otherwise, he wouldn’t have wanted to use two immortal swords as raw materials.

Everyone below felt their hearts turn to ash. The Heaven Mandate Immortal wants to refine us. How could we survive that?

Many desperately tried to flee, but it was futile. How could their meager cultivation break a magical treasure like the Cosmos Cover?

Lu Yang’s heart sank. His worst fear had come true—the Heaven Mandate Immortal intended to silence everyone. This explains why there hasn’t been any information about him since the end of the ancient era.

Anywhere he appeared would be reduced to a dead zone! Especially during the Great Qian and Great Yu eras, when cultivators often destroyed cities, his occasional attacks blended into the chaos, allowing him to remain undetected.

In the Great Xia era, perhaps he had restrained himself a little. Could some of the unsolved massacres not be the work of diabolic creeds but his doing?!

And in places like the East Sea and Demon Region, they have been scattered like sand for the past three hundred thousand years. No one would thoroughly investigate even if entire tribes were exterminated!

“Silent Annihilation Sword Dao Field!”

“Soul Sword Dao Field!”

“Heaven-Earth Single Sword!”

“Vast Wave Sword Technique!”

Two peak Sword Dao experts joined forces, unleashing killing strikes right from the outset. This was an immortal they were facing. If they held back now, they would die without getting to be buried!

“Falling Cloud Palm!” Yun Mengeng steeled herself and made a move too.

Granny is right. The outside world is truly dangerous. My puny strength is utterly inadequate before true experts.

Facing the trio’s combined assault, the Heaven Mandate Immortal neither dodged nor flinched. He simply stood there, allowing the strikes to land, raising clouds of dust and smoke that obscured everything.

When the crowd below saw the three who had been fighting moments earlier now joining forces with overwhelming might, a spark of hope for survival ignited in their hearts.

Yet when the dust dispersed, the Heaven Mandate Immortal emerged completely unharmed!

“An immortal treasure artifact spirit, a half-immortal remnant soul, and a Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. You three think you can harm me?”

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord gritted her teeth. If I were at my peak, I would have a slim chance to fight him to the death. But I’m now just a remnant soul; harming him is indeed wishing for too much.

“Again!”

The three joined forces again, hoping to seek an opportunity for survival. freewebnovel.com

Surprisingly, Liu Ningxuan’s Heaven-Earth Single Sword didn’t target the Heaven Mandate Immortal but the Cosmos Cover instead.

Thud!

Like a stone dropping into a calm river, the Cosmos Cover rippled, absorbing his sword strike.

“Trying to flee?” The Heaven Mandate Immortal strode forward, space shrinking beneath his feet.

In one step, he reached Liu Ningxuan and extended a hand to seize the Chengying Sword as if he were grabbing a chick. “I happen to lack memories of the ancient times. Let me see yours.”

He placed his hand on Liu Ningxuan’s head. With a blood-curdling scream, Liu Ningxuan’s eyes rolled back, and he lost consciousness, helpless as the Heaven Mandate Immortal searched his soul.

When Liu Ningxuan woke up again, he would be deranged and reduced to a fool, no longer himself.

Acquiring Liu Ningxuan’s memories, the Heaven Mandate Immortal instantly made sense of things. “So you are Liu Ningxuan, the number one sword cultivator of ancient times, and also the sworn enemy of this body. You used Person and Sword as One to escape.

“But so what? Haven’t you still fallen into my hands?”

Chapter 917: Corpse-Slashing Method and Corpse-Liberation Transcendence Method

After acquiring Liu Ningxuan’s memories, the Heaven Mandate Immortal radiated renewed vigor, and the atmosphere around Sword Tower shed some of its gloominess.

He had long been gathering information on ancient matters, seeking to understand this body’s former self. Unfortunately, ancient history was too messy, resembling scattered sand. It was extremely difficult to piece together the full picture.

With Liu Ningxuan’s memories of ancient times, some of his regrets were assuaged.

Suddenly, the Heaven Mandate Immortal sensed two fierce attacks shot toward his back. By the time he turned his head, the strikes were less than three inches from his brow!

“Ten Thousand Swords Return to One!”

“Palm Lightning!”

Seizing the opportunity while the Heaven Mandate Immortal was occupied with absorbing Liu Ningxuan’s memories, the Sword Tower Supreme Lord and Yun Mengmeng launched another joint assault.

Fortunately, his momentary distraction gave them a chance to accumulate power for an attack.

Countless sword lights emerged from all directions, responding to the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s call. Like a meteor shower, they streaked across the sky, fusing with the Hanguang Sword with unstoppable momentum.

The Soul Sword Dao Field spread beneath her feet, and various sword-qi demons merged into the Hanguang Sword. Her eyes flickered with fortitude and determination. This was a move originally meant for Liu Ningxuan, but now, she had to use it against the far more powerful Heaven Mandate Immortal.

A dazzling light bloomed in Yun Mengmeng’s palm like newborn lightning, accompanied by deafening thunder rolls. She desperately compressed this lightning, condensing it to a single point.

Seeing that, the Heaven Mandate Immortal jerked his head back, then violently thrust it forward, headbutting both the Sword Tower Supreme Lord and Yun Mengmeng!

“Haha, you do have some skill. My effort in deliberately leaving you an opening wasn’t wasted.”

“He doesn’t possess the Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly remarked.

“Why?”

“If he had it, the Palm Lightning wouldn’t dare to approach him, yet he just tanked the attack head-on just now!

“No Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit, no memories of the ancient era, and he even said ‘this body’... Could the Heaven Mandate Immortal have used the ‘Corpse-Slashing Method’ or the ‘Corpse-Liberation Transcendence Method?’”

“Corpse-Slashing Method and Corpse-Liberation Transcendence Method?” It was Lu Yang’s first time hearing these terms.

“I used the Corpse-Slashing Method when I slew the version of myself with the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit.

“The Corpse-Liberation Transcendence Method leaves the physical body behind while the immortal soul transcends.

“These two methods can make one stronger, but the risk of failure is high. Failure results in what we see here—an immortal corpse left behind, reborn and reanimated, forgetting its past life, and becoming a completely new entity.

“It’s just unclear which method the Heaven Mandate Immortal failed at. Though the good news is that since this immortal corpse lacks the Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit, the real Heaven Mandate Immortal hasn’t died. If the Heaven Mandate Immortal had perished, the Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit would have transferred to this immortal corpse.

Lu Yang couldn’t help asking, “Could it be that the immortal corpse developed spirit intelligence?”

He felt that a sentient corpse would fit this Heaven Mandate Immortal’s behavior.

Lu Yang recalled the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mentioning that the Epoch Immortal’s true body, the Jianmu World Tree, had once died. It was after eons that a new Jianmu grew from the old, giving birth to a new sentience that was the Epoch Immortal.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “Impossible. For an immortal corpse to develop spirit intelligence, it requires eons. Three hundred thousand years isn’t enough.”

Understanding the origin of this Heaven Mandate Immortal didn’t resolve the deadly situation. Lu Yang and the others were still in a perilous predicament. Once the Sword Tower Supreme Lord and Yun Mengmeng fell, there would be no one else to stop him, and demise would await them all.

“Immortal-Stunning Single Sword!” Suddenly, the Sword Tower Supreme Lord yelled, employing some method that elevated her power severalfold beyond Ten Thousand Swords Return to One.

“No!” Mingtai cried. As her sword spirit, he knew exactly what ‘Immortal-Stunning Single Sword’ meant. It was the ultimate sword technique that burned one’s lifespan. Once executed, even Master’s remnant soul would vanish!

Hearing Mingtai’s shout, tears streamed from the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s eyes, but she pressed forward, lunging toward the Heaven Mandate Immortal with steadfast resolve!

The Heaven Mandate Immortal was unfazed, curious to see what power this strike could contain.

Amidst the resplendent sword light, a few drops of immortal blood fell from his brow.

At the cost of her life, the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s strike had finally wounded the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

Meanwhile, her remnant soul thinned. With a clang, the Hanguang Sword dropped to the ground.

She couldn’t even hold her sword anymore!

Touching the blood on his brow, the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s veins bulged with rage as he roared, “I initially planned to play with you a little longer before killing you. You really don’t know what’s good for you!”

All this time, the Heaven Mandate Immortal had been deliberately taking hits. If I fight seriously, victory will be instant!

“You’re courting death!” Enraged, he delivered a strike with his palm.

Winds howled, clouds surged, and heaven and earth changed color, crushing everyone with suffocating pressure.

Suddenly, Yun Mengmeng appeared, shielding the Sword Tower Supreme Lord.

Boom!

Yun Mengmeng was sent flying. Fortunately, her Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit healed her injuries.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal smirked coldly, discerning that Yun Mengmeng wasn’t a simple Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. She possesses an Incipient Dao Fruit with healing effects, which makes her a half-immortal.

But so what if she’s a half-immortal?

“You want to die together? Then I’ll grant your wish!” He prepared to strike again.

This time, I’ll leave no survivors!

“Wait! You cannot kill them!” A voice suddenly rang out, its tone resolute.

“Who are you?!” The Heaven Mandate Immortal hadn’t sensed anyone passing through the Cosmos Cover. Is it someone inside?

Soon, his gaze landed on Lu Yang.

Having absorbed Liu Ningxuan’s memories, he recognized Lu Yang. It’s the young cultivator who inherited this body’s legacy.

Seeing Lu Yang step forward, everyone suddenly recalled that Lu Yang had obtained the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s legacy. Perhaps this connection would make the Heaven Mandate Immortal consider sparing us.

“I obtained the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s legacy. Don’t you want to know where I met him and received his legacy?!

“If you kill the two of them, I won’t tell you where!”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal’s lips twisted into a cold smirk. In an instant, he was before Lu Yang, his hand on his head. “Why would I need you to tell me? I’ll just search your soul directly.”

Lu Yang’s gaze was unflinching as he met the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s eyes, facing death with equanimity. “When I obtained the legacy, the Heaven Mandate Immortal placed a restriction in my mind. If my soul is searched, the restriction will automatically activate and destroy my mental space, ensuring the location of his legacy will never be known. If you don’t believe me, feel free to try!”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal was torn, unable to determine whether Lu Yang’s words were true or false. He truly wanted to know the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s location. “But the restriction won’t activate if you tell me the legacy’s location?”

Lu Yang shook his head. “Of course it will still activate.”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal exploded in anger. “How dare you toy with me!”

Lu Yang shook his head again. “Although I can’t say it directly, I can hint at it through narrating stories, thus bypassing the restriction.”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal’s eyes lit up, finding it a good idea. “Fine. I won’t kill the two of them or the rest. Speak!”

“How do I know you’ll keep your word?”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal sneered. “Kid, do you have a choice?!”

Lu Yang clenched his teeth. He indeed had no choice but to trust that the Heaven Mandate Immortal was someone who kept his promises.

“You must erect a barrier so that they don’t hear me.”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal could surmise that Lu Yang feared he would kill all witnesses afterward. To convince Lu Yang that he would keep his word, the Heaven Mandate Immortal casually set up a barrier.

“Satisfied now?”

Lu Yang nodded and slowly began. “This story begins in a place called the Ember Legacy Dynasty...”

Chapter 918: Luring the Tiger to Devour the Wolf

“Ember Legacy Dynasty?” The Heaven Mandate Immortal furrowed his brows. I’ve never heard of this dynasty.

Lu Yang narrated unhurriedly, “In the ancient epoch, the Four Ancient Immortals refined the stars into continents. Afterward, with supreme immortal might, they coalesced the power of faith and established the Ember Legacy Dynasty. Its indisputable strength far surpassed later dynasties like Great Qian, Great Yu, and Great Xia.

“The Ember Legacy Dynasty also had two great organizations: the Heavenly Court governing the yang world of the living and the Underworld governing the yin world of the dead.

“The Heavenly Court was omnipotent and ruled the world. Be it immortals or mortals, and regardless of cultivation, all had to abide by its heavenly laws and immortal regulations.

“The Heavenly Court’s ruler was not one of the Four Ancient Immortals. She was a peerless female immortal who had perished in the ancient era. Through overcoming trials of reincarnation, she defied the great laws of life and death, condensed a supreme immortal body through faith power, came back to life, and returned as the Heavenly Court Ruler with overwhelming momentum.”

“A Heavenly Court Ruler who came back to life? Interesting.” The Heaven Mandate Immortal smiled, contemplating the hidden clues within Lu Yang’s tale to figure out where exactly the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s legacy was.

Could it be hinting that the legacy is at a place where yin and yang intersect? What places nowadays are related to yin and yang?

Lu Yang continued, “The Heavenly Court Ruler wielded power capable of annihilating the world and reducing all things to one. Even the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others had to bow in submission, conceding they were inferior.

“...One day, the Heavenly Court Ruler suddenly went mad and wanted to destroy the Heavenly Court, the Underworld, and the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

“The Four Ancient Immortals and the Left Historian Immortal, who attained immortality during the Ember Legacy Dynasty, intervened to stop her. Yet no one anticipated the Epoch Immortal’s sudden death, and the perpetrator remained unknown.

“The remaining four immortals ceased cooperating and fought separately, yet none was a match for the Heavenly Court Ruler. Even the Qilin Immortal was gravely wounded after battling the Heavenly Court Ruler to protect the Dragon Ancient Ancestor.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal battled the Heavenly Court Ruler...” Lu Yang paused here.

“What was the battle’s outcome?!” the Heaven Mandate Immortal asked urgently, sensing this might be key to the legacy’s location.

“Indeed, what was the outcome?” Lu Yang smiled, deliberately returning the question.

Only he could hear the Everlasting Immortal Fairy shouting in his ear. “Xiao Yangzi, help is here!”

Seeing Lu Yang deliberately keeping him in suspense, the Heaven Mandate Immortal felt belittled. Just as he was about to act, an inexplicable sense of crisis suddenly gripped him.

He jerked his head upward. A pitch-black pillar of light descended from the heavens, carrying a destructive force that seemed capable of annihilating the world, piercing directly through the Cosmos Cover.

After piercing the Cosmos Cover, the black light pillar showed no sign of slowing and plummeted straight down.

And directly beneath it was the Heaven Mandate Immortal and Lu Yang!

A wide smile gradually spread across Lu Yang’s visage as he looked disdainfully at the Heaven Mandate Immortal and murmured softly, “Goodbye, fool.”

In a fury, the Heaven Mandate Immortal wished to kill Lu Yang, but he had no time to spare. The cataclysmic strike above came too suddenly, and he must defend with all his might!

“Xiao Yangzi, come in!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pulled Lu Yang into the Qingfeng Sword’s small world.

Boom!

The black light pillar descended, obliterating everything. Wherever it passed, all things perished, turning to nothingness. It slammed right into the Heaven Mandate Immortal, driving him deep underground through thousands of li, creating a bottomless pit!

A golden helmet materialized above the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s head, but it was pierced, its edges charred black. Terrifying Silent Annihilation power spread, corroding the golden helmet.

In the blink of an eye, the golden helmet dissolved into nothing and vanished.

No one had expected this turn of events. They didn’t know where this terrifying assault came from and why it targeted the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

“Could Lu Yang survive such an attack?” a sword cultivator mumbled.

Everyone fell silent. Such an attack would likely kill even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, much less Lu Yang, a mere Divine Transfiguration cultivator.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal panted as he flew out from the pit. His eyes were wide with rage as he glared upward and demanded, “Who are you?!”

Above the Cosmos Cover, a figure shrouded in gray mist appeared, their features indistinguishable. The voice was cold and heartless, like the lofty heavens casually deciding mortals’ fates.

“Those who know my identity shall die.”

The incensed Heaven Mandate Immortal was taken aback. Who are you? When did I know you? If I know who you are, why would I have asked?

A series of questions surfaced in his mind, though none were answered.

“Well, well, well, you think one sneak attack makes you impressive? You’re courting death!” Shock and anger surged through him—shock that only the sudden summoning of the golden helmet had saved him from death, and anger at her unreasonable, unprovoked assault.

“Hundred-Refinement Hegemon Halberd!

“Sky-Reaching Chainmail!

“Soul-Shattering Immortal Spear!”

One by one, the Heaven Mandate Immortal produced immortal artifacts. As he lacked a Dao Fruit, he compensated with the quantity of immortal artifacts. I had prepared these to deal with the original Heaven Mandate Immortal. Now, I’ll use them against this haughty gray-mist immortal!

Watching him wrap himself tightly, Hui Doudou revealed a mocking smile. “Foolish. Laughable.”

Although I don’t know how this Heaven Mandate Immortal is related to the real Heaven Mandate Immortal, it doesn’t matter. All who know of my existence must die.

As for that little fellow who had informed me, I wonder where he’s hiding. I can’t detect him at all. Strange.

“Lu Yang!” The crowd of sword cultivators and Yun Mengmeng anxiously went to search for him.

Hiding within the Qingfeng Sword’s small world, Lu Yang exhaled a sigh of relief, collapsing onto the ground and panting from fatigue. Observing Hui Doudou overpower the Heaven Mandate Immortal outside, he revealed a relieved smile.

“She’s finally here. As I thought, she can’t find this place.”

Recalling how Hui Doudou had targeted him and Ao Ling, Lu Yang could roughly figure out the pattern behind Hui Doudou’s pursuit.

Back then, he and Ao Ling had stayed in the Dragon Pearl for days, yet Hui Doudou didn’t make a move. Only shortly after their departure did she appear.

This implies that small worlds can block her perception.

And my Qingfeng Sword possesses a small world.

“Thank goodness for the Qingfeng Sword.”

If it weren’t for the Qingfeng Sword, I couldn’t have survived that terrifying gray light beam. If I’m still outside, Hui Doudou might casually kill me with just a flick of her finger anytime during the battle.

The truth was that he knew nothing of the legacy’s location. If he did, he would have gone there long ago.

Lu Yang had simply sought a pretext for the Heaven Mandate Immortal to listen to Hui Doudou’s story patiently. After all, it would take time for Hui Doudou to arrive. Not only did he have to inform him of Hui Doudou’s matters, but he also needed to stall him as much as possible.

He had used the legacy’s location as bait because he was convinced that this Heaven Mandate Immortal would desperately look for the real Heaven Mandate Immortal. Only by finding the real Heaven Mandate Immortal and killing him could this Heaven Mandate Immortal obtain the Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit.

Given that Hui Doudou would kill everyone who knew of her, Lu Yang had ensured that no one would overhear his conversation with the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

You can do it, Heaven Mandate Immortal. You’ve got to hold out a little longer. Lu Yang silently prayed for him.

Chapter 919: The Powerful Hui Doudou

“Casually deciding this esteemed one’s life or death...do you think you’re unbeatable? Pfft—”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal uttered a few words of bravado before engaging Hui Doudou, only to be sent flying by a single kick. Had he not been fully clad in immortal armor, that strike alone would have cost him half his life.

What kind of strength is that?!

The Heaven Mandate Immortal’s expression was one of pure incredulity. Such offensive power is too absurd. Even if I’m armed with immortal weapons, I can’t muster such power.

Hui Doudou was not a person of words. Faced with his persistent “Who are you?” she showed no intention to answer, attacking in silence.

Watching the two immortals clash, Yun Mengmeng was again convinced that her half-immortal cultivation was indeed insignificant outside; it was only barely enough to show off in secret domains.

One Heaven Mandate Immortal popping up could be a coincidence, but Hui Doudou’s appearance couldn’t be a coincidence as well.

This means that immortals are as common as hemp in the outside world.

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord also felt that leaving a remnant soul to protect Sword Tower was somewhat superfluous. Why has Sword Tower attracted so many immortals? Who could protect it?

“Taste my halberd!” the Heaven Mandate Immortal bellowed, swinging the Hundred-Refinement Hegemon Halberd. This was his proud immortal weapon, its weight rivaling a hundred thousand mountains. Any Transcendent Tribulation cultivator who touched it would meet their demise.

An immortal saber suddenly coalesced in Hui Doudou’s hand. Space collapsed, and time fell into chaos. In truth, this wasn’t a saber, but a beam of light bearing Hui Doudou’s intent of death and finality.

The heavenly saber destroyed everything. The moment the Hundred-Refinement Hegemon Halberd touched it, a massive notch appeared.

Before the Heaven Mandate Immortal could react, Hui Doudou exerted more force with her wrist and channeled her will into the immortal saber, severing the halberd as easily as cutting a hemp stalk. The halbert dropped to the ground with a clang, creating a bottomless pit as the earth shook.

Seeing that Hui Doudou planned to strike him with the immortal saber again, the Heaven Mandate Immortal hastily raised the halberd to block.

Swish, swish.

With two swings from Hui Doudou, the halberd shaft was cleaved into three pieces.

Before the immortal saber, ten-thousand-year Bodhi wood was no different from tofu.

“Three Heads Six Arms!” With a shout, the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s neck bulged, and two extra heads emerged, while arms sprouted from his back and beneath his armpits.

In this state, he wielded six immortal artifacts: the Soul-Shattering Immortal Spear, the Sky-Containing Purple Gourd, the Ocean-Overturning Immortal Seal...each forged from copious amounts of immortal gold and stained with immortal blood. Any single one in the outside world would be a priceless treasure and a true immortal artifact.

If Yun Mengmeng obtained just one, she could handle Liu Ningxuan alone, even without the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s cooperation. freewebnovel.com

Despite facing the Heaven Mandate Immortal armed with six immortal artifacts, Hui Doudou remained unperturbed, not even blinking. She dismissed her immortal saber and recalled her death and finality intent. Fierce crimson flames ignited around her like Buddhist karmic fire and the wails of myriad ghosts.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal frowned. He couldn’t discern the flame’s origin, but found it extremely dangerous.

These were flames refined from the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit, the World-Destroying Fire that had burned the Ember Legacy Dynasty to the ground. In terms of power, no flame could match it.

Unfortunately, the Heaven Mandate Immortal was ignorant of its might. Had he known, he would have instantly taken to his heels.

“Die!” The Heaven Mandate Immortal spat a mouthful of immortal essence blood, empowering his six artifacts with increasingly terrifying might.

Hui Doudou was wreathed in the World-Destroying Fire. The moment the Soul-Shattering Immortal Spear touched her, its tip melted into a blob of mixed immortal gold.

“How is this possible?!” The Heaven Mandate Immortal was astonished. This is an immortal artifact. How could it have melted in an instant?!

“Your artifact-refinement skill is inferior to the real Heaven Mandate Immortal. What a waste of immortal gold,” Hui Doudou assessed coldly. Toward the end of the Ember Legacy Dynasty, I had fought the real Heaven Mandate Immortal, who wielded various immortal artifacts. He was far harder to deal with than this soulless shell.

“Sky-Containing Purple Gourd!”

As the gourd’s mouth opened, a suction force powerful enough to warp space sought to suck her in. Anyone who entered the gourd would dissolve into pus in moments.

Hui Doudou shot a wisp of Silent Annihilation energy. With a bang, the gourd exploded into fragments.

“Ocean-Overturning Immortal Seal!”

“Bagua Mirror!”

“...”

One by one, the Heaven Mandate Immortal produced immortal artifacts. However, before Hui Doudou’s overwhelming might, they were as ineffective as toys at the risk of being destroyed at any time!

Realizing the vast gulf between them, he even doubted that possessing the Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit would make him her match.

Flee!

A single step could carry him millions of li. With just a step, he could escape to the edge of the world.

However, Hui Doudou stamped lightly, disrupting spatial laws. No matter what immortal art the Heaven Mandate Immortal employed, he remained rooted in place.

“Nothing special.”

Step by step, Hui Doudou approached the Heaven Mandate Immortal. In his terrified gaze, she grasped his head, and the World-Destroying Fire ignited within him. It burned from the inside out, from his soul to his flesh, burning through every orifice until only a charred corpse remained.

In his final moments, he finally deduced what her words about “those who know of her existence” meant.

She is the Heavenly Court Ruler whom Lu Yang mentioned...

Lu Yang has gotten the better of me...

Hui Doudou casually tossed aside the corpse and searched for Lu Yang.

Suddenly, her hair stood on end. The gray mist around her had grown unstable. She sensed that a calamity was imminent if she didn’t escape.

It’s that self-proclaimed Heavenly Court Creed Leader, Yun Mengmeng!

This is indeed a trap!

After the incident at the East Sea, I had refrained from making a move on Lu Yang or Ao Ling because I feared that Yun Mengmeng would use them as bait.

Damn it, my worst fears have come true! Hui Doudou couldn’t be bothered to search for Lu Yang and bolted right away.

Seeing Hui Doudou scurry away, Lu Yang knew that Yun Zhi was coming.

“Phew, it’s finally over.”

Only then did Lu Yang dare to emerge from the Qingfeng Sword, though he was still weak and unsteady on his feet. Although he was physically unharmed, conversing with the murderous Heaven Mandate Immortal had been mentally taxing. Lu Yang feared any gesture might arouse suspicion. Even when Hui Doudou arrived, he remained tense.

Now that the overall situation had settled, his taut nerves relaxed, and the previously accumulated exhaustion washed over him, making him sleepy.

But he knew one task remained; he couldn’t rest yet.

Everyone rejoiced upon seeing Lu Yang.

“Lu Yang, so you’re fine!” Yun Mengmeng, who had the highest cultivation, ran the fastest, rushing to embrace Lu Yang.

“Gently, be more gentle, I’m dying.” Lu Yang winced. Yun Mengmeng’s embrace nearly broke his ribs.

“Oh, oh.” Startled, she released him.

“Master!” Amidst the cheers, Mingtai’s anguished cry drew everyone’s attention.

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s remnant soul had grown dim, nearly transparent. If she hadn’t been worried about Mingtai’s safety after the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s appearance, stubbornly clinging to her last breath, she would have dissipated long ago.

“Mingtai, I can no longer look after you. Take care.”

“Master!” Mingtai let out a heart-wrenching wail. It wasn’t easy for me to see Master again. Why must eternal separation come so soon?

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord spoke softly. “Don’t grieve. Life and death are part of the natural order. After so many years by my side, haven’t you comprehended such simple principles?”

She wished to wipe his tears, but lacked even the strength to touch anything tangible.

Everyone fell silent. The joy of surviving the hopeless catastrophe was greatly diminished.

“Senior Sword Tower Supreme Lord, I have a method that might preserve your soul.” With Yun Mengmeng’s support, Lu Yang approached Mingtai.

“What is it?”

“Abandon your Incipient Dao Fruit, perform Person and Sword as One, and become part of the Hanguang Sword.”

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s dim eyes gradually brightened at his words.

Right, why haven’t I considered this? If Liu Ningxuan can achieve the pinnacle of Person and Sword as One, there’s no reason I can’t.

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord sat in meditation on the spot, recalling the integral aspects of Person and Sword as One and Liu Ningxuan’s state, vaguely grasping how he had achieved it.

Soon, the Hanguang Sword trembled, merging with her soul. With the sword as a foundation, her nearly transparent soul gradually solidified.

“Master!” Mingtai shed tears of joy, embracing the Hanguang Sword and bawling again.

The Sword Tower Supreme Lord smiled playfully, tapping his nose. “Now you are the master.”

Seeing the final matter resolved, Lu Yang finally relaxed and collapsed into sleep, completely unresponsive to Yun Mengmeng’s anxious calls.

He didn’t know how long he slept, but was eventually roused by her voice. Blinking groggily, he saw that familiar, reassuring figure.

Big Senior Sister has arrived.

He vaguely saw Yun Mengmeng tugging at Yun Zhi’s sleeve, urgently beseeching, “Little Zhi, please save Lu Yang! I just found you a Sword Dao shifu; nothing must happen to him!”

Lu Yang had intended to wake up, but peacefully drifted back to sleep.

Senior Yun Mengmeng, I will definitely not save you in my next life.

Chapter 920: If I Recall Correctly, All I Wanted Was Just to Purchase a Sword

When Lu Yang awoke once more and saw the familiar canopy of leaves overhead, he knew Yun Zhi had brought him back to Heaven’s Gate Peak.

Whenever he was tired from cultivation, he would often lie beneath these trees, enjoying a moment of tranquility.

Heaven’s Gate Peak is still the most reassuring place.

I wonder how long I’ve been unconscious.

Come to think of it, I seem to have had a strange dream. Inside it, Big Senior Sister had taken me as her shifu, and I’d taught her Sword Dao.

Thank goodness it was just a dream.

Exhaling a sigh of relief, Lu Yang turned his head and saw Yun Zhi seated beside him. She was peeling an apple for him, her face blank, blending into the background like she was part of a painting.

Lu Yang jolted, sitting up abruptly. “Big Senior Sister!”

Yun Zhi lifted an eyelid and casually handed him the peeled apple. “Awake? You suffered immense mental shock at the Sword Tower ruins and fell unconscious. I suggest you rest well for a few days.”

“Yes, yes!”

Lu Yang gingerly accepted the apple, as if it were some magical treasure that could explode at any moment.

“Sword Tower ruins?” Lu Yang noticed a peculiar term.

Yun Zhi looked at him oddly. Is Little Junior Brother’s mind still fuzzy from waking? “After two successive major battles, the Sword Tower was reduced to rubble. Surely you don’t think that place can still be called the Sword Tower?

“More than half of the spirit swords in the sword vault were also lost in the battle. Restoring them all will take at least a century.”

Lu Yang shrank his neck, feeling somewhat apologetic toward the Sword Tower.

I’d visited the Sword Tower once, yet it collapsed, and the spirit swords in the sword vault are no more.

“But the good news is that the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s remnant soul survived using the method you taught. All of Sword Tower is deeply grateful to you.”

For the Sword Tower, as long as the Sword Tower Supreme Lord survived, losing the building and spirit swords were minor issues.

“You obtained the Chengying Sword at the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony. When I left, the Sword Tower requested that I pass it to you.” With a flick, the paring knife in Yun Zhi’s hand was enveloped by a long, pitch-black shadow. The knife elongated, gradually merging with the shadow until it became a sword as dark as the shadow.

It was none other than the Chengying Sword.

After acquiring the Chengying Sword, the Heaven Mandate Immortal deemed it below the level of immortal artifacts and hadn’t used it against Hui Doudou. During the battle, he had tossed it aside, sparing it from calamity.

With Liu Ningxuan dead, Lu Yang was finally the true master of both the Chengying Sword and the Seven Stars Sword Set.

It was only upon taking the sword that Lu Yang recalled his original purpose for attending the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony—to purchase a suitable sword from the Sword Tower.

Everything that followed was accidental.

Lu Yang stowed the Chengying Sword away properly. He was currently not in the appropriate state to have the Chengying Sword recognize him as its master.

“Now, who will explain what’s going on with this corpse?” From behind, Yun Zhi produced a charred corpse that was beyond recognition.

Hui Doudou was too ruthless. The Heaven Mandate Immortal’s body held no artifact-refinement value, barely even useful as a material for refining magical treasures. Yun Zhi found this rather regrettable.

“I heard from the Sword Tower that this corpse is the Heaven Mandate Immortal?”

“Mmhm. According to the Immortal Fairy’s analysis, the real Heaven Mandate Immortal failed in either the ‘Corpse Slashing Method’ or the ‘Corpse-Liberation Transcendence Method,’ thus splitting off this corpse with its own will.”

“Just as I thought,” Yun Zhi mumbled.

“Both methods can make one stronger. I believe the Heaven Mandate Immortal had to take the risk to deal with Hui Dou...Senior Gray Immortal Fairy.”

Yun Zhi nodded. It aligns with my speculation. This is definitely not the real Heaven Mandate Immortal.

Had it been the real Heaven Mandate Immortal, he would have lasted until she arrived, not dying so quickly. This Heaven Mandate Immortal lacked experience fighting peers and only knew to overwhelm others with his cultivation.
