“Given how many immortal artifacts the Heaven Mandate corpse forged, he likely prepared to fight the real Heaven Mandate Immortal.”

Yun Zhi found it a pity. During the battle, Hui Doudou had melted the artifacts into mixed immortal gold, which would stay a worthless heap of scrap unless they were separated. Among the people she knew, no one was capable of separating such mixed immortal gold.

Yun Zhi identified the underlying issue. No one had guarded the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s cultivation.

Both methods carry high risks of failure. Logically, the Heaven Mandate Immortal should have sought help to guard his cultivation. That way, even if he failed, the Heaven Mandate corpse wouldn’t have been able to escape.

Why hadn’t the Qilin Immortal and the Qilin Immortal looked out for him?

But such matters don’t need to be voiced, lest Little Junior Brother become too involved.

Yun Zhi felt helpless. Although I try my best to prevent Little Junior Brother from participating in matters related to ancient immortals, he always gets closer and closer whenever I’m not paying attention.

The last time I’d felt this way was when I taught him spells.

“Speaking of which, my safe return owes much to the Qingfeng Sword you gifted me, Big Senior Sister.” Lu Yang grinned. The Qingfeng Sword’s small world had saved his life.

“Big Senior Sister, I have a conjecture: to evade Hui Doudou’s perception, could the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others have decided to hide in a small world like what I did?”

“It’s possible. But small worlds are too numerous to search, and that’s not including the many hidden ones that remain undiscovered.”

Mobile small worlds like the Dragon Pearl and the Qingfeng Sword were rare, but fixed ones were innumerable.

Small worlds were a type of secret domain, worlds carved out by cultivators. From ancient times until now, who knew how many had been created?

Furthermore, even the universe above harbored countless undiscovered small worlds. Those who had created them and left legacies deliberately concealed their locations, leaving cultivators of later generations to search slowly.

In their words, this was called fate and affinity.

“Ah? Lu Yang, you’re awake?” A cheerful voice sounded behind Yun Zhi.

Yun Mengmeng stepped around her, holding a freshly woven flower garland, looking at Lu Yang in delight. “I never imagined you to be the Little Junior Brother Little Zhi often talks about. Both of us are truly fated! If I had known you were from the Dao-Seeking Sect, I would have asked you how to get there when we had hotpot.”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, I also didn’t know that your single-minded “good sister” was Big Senior Sister. If I had known you knew her, I would have eaten hotpot elsewhere.

Yun Mengmeng gently placed the flower garland on his head. “This is a blessing from where we’re from, wishing you safety and peace.”

Lu Yang felt somewhat touched. Although Yun Mengmeng had sabotaged me, that wasn’t on purpose, and her nature is kind.

Then Yun Mengmeng sighed with emotion. “You really can sleep. No wonder you’re Little Zhi’s junior brother. You’re exactly like her. Once you’re asleep, there’s no waking you up.

“I even suggested that Little Zhi take you as her shifu, but she was coy and hesitant. As the saying goes, ‘an accomplished person can become a teacher.’ Though Little Zhi is older than you, her swordsmanship indeed can’t compare to yours. She’s just too proud. If you ask me, that’s no big deal. When we played house as kids, she often called me mom...”

Lu Yang broke out in a cold sweat. He dared not listen further.

Yun Zhi rose silently, placed a hand on Yun Mengmeng’s shoulder, and smiled at her.

“Mengmeng, we sisters haven’t seen each other in ages. I didn’t expect you to have broken through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Come, let’s find somewhere to spar.”

Chapter 921: A New Addition to the Everlasting Lineage

After Yun Mengmeng and Yun Zhi finished catching up, the former had visibly become obedient, though she still mumbled under her breath, “It’s still that issue—Little Zhi, you’re too concerned with saving face. You should learn from me...”

After returning from Sword Tower, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had relocated from the Qingfeng Sword’s small world back to Lu Yang's mental space.

“Yun Mengmeng pays respects to Senior Doudou.” Her bow was proper. Yun Mengmeng remembered the etiquette her Granny had taught her. The outside world is unlike secret domains; one must bow frequently before seniors.

She circled Yun Mengmeng twice. Setting aside how excessively well Lu Yang treats this girl, I’m quite satisfied with her. “I didn’t expect there’s still someone who could condense an Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit. Not bad, not bad at all, I have high hopes for you.”

Although many cultivators had condensed Incipient Dao Fruits like “Undying” and “Imperishable,” they fell short of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s standards. Someone like Yun Mengmeng is good.

Hearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy's praise for her, Yun Mengmeng’s heart blossomed with joy. I didn’t expect myself to be so outstanding.

“From now on, you’ll be the Third-in-Command of my Everlasting Lineage,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy announced excitedly, adding another member to their ranks.

“Ah, oh.” Yun Mengmeng didn’t know what the Everlasting Lineage was, but the name sounded impressive to her.

“By the way, would you like to join the Great Dou Dynasty that I founded? My Great Dou Dynasty spans vast territories—the East Sea, the Demon Region, and the Central Continent are all part of it.”

“I’ll join...I guess?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy prepared to confer an official post upon Yun Mengmeng. Turning to Lu Yang, she asked, “Xiao Yangzi, what official posts are vacant?”

Lu Yang set down the apple, tucked both hands into his sleeves, and gave a slight bow. “Your Exalted Majesty, in our Great Dou Dynasty, all official posts are vacant except for the Prime Minister.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy folded her arms and lowered her head in vexation. A soft mmhm escaped her lips as she said, “In that case, I shall appoint you as the Minister of Rites!”

Yun Mengmeng hesitated, unsure how to respond. Recalling descriptions of the imperial court in the strange tales she had read, she could only reply, “Many thanks for Your Majesty’s boundless grace.”

With that, the Everlasting Lineage and the Great Dou Dynasty gained another half-immortal.

Yun Zhi stood by silently, with only the corner of her eye twitching slightly.

“Your Exalted Majesty...”

Yun Mengmeng nodded eagerly, committing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s earnest teachings to heart.

An immortal’s words definitely contain profound meaning. If I analyze them word by word and line by line, I will surely gain something!

Yun Mengmeng couldn’t help but feel something was off. Wasn’t I the one who told Little Zhi to take Lu Yang as her shifu? How did I become the one taking a shifu?

And Lu Yang even became my senior brother?

Did I get tricked by Little Zhi?

Is this truly a promotion? It doesn’t feel like it.

Bu Yaolian. “...”

How come everyone in the Everlasting Lineage got in through connections?

Chapter 922: The Everlasting Lineage’s Mandatory Curriculum

As the Everlasting Creed’s faith and a product of faith power, Bu Yaolian was meticulous and calculating, able to regulate his expression. For instance, upon encountering joyous news such as being promoted to Fourth-in-Command, he showed hardly any trace of delight.

She is Yun Zhi’s good sister; it’s only fitting that her status is higher than mine.

As expected of the Second-in-Command, he’s well-off indeed. We could sell barbeque skewers our whole lives and still never be able to afford such a sword.

Lu Yang felt that he probably didn’t need the lesson. He stepped aside and took out the Chengying Sword, attempting to imprint his mark for it to acknowledge him as its master. Although the sword spirit Liu Ningxuan was gone, the sword’s spiritual nature remained. Making it recognize a master wouldn’t be easy.

After some rumination, Lu Yang inserted the Chengying Sword into the ground, then did the same for the Seven Stars Sword Set, surrounding the Chengying Sword. He hoped the Seven Stars Sword Set would persuade their fellow sword. freewebnovel.com

The eight swords hummed, seemingly engaged in intense communication. As Lu Yang shared a bond with the Seven Stars Sword Set, he could vaguely sense what they were saying.

“Big Brother Chengying, just follow Lu Yang. He has the Sword-Cleansing Pond. Trust your little brothers once, just soak there one time, and you’ll never forget how comfortable it was!”

“What’s so great about Liu Ningxuan? He occupied your body; can’t you forget him?”

“Liu Ningxuan is dead. Just forget him. As swords, we must look forward.”

“Just yield to Lu Yang."

Lu Yang couldn’t sense the Chengying Sword’s responses, but its diminishing vibrations suggested that the persuasion was working.

~~~

Meanwhile, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy took on the role of a respectable teacher and expounded the true Everlasting teachings.

“Self-detonation is our Everlasting Lineage’s most fundamental skill, a mandatory part of the curriculum.

“Back when I was researching how to maximize the self-detonation power, I could only imagine the misery I inflicted on my opponents. Fortunately, their sacrifices weren’t in vain; they helped continually refine my self-detonation theories.

“Third-in-Command, I observed that you were getting beaten throughout the battle, demonstrating scarcely any offensive moves. I presume you haven’t learned self-detonation.”

Yun Mengmeng nodded. Indeed, I hadn’t realized that self-detonation could also be an offensive method. All my moves came from the techniques passed down through the family.

“Fourth-in-Command, demonstrate for her,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy instructed.

Hearing this, Bu Yaolian felt that it was time to display his prowess as a senior.

He ran twenty li away and split himself into three ethereal souls and seven corporeal souls. With a bang, he self-detonated half his soul.

Yun Mengmeng observed the Fourth-in-Command’s self-detonation intently. That half a soul grew agitated, swelling like a balloon. In the blink of an eye, it burst, releasing terrifying soul power and engulfing the surrounding dozen li in its blast radius.

After the self-detonation, Bu Yaolian’s soul was quickly restored, becoming whole again.

“Amazing!” Yun Mengmeng’s eyes sparkled, as if a new world had opened before her. She felt that her previous combat style was too conservative.

What’s self-detonation? It’s what cultivators resort to in desperation, unleashing their most powerful attack at the cost of their lives. Yet our Everlasting Lineage can use it repeatedly. Its power speaks for itself.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pointed at Bu Yaolian, who returned with a silly, smug grin. “See? Standing in place dumbly after self-detonation is a classic mistake.

“Can you guarantee that your opponent was killed by the explosion and won’t attack you while you’re in the vulnerable process of restoring your soul?”

“Then what should one do?”

“You need to ride the blast wave at high speed, restoring your soul as you move. That way, when the explosion wave ends, and your soul is restored, you can seamlessly perform a second self-detonation, leaving no breathing room for your opponent!

“Also, don’t stand on the ground when self-detonating. You need to be in the air. That maximizes the destructive power.

“As for scattering the self-detonation and such, they’re not skills you can grasp now. You should first master what I’ve taught. Go somewhere far to practice and aim to be proficient in the basics as soon as possible.”

“Yes!”

Yun Mengmeng jubilantly went somewhere far to self-detonate. Afterward, there was a boom, and the blast waves swept toward them. At the edge of the explosion, Lu Yang clung desperately to the Chengying Sword planted in the ground.

He was blown until he was parallel to the earth.

When the waves dispersed, Lu Yang saw the blast site: forests reduced to charcoal, mountains turned into dust, and the pit flooded by rivers, soon forming a lake.

Yun Mengmeng’s self-detonation of her physical flesh directly affected reality.

“My small world!” Lu Yang cried in despair.

This serenely beautiful small world I’ve just obtained and visited only twice has turned to ruins in a flash.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had clearly forgotten a self-detonation’s impact on reality. She hurriedly comforted Lu Yang, seeking ways to salvage the situation. “Uh, minor issue. I’ll teach them both the Tree-Planting Mantra later.”

Chapter 923: The Unlucky Merchant Guild

Yun Mengmeng and Bu Yaolian, engrossed in their self-detonations, failed to hear Lu Yang’s despairing cry amidst the thunderous explosions, blasting away with great relish.

Bu Yaolian thought, Learning from Big Boss is indeed far more efficient than muddling through alone. With just a few words, she had dispelled the clouds and shown me the path ahead.

If I had received her guidance earlier, I wouldn’t have needed to resort to a war of attrition when fighting Great Yu’s Second Imperial Preceptor. I would have blasted him to smithereens.

Yun Mengmeng was playful by nature and found something as fun as self-detonation to be right up her alley. It was a perfect example of edutainment, and she devoted herself to learning with remarkable zeal.

BOOM! BOOM! BOOM!

As the two half-immortals gradually mastered the minor skill of self-detonation, the continuous explosions caused the small world to tremble.

Just like that, they blasted for five days.

During these five days, Lu Yang successfully used the Seven Stars Sword Set to weaken the Chengying Sword’s resistance, imprinting his mark upon it and becoming its master.

He had a wooden clone hold the Chengying Sword while he wielded the Qingfeng Sword. They sparred in impeccable synchrony, and he familiarized himself with the feel of it in his hand.

In contrast to the Third-in-Command and the Fourth-in-Command‘s self-detonations fifty li away, Lu Yang’s sword dance forms were quite elegant.

Compared to the Mingyue Sword, the Chengying Sword was lighter and sharper, and its lingering spiritual nature was obedient, allowing him to wield it with ease.

“Good sword, good sword.” Lu Yang grinned from ear to ear. As a sword cultivator, he loved swords, especially legendary peerless ones like this.

Like the Qingfeng Sword, the Chengying Sword had been sealed layer by layer by Yun Zhi to prevent Lu Yang’s overreliance on divine weapons. Now, it suited Lu Yang perfectly.

The Third-in-Command and the Fourth-in-Command also returned with success from their training. They dutifully planted trees, moved mountains, and filled seas, restoring the small world to its original state.

In the secret domain, Yun Mengmeng had been the playful and trouble-making type, often accidentally knocking down trees, so she had learned the Tree-Planting Mantra.

Possessing the memories of all Everlasting Creed members, Bu Yaolian also knew the Tree-Planting Mantra.

The two were so disciplined that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t need to teach them.

Cleaning up took half a day. A rough job would have been quick given their cultivation, but under the Second-in-Command’s oppressive gaze, they had to tidy up everything meticulously.

Only after seeing the small world fully restored did Lu Yang finally let them off.

“Let’s stop the training here for now. You’re still beginners and can’t self-detonate at will; there’s still a small gap between self-detonations. Experienced opponents might exploit this opening.

“However, constant self-detonations aren’t sustainable. Go rest outside and practice slowly when you have time.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy emphasized balance in cultivation. Daily self-detonation would blast them stupid.

“Yes.”

~~~

After leaving the small world, Bu Yaolian stayed at the barbeque shop, while Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng chose to walk away.

Since she lacked contribution points, Lu Yang had to accompany her to shop for snacks, just like in Shu Province.

Wait, while I was dragged around by the Old Ancestor for training all day long, this fellow got to spend the whole day with a beauty?

Meng Jingzhou was taken aback. Yun Mengmeng? Big Senior Sister, so you’ve been using your good friend’s name in public?

“Senior Brother, who is this?”

“Meng Jingzhou, my junior brother.”

Meng Jingzhou was taken aback. What did she call you? “Senior Brother?” What’s the relationship between the two of you? Is she even twenty years old? I’ve only been gone for a little over a year. Why does it feel like everything has changed beyond recognition? freewebnovel.com

The three found a spot at the Food Stall Federation and ordered a few signature dishes, with Meng Jingzhou treating.

“Don’t talk nonsense. I went to Sword Tower to participate in the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony. Its collapse was due to a battle between immortals. What does that have to do with me?” Lu Yang believed his conscience was clear.

Meng Jingzhou snorted, not buying it. The outside world had been spreading tales of a battle between two immortals at Sword Tower, and Lu Yang clinching first place at the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony. These two matters seem completely unrelated, but I can tell at a glance that they’re one hundred percent related to Lu Yang.

The merchant guild would have to be suicidal to look for Hui Doudou.

This battle at Sword Tower had exposed much information. By the time several versions reached Meng Jingzhou, they had been distorted. As I thought, the best way to understand what happened at Sword Tower is to ask the original culprit.

When Lu Yang asked how Meng Jingzhou was trained by Meng Junzi, his eyes showed terror, clearly unwilling to recall that miserable period.

After chatting for a while with Meng Jingzhou, Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng returned to Heaven’s Gate Peak.

~~~

After over a year of torture, Guan Shanhai finally succumbed and divulged crucial intelligence. He felt that if he didn’t disclose something valuable soon, Yun Zhi would directly search his soul.

Lu Yang’s eyes lit up. This is an amazing sight that one might not witness even in hundreds of millennia. I naturally can’t miss it.

Chapter 924: Entering Outer Space

Unlike the sun of the ancient era, which evolved from Jinwu golden crows, the sun after the ancient era was the embodiment of pure yang power, possessing boundless might. Countless cultivators relied on it for their cultivation; otherwise, the Radiant Sun Creed wouldn’t have come into existence.

In the Great Qian era, the sun was sealed by the founding Qian Emperor, the Midheaven Emperor-Lord, who claimed it as his.

In the Great Yu era, the founding Yu Emperor Wu Yao saw the seal left by the Midheaven Emperor-Lord and added another layer of seal atop it.

Hence, neither of them could obtain the sun.

With Wu Yao suspected of having gone to the outside world through replacement, Lu Yang had thought the second seal would never be undone. He didn’t expect Guan Shanhai to know the method.

“According to Guan Shanhai, the Midheaven Emperor-Lord sealed the sun, weakening the solar power and luna power it emitted, so that all citizens of Great Qian would worship him.

“At the time, any cultivator wishing to rely on the sun to cultivate had to worship him. After the worship, a sliver of the seal would open, channeling solar power and luna power to them before it was resealed again.

“Therefore, legend had it that the Midheaven Emperor-Lord possessed the power to command the sun and moon.”

During the Great Qian era, faith power was the primary cultivation method. Temples and divine statues were everywhere, and people would go to any lengths to seize faith power. With dynastic changes and shifts in cultivation methods, these temples and statues gradually vanished into the river of history, leaving little trace behind.

“After Wu Yao ascended the throne, he repeatedly tried reaching the sun, but was blocked by the Midheaven Emperor-Lord’s seal. Thus, he added his own seal, preventing the Midheaven Emperor-Lord from approaching the sun, too. This double layer of seals caused the sun’s emitted solar and luna powers to diminish significantly.”

This was a matter hidden in history, not recorded in any ancient text.

“Removing Wu Yao’s seal this time will release a part of the solar and luna powers, greatly benefiting cultivators reliant on them.”

En route to the sun, Yun Zhi explained the background of the matter to Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng.

“Is the sun in such great demand? So many people are fighting over it.” Yun Mengmeng was baffled. As there was no sun in the secret domain, she couldn’t really understand the importance of the sun.

With Lu Yang’s current cultivation, he could traverse outer space, but not as effortlessly as Yun Zhi. He had to allocate a large portion of his mental power to deal with the harsh conditions of outer space.

On the other hand, Yun Mengmeng didn’t fear outer space’s hostile environment, but her habit of glancing here and poking there severely slowed their flight.

Left with no choice, Yun Zhi encased them in transparent domes and carried them as she flew.

During their journey, Lu Yang beheld countless resplendent stars. Whenever they encountered one, Yun Zhi would unhesitatingly charge toward it. Lu Yang braced for an impact, only to discover that the star before them was merely an illusory projection.

However, some were not phantom images and required Yun Zhi to navigate around them.

“Eh, this star here is Lass Yun’s golden core?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy noticed something amiss. The star before her did exist, but it wasn’t preserved from the ancient era; it had been filled with Yun Zhi’s golden core.

“Little Zhi’s golden core is this big?” Yun Mengmeng was astonished. Why is my golden core so small?

“It just looks big. In terms of power, it cannot rival my Unbeatable Golden Core.”

“What is the Unbeatable Golden Core?” Yun Mengmeng asked. freewebnovel.com

“The Unbeatable Golden Core is a golden core that only those of the Everlasting Lineage can form. It ranks first in power among first-grade golden cores! What a pity, your cultivation is too high. You’ve missed the window to condense an Unbeatable Golden Core.”

“That’s so impressive!” Yun Mengmeng’s eyes sparkled. Our Everlasting Lineage is so strong.

Although Lu Yang had long found out that the countless stars overhead were actually Yun Zhi’s golden cores, knowing was one thing, and witnessing it firsthand was entirely another thing.

Only by witnessing them with his own eyes could he grasp the sheer terror of Yun Zhi’s golden cores. If one were to stand upon one, they would mistakenly believe the land beneath their feet was flat.

And this was merely a single golden core. Countless more of Yun Zhi’s golden cores were scattered throughout outer space.

Outer space was dark and frigid, a vast, empty expanse of terrifying silence. Adrift within it, Lu Yang was imperceptibly small. As formidable as cultivators were, compared to the universe itself, they couldn’t be any more minute and insignificant...

“This pitch-black place reminds me of something,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s emotional musings interrupted Lu Yang’s internal monologue. “Back then, the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the other three managed numerous stars, but the distances between them were terribly inconvenient for travel. Hence, they would often tinker with the positions of stars, moving them closer together or simply establishing spatial passages between the stars.”

After an indeterminate amount of time, Lu Yang spotted a colossal ball of fire. Extreme temperatures raged across outer space. Without the transparent dome Yun Zhi had placed around him, the sheer heat alone would have been sufficient to incinerate him.

Innumerable trailblazers of the Radiant Sun Creed had personally tested the sun’s power. Lu Yang could even discern human-shaped charcoal briquettes orbiting the sun.

Undeterred by the infernal heat, Yun Zhi attempted to draw closer, but just then, a golden chain encircling the sun barred their path.

Brilliant runes shimmered upon the golden chain, and they were so dazzling that they were blinding. They intensified the sun’s already terrifying temperature. These luminous runs seemed to encompass all the principles of the world. A single glance would flood the mind with such a torrent of knowledge that one’s mental space would burst asunder.

With Yun Zhi shielding him and blocking the overwhelming influx of knowledge, Lu Yang could observe the runes at his own pace.

“Big Boss, what do all these runes mean?” No matter how long Yun Mengmeng stared, she couldn’t make sense of any of them and had to turn to their all-knowing leader for help.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was indeed omniscient, effortlessly deciphering the talismanic runes’ meaning and analyzing them for the Second-in-Command and the Third-in-Command.

“Although there’s no explicit subject, judging by the semantics, it appears to be Wu Yao cursing the Midheaven Emperor-Lord. Do you need me to recite the exact invectives...” Toward the end, she hesitated, a rare occurrence. Her cheeks flushed, clearly too embarrassed to voice such profanities.

“No need, no need at all,” Lu Yang replied hastily.

“Speaking of which,” she said, “this sun is truly a creation of the Nine-Layers Immortal. All the Jinwu golden crows of the ancient era combined could never have forged a sun containing such power. Furthermore, it also contains an equal measure of luna power.”

Ao Ling had mentioned that both the sun and moon of the Ember Legacy Dynasty were created by the Nine-Layers Immortal using his Yin-Yang Dao Fruit. To save trouble, he had constructed the sun and moon as a single integrated entity.

However, he also considered that this design would render sundials nearly useless, making it difficult for common folk to perceive the passage of time and impacting daily life. Therefore, he painted a dial and hands onto the sun itself, allowing everyone to tell the time at a glance.

Since the time was verified by the Epoch Immortal himself, its accuracy was guaranteed.

Chapter 925: Removing the First Seal on the Sun

Telling time by looking at the sun had been a privilege reserved solely for the people of the Ember Legacy Dynasty. It was meticulous work that demanded regular upkeep. With the fall of the Ember Legacy Dynasty, the timekeeping function of the sun vanished as well.

Whenever Yun Zhi approached the sun in the past, she had always been stopped by the Immortal Dao chain that Wu Yao had left behind. This time, things would be different.

Flipping her palm upward, Dao charm surged forth and stirred spatial ripples as if the space had come alive. Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng heard what seemed like the sound of the Great Dao drifting from the horizon’s edge—ethereal and crystalline, its meaning unclear.

An unseen force coalesced in Yun Zhi’s palm, gradually taking the shape of a key with a long handle.

Sensing the presence of the Immortal Dao chain, the key flew forth of its own accord, going close and resonating with it.

The Immortal Dao chain shook, and Wu Yao’s voice rang out, so vigorous and full-throated that not even the vacuum of the universe could stifle it. “You f*cking *********”

A torrent of profanities followed, unbearably coarse to the ear. They were so vile that if Wu Yao had dared show himself before Yun Zhi in that moment, she would have felt compelled to punch him in the face immediately.

Had she known that breaking the seal would result in such an “unusual phenomenon,” she would never have brought Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng along.

Yun Mengmeng thought, The people in the outside world are truly something else—even their invectives never repeat themselves, unlike me. When I’m pushed to the brink, I can only curse, “You’re a bad peach.”

Having a feeling that the tirade wouldn’t be ending anytime soon, Yun Zhi had no choice but to encase Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng in another layer, ensuring that the three leaders of the Everlasting Lineage could no longer hear the curses.

After the stream of invectives finally ceased, the Immortal Dao chain gradually dimmed, then disappeared without a trace.

The solar power that had been sealed for two hundred thousand years burst forth. Waves of energy billowed, flames soared to the sky, and Solar True Fire leaped and danced with such intensity that even a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator would be reduced to ashes in the face of such power.

Those pioneers of the Radiant Sun Creed orbited the sun and weathered fiery trials, but ultimately failed to survive the final test. The unleashed solar power incinerated them until not even a speck of them remained.

As the solar power spread outward, numerous cultivators sensed the overwhelming impact.

However, those who felt it most keenly were cultivators specializing in cultivating solar power. They could clearly perceive the increase in the sun’s emitted power, now incredibly dense. Their cultivation methods could even begin circulating autonomously, greedily absorbing this energy, expanding their meridians, and flooding their bodies.

Some cultivators even seized this opportunity to break through their bottlenecks, achieving significant improvements in their cultivation realms.

Meng Jingzhou trembled, as if he was about to lose control of himself. Only after dousing himself with barrel after barrel of ice water transported from the depths of the Extreme North could he temporarily suppress the burgeoning desires within him.

“What the hell is going on?!” Meng Jingzhou could sense his Single’s Spirit Root ravenously absorbing the solar power, intensifying the desires in his heart.

“Brother, stop absorbing! If you keep this up, I really won’t be able to hold on!” Meng Jingzhou wanted to cry, but had no tears. Why didn’t I encounter such an uncanny event while at home, only to face it as soon as I returned to the sect?

The sun had suddenly erupted with solar power, bathing his Single’s Spirit Root in its power. Across all generations of individuals with the Single’s Spirit Root, none had ever experienced something like this. Why did it have to happen to me?

Admittedly, the strengthening of my spirit root enhances me in every aspect—my Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivation realm has grown more solid, my spirit energy reserves in my dantian have expanded, and my meridians, qi and blood, mental power, and primordial soul...have all undergone transformation.

“But I don’t need this!”

Meng Jingzhou hastily sat in meditation, silently reciting Buddhist heart mantras to view females as mere skeletons with rouge. He began to acquire the bearing of an enlightened senior monk.

~~~

Wu Yao’s seal only affected the solar power, not the sun’s temperature. Even if the seal was broken, it wouldn’t make summers hotter or melt the glaciers in the Extreme North.

“Senior Immortal Fairy, can you sense the Nine-Layers Immortal here?” Yun Zhi asked, wondering if the Nine-Layers Immortal was hiding within the sun.

“Nine-Layers, are you there?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shouted at the sun.

There was no response except for the swaying of the chain left by the Midheaven Emperor-Lord.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned, realizing the chain blocked sound.

“In that case, let’s wait until we find the Midheaven Emperor-Lord and have him undo the first seal.” Yun Zhi had anticipated such a situation and had simply thought it wouldn’t hurt to try.

“By the way, Big Senior Sister, if only the Midheaven Emperor-Lord’s seal is left, does that mean that cultivators can obtain all the solar power by praying to him?”

Yun Zhi shook her head. “That won’t work. It may be that sufficient faith power has been collected, or perhaps for other reasons, the Midheaven Emperor-Lord no longer absorbs faith power, removing this method of acquiring solar power through praying.

“The current chain merely seals the sun.”

Yun Mengmeng remained silent throughout. The topics that Big Boss, Second-in-Command, and Little Zhi are discussing are too profound. I can’t understand anything.

As I thought, there’s a reason I’m only Third-in-Command—my knowledge is terribly lacking.

Yun Mengmeng seemed to have found a goal to work toward and asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy excitedly, “Big Boss, if I study hard, will I have a chance to become Second-in-Command?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shot her a sidelong glance. “If you continue harboring such rebellious thoughts, you’ll be Fourth-in-Command.”

“Oh.”

~~~

After dropping Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng at Heaven’s Gate Peak, Yun Zhi headed to the imperial city alone to look for the Xia Emperor, without informing anyone.

“Did you say that you want to find some death-row prisoners for experiments?” The Xia Emperor stared at Yun Zhi in shock. This is the first time Yun Zhi has requested something like this from me.

“Just find one first to verify a hypothesis.”

With a wave, the Xia Emperor issued a decree to the Ministry of Justice to select a death-row inmate for Yun Zhi, instructing them to supply her with as many as she wished in the future.

Yun Zhi sealed the death-row prisoner’s cultivation and speech, then left the imperial city, bringing him to a thatched hut on a nearby hill.

Setting him down, she kindly filled him in on historical knowledge. “Do you know the Ember Legacy Dynasty?”

After a quarter of an hour, the person she was waiting for didn’t come. Yun Zhi had no choice but to leave the bewildered prisoner behind and depart.

Concealing her aura, she waited on the hillside, at its foot, and even from a distance, yet the person still didn’t appear.

Returning to the thatched hut after an hour, she found a large hole in the hut. Directly beneath the hole, the death-row prisoner had been annihilated, with death permeating the air.

Yun Zhi fetched another death-row inmate from the Ministry of Justice and repeated the method, leaving him in the thatched hut and filling him in on historical knowledge.

Despite waiting in the thatched hut for two hours, the person she was waiting for still didn’t show up. Yun Zhi had no choice but to depart.

By the time she returned to the thatched hut, she found another hole, and the second death-row prisoner was also dead.

“It’s useless even if I conceal my aura—she can still sense that I’m nearby?” Yun Zhi mumbled, fetching a third death-row prisoner from the Ministry of Justice.

To test her conjecture, she repeated the method. After filling the prisoner in on historical knowledge, she hid in the shadows.

Still no movement.

When she left the hill and returned, she found that the hilltop was leveled; the thatched hut and the death-row prisoner had vanished. All that remained was a slip of paper.

Do you never stop?!

Chapter 926: Luck

Yun Zhi held the note left by Hui Doudou, lost in thought.

“The Gray Immortal Fairy eliminates those in the know with such frequency, yet she has never once made a move against Senior Ao Ling or Little Junior Brother.

“Senior Ao Ling’s case can be easily explained. When the Gray Immortal Fairy attempted to kill Senior Ao Ling in the Ember Legacy Dynasty, the Dragon-Pattern Bracelet blocked numerous attacks. Now that the bracelet is fully charged and capable of traversing space, the Gray Immortal Fairy knows that ambushing or trapping Senior Ao Ling would be extremely difficult.

“But why hasn’t she made a move on Little Junior Brother?

“Could it be that she knows she’ll be the unlucky one if she lays a hand on him?”

Yun Zhi pondered for a while, then dismissed this theory. Had the Gray Immortal Fairy known that Little Junior Brother was so dangerous, she wouldn’t have struck at Sword Tower.

“Is it because she inherited Senior Immortal Fairy’s luck, instinctively steering clear of the most disastrous choice?

“If the Gray Immortal Fairy had decided to eliminate Little Junior Brother at Sword Tower first and deal with the Heaven Mandate corpse afterward, she would have become the unlucky one.

“That’s right. She was once Senior Immortal Fairy after all. It’s only natural that she possesses Senior Immortal Fairy’s luck.”

To test her conjecture, Yun Zhi carved out a hidden small world beside the fourth death-row inmate and concealed herself within it.

Technically, Hui Doudou shouldn’t be able to sense Yun Zhi. Yet, while Yun Zhi was hiding in the small world, Hui Doudou didn’t take action. Only after Yun Zhi departed and went far away did Hui Doudou finally kill the death-row inmate.

“As I thought, it’s a matter of luck.

“It seems that if we want to deal with the Gray Immortal Fairy, we’ll have to rely on luck stronger than hers.”

Yun Zhi ceased tormenting Hui Doudou and left the hill.

~~~

The world only knew that solar power had increased, with few understanding the reason behind it.

The Radiant Sun Creed, however, belonged to that “few.”

“The sharp increase in solar power must be due to the removal of one of the seals!” The Radiant Sun Creed’s higher-ups were ecstatic.

What does this signify? It signifies that our recent foray into the solar energy industry has earned the sun’s recognition through the unseen workings of destiny!

Granted, some exalted personage has removed one of the sun’s seals. But then again, why now of all times, precisely when the solar energy industry is booming?

There are no coincidences in this world; everything happens through the unseen workings of destiny.

“This is a divine revelation! The sun is telling us to redouble our efforts in developing the solar energy industry!”

Although their on-site inspection of the imperial city hadn’t been smooth sailing and nearly put their lives in danger, under Mu Baiyi’s persuasion, the two creeds reached a consensus, agreeing to use the imperial city as a starting point for producing solar energy technologies.

By now, they had manufactured products like solar-powered lamps and water heaters, which had garnered widespread approval.

“Come to think of it, the smooth promotion of solar lamps was thanks to someone inexplicably buying up a huge stockpile of candles. That caused a shortage in the market, and many civilians decided they might as well give our solar products a try,” a Radiant Sun Creed higher-up remarked with emotion, feeling that they had chosen the right strategy.

In the past, they were obsessed with reaching the sun, a goal fraught with difficulties, and that caused countless people to be burned to death. Now that they had pivoted to developing the solar energy industry, everything had taken a turn for the better.

“Furthermore, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed has been invested in our collaboration, constantly devising ways to promote our products,” Creed Leader Chi added. He found Mu Baiyi and Shi Huagu particularly admirable. They work day and night researching market strategies and act swiftly, such as when they advertised through channels like the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage.

Sincere cooperation between two major diabolic creeds was something previously unimaginable.

Could the removal of the sun’s seal be the work of the ancient Heavenly Court? This thought suddenly struck Creed Leader Chi. Although he had no proof, the feeling had arisen within him unbidden.

Creed Leader Chi often counted himself fortunate for having allied with the ancient Heavenly Court early. With their aid, his influence within the Radiant Sun Creed grew with each passing day.

Now that the sun’s first seal was undone, the strength of all Radiant Sun Creed followers had increased significantly. He even felt that he could attempt to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation and become a true powerhouse, no longer having to fear for his life.

~~~

“You are from the same hometown as Big Senior Sister?” Gan Tian circled Yun Mengmeng with keen interest. Though her eyes were covered with a black cloth, she appeared to be scrutinizing Yun Mengmeng.

She had been away seeking inspiration for a musical composition and had just returned today, only to discover a newcomer on Heaven’s Gate Peak. To her surprise, this person came from the same hometown as Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi rarely spoke of her hometown. Gan Tian only knew that Yun Zhi had been born in a secret domain and was brought out by their shifu. Beyond that, she knew nothing.

“Quick, tell me! Where is Big Senior Sister’s hometown? What is it like?” When it came to matters concerning Yun Zhi, Gan Tian was completely unlike her usual serene self while playing the qin.

Lu Yang merely observed from the side. He was also quite curious about matters concerning Yun Zhi.

Oh, except for any embarrassing anecdotes.

Yun Mengmeng shook her head vigorously, clamping shut her mouth that had been itching to speak. Little Zhi has warned me not to speak of matters regarding the secret domain, especially not to Big Boss and Second-in-Command.

“Sister Mengmeng, do tell,” Lu Yang inquired, adopting a gentle, coaxing tone, which left Yun Mengmeng rather tempted.

Fortunately, her willpower proved steadfast. She refused to speak, leaving both Lu Yang and Gan Tian discouraged.

“Little Lu, I heard something happened at Sword Tower. Are you alright?” Suddenly, a solicitous voice that hadn’t been heard for a long time sounded, causing both Lu Yang and Gan Tian to freeze.

Shifu is back!

It has been two years since we last saw him, hasn't it?

Previously, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had been far away in the Demon Region. When he heard about the events at Sword Tower, where Lu Yang had stalled the Heaven Mandate Immortal until the battle between the two immortals, then fallen into a coma, he immediately hurried back.

He was now a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, his cultivation level far exceeding what it once was. Many who tried to track him down failed, and his journey back was largely without hindrance.

Chieftain Jin was no longer by the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s side. With the proliferation of solar lamps, the candles hoarded by the Qiongqi Tribe had become worthless, forcing them to sell at a severe loss.

To recoup their losses, Chieftain Jin had no choice but to temporarily abandon his studies under the Taciturn Daoist Priest and rush back to the Qiongqi Tribe to come up with a solution.

Halfway up Heaven’s Gate Peak, even before the Taciturn Daoist Priest saw Lu Yang, he could already sense his disciple’s vibrant presence at the summit. He breathed a sigh of relief. “Little Lu, it’s great that you’re fine.”

Upon reaching the summit, before the Taciturn Daoist Priest could utter another word, a fierce attack came hurtling toward him, forcing him to dodge immediately.

“So you’re the one who took Little Zhi away back then, and you still dare show your face!” Yun Mengmeng was incensed at the sight of the Taciturn Daoist Priest, letting out a growl and lunging at him.

If he hadn’t appeared and regaled Little Zhi with tales of how wonderful the outside world was, Little Zhi wouldn’t have left the secret domain, and we wouldn’t have been separated for centuries.

Bad peach!

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was flummoxed. How could I get ambushed even when I’ve already returned to my territory?

Who is so audacious as to ambush me at Heaven’s Gate Peak?

Chapter 927: The Dao-Seeking Sect Gains Another Transcendent Tribulation Cultivator

Throughout history, none who had left the Peach Blossom Secret Domain had ever returned. Back when Yun Mengmeng parted ways with Yun Zhi, she had wept with such heartbreaking sorrow, convinced it was a farewell for eternity.

And the culprit who had caused Little Zhi to leave the Peach Blossom Secret Domain was this fellow called Ye Wanli!

The Taciturn Daoist Priest had met Yun Mengmeng only once, and that was when she was less than ten years old. Since he hadn’t accompanied Yun Zhi when she returned to the secret domain to visit her family, he failed to recognize Yun Mengmeng’s identity at first glance.

It was only when he carefully replayed her words upon their meeting that realization finally dawned on him. “You’re that little lass who cried her eyes out back then!”

“How dare you bring that up?!” Yun Mengmeng’s eyes widened with fury. Without another word, she self-detonated, catching the Taciturn Daoist Priest off guard.

Even the most battle-hardened cultivator would be hard-pressed to instantly register that their opponent had launched a self-detonation attack.

The continuous self-detonation technique that Yun Mengmeng had just learned from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was now being employed against the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Above Heaven’s Gate Peak, explosions thundered endlessly, and the Taciturn Daoist Priest was tossed about by the shockwaves like a tattered kite in a gale.

Lu Yang felt a twinge of relief—relief that Yun Mengmeng had just learned how to use the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Had she not mastered it, she might not have ambushed Shifu so easily.

“It is in Shifu’s destiny to face this tribulation,” Lu Yang remarked with the unruffled air of a blind fortune-teller, conjuring excuses for not rushing to his master’s aid.

Gan Tian agreed with his assessment. “Since Shifu is at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, it’s reasonable that he should undergo a few human tribulations.”

Her trip in search of musical inspiration had borne fruit; she had brought back a local specialty—a white melon. It had few seeds and was exceptionally crisp and sweet, bursting with juices. Using a single qin string, she sliced the white melon into eight pieces and handed one to Lu Yang. The two of them munched away with great relish.

The commotion at Heaven’s Gate Peak had also drawn a crowd of onlooking disciples in the sect. They pointed at the Taciturn Daoist Priest and whispered about him as he was repeatedly blasted. All of them were immensely curious about who the attacker was.

“Impressive! Our Dao-Seeking Sect has an expert like this?”

The Dao-Seeking Sect disciples buzzed with speculation, all eager to learn the identity of this expert. Even the Grand-Shifu from Incarceration Peak or Old Tao from the scripture library couldn’t have achieved such a dramatic effect.

Just then, Yun Zhi hurried back. Taking in the sight of Yun Mengmeng’s frenzied self-detonations and the Taciturn Daoist Priest flickering like a guttering candle in the wind, the corner of her eye twitched.

“Alright, alright, Mengmeng, stop now. That’s enough.”

Yun Zhi interposed herself between the two, cutting short Yun Mengmeng’s relentless chain of self-detonations. As for the Taciturn Daoist Priest, he could finally cease maintaining his sword-qi protective state.

Seeing that Yun Zhi had arrived, Yun Mengmeng huffily stopped attacking. The Taciturn Daoist Priest exhaled a sigh of relief. He really didn’t know he should handle Yun Mengmeng.

If I strike back, she indeed holds the high ground, and the conflict between us isn’t a trivial one.

But if I don’t strike back, my old bones won’t be able to withstand such continuous bombardment.

Suddenly, a peal of thunder boomed, causing the Taciturn Daoist Priest to instinctively think that Yun Mengmeng was about to self-detonate again.

Then, he realized the thunder came from the distance, and it sounded familiar.

“Tribulation thunder. Who is about to become a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest looked in the direction of the thunder, his eyes narrowing slightly.

If my guess is correct, that place is the canyon, where Big Brother is in seclusion.

“First Elder is about to undergo his tribulation!” Lu Yang also realized.

He had visited First Elder’s seclusion site before, and it was filled with coffins. After being in seclusion for over a year, First Elder could finally reap the fruits of his labor.

Drawn by First Elder’s commotion, the members of the Dao-Seeking Sect hastened toward the canyon to observe the tribulation process. freewebnovel.com

Lu Yang and the others also rushed over.

~~~

At the moment, the sky above the canyon was as black as ink, and the oppressive aura of thunder and lightning resembled an abyss, deep and unfathomable.

Although the lightning tribulation First Elder faced wasn’t as intense as what the Taciturn Daoist Priest had endured, it was close, worthy of his title as a Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

Below in the canyon, coffins trembled. The immortal peach placed before one coffin had been reduced to nothing but its pit. Suddenly, a pale hand reached out from the coffin and gripped its lid, the veins on the back of the hand bulging.

With a thunderous blast, the coffin exploded. First Elder soared into the air, rising above the canyon to confront the lightning tribulation directly, his face devoid of fear. His head drooped, and he was snoring.

“First Elder seems to be sleeping. Is he alright?” Lu Yang asked with concern.

“It’s fine. Big Brother cultivates the Dao of Dream. His strongest state is when he’s asleep. Enemies in reality will manifest in his dreams in a different form. As he battles them in his dreams, his physical body in reality will move accordingly,” the Taciturn Daoist Priest explained, memories of being disciplined by a sleepwalking First Elder in his childhood still vivid.

First Elder undergoing tribulation was a momentous event. Second Elder, Third Elder...and even Sixth Elder had all arrived. The Grand-Shifu and Old Tao had also come.

Boom!

No one had anticipated that the first lightning tribulation would emerge from beneath the canyon. The lightning tribulation in the sky was merely a decoy!

A sudden lightning bolt surged from the ground, hurtling straight toward First Elder’s face. With eyes tightly shut, First Elder delivered a knifehand strike, intending to clash head-on with the lightning tribulation.

Countless lightning bolts rose from below like tentacles, binding First Elder. With a mighty roar, his muscles bulged, and an arhat dharma body wielding a vajra scepter appeared, breaking free from the lightning tribulation’s restraints.

As Lu Yang watched, his heart shuddered with fear. He could see clearly that First Elder was battered until his skin split, his wounds so deep that the bone was visible. Yet First Elder seemed insensate, solely focused on counterattacking the lightning tribulation, utterly disregarding his own injuries.

“That’s how he is when asleep. He only attacks and doesn’t defend, and he feels no pain,” the Taciturn Daoist Priest explained again.

First Elder seemed to have dreamed of something; his face twisted into a ferocious expression, like an arhat in a mural subduing demons.

“I’m telling you, I am the strongest jiangshi! I’ve already cultivated to the Hanba Realm! How could a bunch of unfossilized bones like you be stronger than me?” First Elder suddenly bellowed.

“I’m telling you, this graveyard is my territory! No one else can seize it!”

“Not convinced? Then let our fists do the talking!”

Lu Yang. “...”

First Elder, what on earth are you dreaming about?

When First Elder repelled the ninety-ninth lightning tribulation, the lightning above and below the canyon simultaneously dissipated. Sunlight shone upon First Elder, who hovered in the air. He was covered in wounds, yet resembled a war god. Slowly opening his eyes, his expression was stern and rigid, as if he was still savoring the feeling of becoming a hanba drought demon.

“Hiss, ow, ow, ow!” The pain yanked First Elder back to reality. The power left within him by the lightning tribulation continuously repaired his body. Only then did he realize he had just undergone a tribulation and that he was now a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was the first to step forward and offer his congratulations. “Big Brother, you’ve finally become a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. Congratulations.”

Grandpa Ba and the others also flew up to offer their well-wishes.

The whole of Dao-Seeking Sect was awash in jubilation; gaining another Transcendent Tribulation cultivator was cause for celebration.

“Senior Brother, how did Little Qin develop his habit of liking jiangshi and graves?” Old Tao looked at the Grand-Shifu with a peculiar expression, suspecting this matter was related to him.

The Grand-Shifu coughed dryly, too embarrassed to admit that he used to constantly scare First Elder with jiangshi stories, only to find that they had backfired. Instead of being frightened, First Elder had developed an interest in them.

Chapter 928: The Flaw of Ten Thousand Swords Return to One

First Elder’s popularity was clearly several notches above that of the Taciturn Daoist Priest. When First Elder advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, the entire Dao-Seeking Sect erupted in jubilant celebration.

Only after three days did that scene of collective revelry gradually subside.

“So this is the legendary Chengying Sword.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest stroked the sword with unbridled affection. My good disciple truly has skills. Back when I visited the sword vault, I had sought the Chengying Sword’s approval, only to fail and settle for a spirit sword of a lesser grade.

And there is Lu Yang’s Qingfeng Sword, which possesses its own small world. I’m envious.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s spirit sword was no ordinary item either. It was a growth-type spirit treasure, capable of elevating its grade as his cultivation advanced, growing alongside him. With sufficient investment of materials, it might even one day ascend to the immortal grade.

“I heard that Liu Ningxuan’s personal sword reached the level of an immortal sword before he became a half-immortal. That’s truly remarkable.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest expressed a trace of regret. I heard that Liu Ningxuan had just died within Sword Tower. I won’t ever have the chance to cross swords with this Sword Dao legend.

Then again, now that the Sword Tower Supreme Lord has been resurrected, I can try sparring with her instead.

But definitely not now. My cultivation and the quality of my personal sword are still insufficient. I need to grow stronger first.

“I heard you executed Ten Thousand Swords Return to One at the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony?” the Taciturn Daoist Priest asked.

“Mmhm.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest looked at Lu Yang with satisfaction, never expecting his disciple to master this technique before he could even teach it.

“Come, demonstrate it for me.”

Lu Yang spread his Sword Dao incipient field. Countless Qingfeng Swords materialized from the ground and the sky, their presence as stern and imposing as hell.

He raised the true Qingfeng Sword. The swords embedded in the ground and sky burst free from their seals, merging with the true Qingfeng Sword, causing its sword momentum to swell by more than three chi.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s eyes lit up. “Sword Dao incipient field and Ten Thousand Swords Return to One? Come, use one sword strike on me.” He was eager to have a taste of its power.

Without hesitation, Lu Yang let out a shout. A great sword-qi dragon roared forth, then abruptly transformed into the real Qingfeng Sword, slashing toward the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest unhurriedly extended two fingers and gently pinched the Qingfeng Sword’s blade. The ferocious sword suddenly fell silent, unable to press downward a fraction further.

“It indeed is Ten Thousand Swords Return to One. It seems you learned it by watching me perform it back then, though the version I executed was a clever expedient.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest recalled having displayed this technique only once before Lu Yang, during his battle against the Heartless Creed.

To comprehend seventy to eighty percent after seeing it once, he’s truly an extraordinary genius of Sword Dao.

“A clever expedient?”

“Sit. I will explain it to you slowly.”

At the summit of Heaven’s Gate Peak, only Lu Yang and the Taciturn Daoist Priest remained.

Yun Mengmeng and Gan Tian had no interest in Sword Dao. Gan Tian had found a scenic spot by a stream to play her qin, while Yun Mengmeng brought snacks purchased from the dining hall in a cloth bundle and lay sprawled atop a large boulder in the river, nibbling on treats as she listened to Gan Tian’s music.

The dining hall’s snacks and pastries could double as weapons, but Yun Mengmeng was no pushover herself. Her teeth at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage possessed terrifying power, making short work of those snacks as easily as ordinary confections.

As for Yun Zhi, she claimed to have no interest in Sword Dao and had also gone to the riverside to listen to the qin.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest said, “I heard that during your match with Mingtai, the battle ultimately devolved into a contest of sword qi.

“This reflects a particular issue. Each time you or Mingtai unleashed sword qi, it represented your limits, but those were the limits of condensing sword qi into form, not your true limits. Had it been your genuine limits, your strength should have been depleted after unleashing sword qi once.

“Your version of Ten Thousand Swords Return to One was reverting the Qingfeng Swords formed from sword qi back into pure sword qi and reabsorbing them. This effectively elevated the limits of your sword qi.”

Lu Yang understood what the Taciturn Daoist Priest was getting at. In other words, my version of Ten Thousand Swords Return to One enhanced my explosive power.

Then the Taciturn Daoist Priest shifted his tone. “However, this is not the original intent of Ten Thousand Swords Return to One. Its purpose is to concentrate the power of myriad swords into a single blade, thereby unleashing explosive power that transcends all limits.”

Lu Yang recalled the battle between the Sword Tower Supreme Lord and the Heaven Mandate corpse. All the spirit swords from the sword vault had fused into the Hanguang Sword. It was precisely the scenario Shifu described.

“Come, let your shifu teach you how to comprehend the original intent of Ten Thousand Swords Return to One.

“First of all, the technique requires you to resonate with other swords. The version you previously executed omitted this step, which is why I said that this is a clever expedient.

“After that, with the Qingfeng Sword as your main anchor, you must let the resonance of the other swords gradually harmonize with it...

“It’s best to generate the resonance when the Qingfeng Sword’s momentum reaches its peak..."

“...”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s explanation was straightforward. If it were someone else, such as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, one would have been left utterly befuddled. For Lu Yang, however, it would be easy to understand.

Lu Yang’s eyes gleamed as he mentally rehearsed the process again and again, ruminating on the original intent of Ten Thousand Swords Return to One.

“Let me try.”

Lu Yang produced the Chengying Sword and the Seven-Star Sword Set in succession, drawing looks of undisguised envy from the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

He planted his feet firmly on the ground. Ripples spread across the grassland beneath him, as if sword qi had brushed past. The Chengying Sword and the Seven-Star Sword Set vibrated incessantly until their frequencies aligned perfectly with the Qingfeng Sword’s, whereupon they flew into it, merging as one.

“Ha!” Lu Yang slashed at the Taciturn Daoist Priest with his sword once more. Sword qi cascaded for a thousand li like a waterfall.

A streak of silver flashed, and once again, it was pinched by the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s two fingers.

“Excellent!” the Taciturn Daoist Priest laughed heartily. He hadn’t expected Lu Yang to comprehend the true meaning of Ten Thousand Swords to One with just a few pointers.

With a flick of his wrist, he sent Lu Yang and the Qingfeng Sword flying while hiding his right hand behind his back, rubbing his index and middle fingers together surreptitiously.

The power of this sword strike had exceeded his expectations.

Lu Yang somersaulted twice before landing steadily, the Chengying Sword and the Seven-Star Sword Set tumbling out beside him.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest strode forward, his face wreathed in smiles. “Well done! With diligent practice, you’ll definitely be able to execute Ten Thousand Swords Return to One... Little Lu?”

He noticed Lu Yang standing transfixed, staring at the eight swords on the ground and lost in thought.

After a while, Lu Yang snapped out of it and asked, “Shifu, isn’t executing Ten Thousand Swords Return to One a bit too ostentatious?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest nodded. The technique was indeed grand and spectacular, particularly the moment when myriad swords resonated and trembled, converging in sequence. It could be considered ostentatious, which explained why it was well-liked among sword cultivators.

Then Lu Yang continued to ask. “But if the technique is so ostentatious, doesn’t that mean the opponent will know that you’re about to use it, giving them time to react?”

“This is indeed a flaw of the technique.” It could allow opponents to dodge or charge up power.

An idea gradually took shape in Lu Yang’s mind. “What if I hide the Chengying Sword and the Seven-Star Sword Set within the Qingfeng Sword’s small world? When I perform Ten Thousand Swords Return to One, the nine swords will merge inside, with no signs on the outside. Wouldn’t the opponent be clueless that I have executed the technique? They would have no chance to guard against it in advance.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest simply patted Lu Yang on the shoulder.

“Remember, tell everyone you figured out this technique yourself. It has nothing to do with your shifu.”

Chapter 929: A Little Trick With the Sword

Hearing Lu Yang's proposed method, the Taciturn Daoist Priest was suddenly struck with the feeling that his disciple had already graduated and that he no longer needed to impart his shameless trump cards to Lu Yang.

He felt that Lu Yang was perfectly capable of comprehending a set of shameless techniques that would suit him better.

The disciple has surpassed the teacher indeed.

With this Ten Thousand Swords Return to One, even if Lu Yang weren't my disciple, any outsider would assume he is.

Lu Yang found his improved method truly effective. Not only did it resolve the issue of the technique being too conspicuous, but it also solved the problem of being unable to use the Seven-Star Sword Set publicly, testament to how wonderful a method it was.

After all, as far as outsiders were concerned, the Seven-Star Sword Set belonged to Young Creed Leader Lu and had nothing to do with Lu Yang. Having never had the chance to wield the Seven-Star Sword Set properly, Lu Yang had always felt somewhat apologetic toward the swords.

This is an amazing method that kills many birds with one stone.

Soon, Lu Yang hid the Chengying Sword and the Seven-Star Sword Set in the Qingfeng Sword's small world before performing Ten Thousand Swords Return to One once more.

As expected, no trace of the technique was visible on the outside. Even the Taciturn Daoist Priest would have to give him a thumbs-up and pronounce it underhanded.

Complimented by his shifu, Lu Yang didn't grow haughty and complacent. Instead, he settled his mind and concentrated on mastering the technique.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest watched by the side and nodded repeatedly. My youngest disciple’s temperament is far better than mine when I was young.

Back in my youth, if I had conceived of any underhanded trick, I would have rushed to sabotage someone immediately. How could I have continued cultivating?

Seven days passed. Lu Yang could finally perform Ten Thousand Swords Return to One proficiently. With a slash, even the Taciturn Daoist Priest couldn't distinguish whether this attack was part of the technique or an ordinary sword strike, let alone anyone else.

During those seven days, Yun Zhi, Yun Mengmeng, and Gan Tian came and went. Yun Mengmeng even crouched nearby for a while to watch Lu Yang cultivate, though she found it dull and returned to listening to tunes.

With food, drinks, and melodies to enjoy, she had a comfortable time, far more than life in the secret domain.

“If I had known, I would have left the secret domain long ago and looked for you, Little Zhi,” Yun Mengmeng remarked as she listened to the music. When she was in the right mood, she would sway her head and hum a few lines, her voice so melodious and pleasing that it harmonized with Gan Tian’s tunes, much to the latter's surprise.

“Did you learn how to sing?”

“Not at all. I just sing for fun.”

Gan Tian was even more surprised. This means that it is pure talent.

“How about we perform together? I'll play, and you'll sing?”

The harmony of the qin and voice would greatly aid her cultivation of the Melody Dao

“Sure.” Yun Mengmeng agreed happily.

Having mastered the divine ability, Lu Yang sheathed the Qingfeng Sword in satisfaction and bid goodbye to the Taciturn Daoist Priest, rushing off eagerly to find Meng Jingzhou.

~~~

“Old Meng, you there? Come out for a spar!” Lu Yang shouted outside Meng Jingzhou’s door.

The old horse stood guard at the entrance, completely disregarding his duty as a guardian, allowing Lu Yang to yell as he pleased.

With the increase in solar power, the old horse had discovered that the hay he was currently sun-drying had become extremely chewy, far tastier than before. Lately, he had been occupied with sun-drying hay.

Gazing at the hay spread across the ground, the old horse felt that this brought him more sense of accomplishment than serving as a guardian ever had.

“Why are you shouting like a ghost?” Meng Jingzhou emerged from ice-cold water, dripping wet from head to toe. To soothe his restless heart, Meng Jingzhou had taken to immersing himself in freezing water, forcing himself to calm down.

“I just learned a couple of moves and wanted to spar with you,” Lu Yang said with a grin.

“Oh ho? Feeling confident in your abilities, are you?” Meng Jingzhou’s interest was piqued. With a shake, he ceased suppressing his yang energy, and the terrifying yang energy radiating from him instantly dried his clothes and hair.

He had been studying under his old ancestor for over a year now, and with the surge in solar power strengthening his Single’s Spirit Root, his improvement could only be described as meteoric. A mere Lu Yang is nothing to fear.

“So what did you learn?” Meng Jingzhou shot a sidelong glance at Lu Yang. I can’t help but feel that this grandson is up to no good.

“Just a couple of little tricks with the sword,” Lu Yang replied with feigned modesty.

Just as Lu Yang didn’t believe Meng Jingzhou’s nonsense, Meng Jingzhou didn’t believe a word of Lu Yang’s either.

Seeing that the two were about to come to blows, the old horse gathered up the hay he had been drying, clearing the space for them.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou stood facing each other on the lawn. A gentle breeze swept through, sending waves across the grassland and rustling their robes.

With a mighty shout, Meng Jingzhou’s abundant yang energy formed a distinctive aura field around him. He settled into a horse stance, fists positioned one before the other, watching Lu Yang warily.

Lu Yang drew the Qingfeng Sword from his waist, the blade scraping against the scabbard’s mouth with a sharp shiiing. He raised the sword steadily, the tip aimed at Meng Jingzhou without the slightest tremor, and demanded sternly, “Meng Jingzhou! Why do you not kneel before this genius?!”

Meng Jingzhou flew into a rage on the spot. “I’ll kneel to your grand—”

Before he could finish speaking, Meng Jingzhou dropped to his knees with a thud, a dazed look on his face.

Even the old horse who was chewing on his hay was dumbfounded. He couldn’t make sense of what technique Lu Yang had just employed.

Lu Yang put on a surprised expression. “Aiya, I was just joking, Old Meng. Why did you actually kneel? No need for that, no need at all.”

This sensation of being forced to kneel was all too familiar to Meng Jingzhou. This is the damn Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array!

The question is, when did Lu Yang activate it?

“Well? Can’t figure out how I did it, can you?” Seeing the dumbstruck expression on Meng Jingzhou’s face, Lu Yang was incredibly thrilled.

Meng Jingzhou nodded honestly. He really wanted to know how Lu Yang did it.

“Simple. My Qingfeng Sword contains a small world. I can activate the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array inside it, then execute Ten Thousand Swords Return to One. That way, whoever I point this sword at will have to kneel.”

Meng Jingzhou. “...”

This is what you call a little trick with the sword?

He had prepared himself to counter Lu Yang’s Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array, but no amount of preparation could have let him anticipate how much the array had evolved.

Who could possibly defend against that?

Lu Yang stopped the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array, allowing Meng Jingzhou to rise.

“Come, come, now we’ll officially begin fighting.” Lu Yang smiled, assured of his victory.

Meng Jingzhou ground his teeth in frustration. Do you really think I have no way to deal with you?

“Take my sword! Breaking Word Mantra!” With a yell, Lu Yang thrust the Qingfeng Sword forward. It tore through the air, swift as lightning.

The corner of Meng Jingzhou’s mouth curled into a cold smirk. It’s just the Breaking Word Mantra. You’re totally looking down on me.

He originally wanted to face it head-on, but suddenly, an inexplicable sense of foreboding seized him, causing him to instinctively dodge. A trench now scarred the spot where Meng Jingzhou once stood.

This is definitely not the power of the Breaking Word Mantra!

“That’s not the Breaking Word Mantra at all, damn it!”

Meng Jingzhou suddenly recalled that when Lu Yang was explaining how to secretly employ the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array, he had mentioned needing to execute it first, then combine it with Ten Thousand Swords Return to One.

If I take a step back and think about it, is it possible to just perform Ten Thousand Swords Return to One?

Of course, that’s possible.

This strike outwardly appears to be the Breaking Word Mantra, but in truth, it is Ten Thousand Swords Return to One!

A massive hand emanating an ancient, primordial aura materialized behind Meng Jingzhou, its elbow bending to shield him.

A resounding clang echoed as the Qingfeng Sword collided with the ancient hand, piercing its surface and nearly penetrating it.

“Dharma manifestation?” Lu Yang exclaimed in surprise. This ancient hand was part of some kind of dharma manifestation. It seems that Old Meng had learned to manifest a dharma body while studying under Meng Junzi.

Lu Yang struck again, his sword meeting the ancient hand again.

Surprisingly, the Qingfeng Sword failed to pierce it this time—it was merely an ordinary sword move.

Just as Meng Jingzhou was about to retract the ancient hand, Lu Yang delivered a fourth strike, once again nearly penetrating the hand, frightening Meng Jingzhou into refraining from any other actions.

Ten Thousand Swords Return to One!

Meng Jingzhou’s forehead was drenched in sweat as he vaguely figured out Lu Yang’s battle tactic.

There was no discernible difference between Ten Thousand Swords Return to One and an ordinary sword strike. One couldn’t distinguish them without engaging the moves.

And he simply dared not gamble on what sword move Lu Yang would employ next, as a single wrong guess meant defeat. His only option was to maintain the dharma manifestation continuously.

Lu Yang thrust the Qingfeng Sword again and again in rapid succession, interspersing numerous ordinary moves with occasional strikes of Ten Thousand Swords Return to One.

Meng Jingzhou still couldn’t sustain the dharma manifestation indefinitely. In the end, the ancient hand disintegrated, and he was forced to admit defeat.

“Alright, alright, you win.” Meng Jingzhou glared at Lu Yang sullenly. “Where did you learn such a devious move?”

Forget myself, any Basic Divine Transfiguration cultivator would be hard-pressed to deal with such an underhanded move.

Lu Yang straightened out his collar and replied earnestly, “Shifu said I must tell outsiders that I comprehended this technique myself and that it has nothing to do with him.”

Chapter 930: The Barbarian Tribe’s Ancestor With the Highest Combat Prowess

Logically speaking, such an underhanded move did seem like something the Taciturn Daoist Priest would teach, but Meng Jingzhou couldn’t shake the feeling that Lu Yang wasn’t being entirely truthful.

“Did the sect leader really say that?” Meng Jingzhou eyed Lu Yang suspiciously.

Lu Yang took umbrage at Meng Jingzhou’s suspicion. I have spoken nothing but the truth. “If I’m lying to you, may I be hit by a couple more lightning strikes during my heavenly tribulation. Is that enough?”

Since he had already weathered the Qian-Heaven Heavenly Tribulation—the number one heavenly tribulation at the Divine Transfiguration level—at the Nascent Soul Stage, Lu Yang figured that when he eventually had to undergo his tribulation to break through to the next realm, it would surely be a walk in the park.

Meng Jingzhou rolled his eyes and was about to retort when Lu Yang suddenly vanished before his eyes, frightening him.

“Where did he go? Did retribution really come for him?”

~~~

Somewhere in the wild mountains of Great Xia, three figures darted and clashed in fierce combat. Mountains shifted, and heaven and earth were turned upside down.

Boom!

The two weaker figures were sent flying, piercing through a mountain and embedding themselves in the cliff face of the next.

“Senior Sister Lan Ting, are you alright?” Man Gu crawled out of the cliff wall and asked in concern as he winced. With my thick and coarse skin, suffering such a blow is no big matter, but it might not be the case for Senior Sister Lan Ting.

Lan Ting was wrapped in her waistband as she crawled out from an adjacent cliff wall. The waistband had cushioned most of the attack’s impact, sparing her from serious injury.

“Two juniors, did you truly believe that reaching the Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage would allow you to challenge someone of a higher level?” Their opponent gazed at them coldly, emanating the aura of a Basic Fusion cultivator.

Both Man Gu and Lan Ting were engaging a Fusion cultivator in formal combat for the first time. Based on their battle prowess, they indeed had the qualifications to challenge a Basic Fusion cultivator, provided that the other party didn’t employ [Rules].

Initially, their combined efforts had given them the upper hand, but once their opponent activated [Rules], the tide of battle reversed completely, leaving the pair battered and disheveled.

“It seems we can’t win. What do we do?”

After advancing to the Divine Transfiguration Stage, Man Gu had gone to the Great Mission Hall to accept his first mission, which concerned leads on the Heartless Creed. Upon arriving at the designated location, he bumped into Lan Ting, who had also come to investigate.

Joining forces, they managed to follow the faint traces to uncover clues about the Heartless Creed, thus encountering this Heartless Creed elder before them.

The only problem was that it seemed they couldn’t defeat him.

With the Heartless Creed elder right before their eyes, if they fled now, finding him again in the future would be exceedingly difficult.

“Fight!” Lan Ting declared through gritted teeth.

Man Gu was also decisive. Fight we shall! He transmitted an auditory message to Lan Ting. “Senior Lan Ting, please hold off the Heartless Creed elder. I have a way to summon the bygone power of a Barbarian Tribe ancestor to descend upon my primordial soul. Perhaps it can turn the tide.”

“Got it!” Lan Ting chose to trust Man Gu and charged forward.

“Reckless juniors courting death.” The Heartless Creed elder wielded a bone saber whose hilt was composed of numerous tiny skulls. When swung, it emitted a chilling sound, like ghosts wailing.

Lan Ting dared not meet the Heartless Creed elder head-on. Her cyan waistband fluttered, overcoming hardness with softness. They coiled around the Heartless Creed elder’s arm, altering the trajectory of his saber. Her movements were light and ethereal, like an immortal fairy dancing in the Moon Palace, leaving the Heartless Creed unable to bring out his full strength.

“I hereby establish Rule: The bone saber cuts through all things!”

A layer of mysterious force adhered to the bone saber’s surface. With a single slash, it sliced Lan Ting’s waistband into tatters. Freed from the annoying interference of the waistband, the Heartless Creed elder swung his blade directly at Lan Ting.

Man Gu summoned his primordial soul and rubbed his hands vigorously as he murmured incantations. His advancement to the Divine Transfiguration Stage had resolved the unpredictability that came with summoning his ancestors’ power at the Nascent Soul Stage.

“By the blessings of immortals, Man Gu humbly welcomes the Barbarian Tribe’s ancestor with the strongest combat prowess!”

Man Gu’s primordial soul transformed. A dazzling milky-white radiance flashed, and a surge of immense power descended from the heavens, pouring into his primordial soul.

The Barbarian Tribe ancestor abruptly lifted his head. In an instant, he teleported and materialized before the Heartless Creed elder.

Clang!

Sword in hand, the Barbarian Tribe ancestor blocked the bone saber that was supposed to cut through all things.

Lan Ting stared in disbelief at the Barbarian Tribe ancestor who had saved her, her mouth agape. “Senior Brother Lu Yang, when did you become the Barbarian Tribe’s ancestor?”

Man Gu was equally astonished. Why has my primordial soul transformed into Senior Brother Lu Yang?

“Ah?” Lu Yang was just as bewildered, completely unable to make heads or tails of the situation. I was bamboozling Meng Jingzhou a moment ago. How did I end up here in the blink of an eye?

The instant he arrived, he saw Lan Ting in peril, so he had no choice but to strike first and talk later.

“Never mind all that for now. Who’s this in front of us?” Lu Yang asked, sensing the murderous intent from their opponent. This is no friendly spar.

“An elder of the Heartless Creed!”

“Then let’s deal with him first and worry about everything else after!”

Under the enhancement of the [Rule], the bone saber was extremely sharp, cleaving apart anything it touched—except for the Qingfeng Sword.

The Qingfeng Sword was an immortal sword, not something a mere Fusion cultivator employing rules could damage.

“Die!” Killing intent kindled in Lu Yang’s eyes as well. Against the Heartless Creed, there is no need to hold back. It’s fine as long as the soul remains.

“Taste my sword!”

The Heartless Creed elder cast a disdainful glance at Lu Yang’s sword strike. It’s so ordinary, yet you wish to injure me?

Crack. Squelch.

This strike cleanly severed the bone saber, and the sword’s power, which was hardly diminished, rended the Heartless Creed elder! A gash ran from the elder’s left shoulder down to his right flank, blood pouring forth in torrents.

Lu Yang was also taken aback. The force behind this sword strike had exceeded even his own expectations.

Ever since arriving here, he had sensed an additional power within him that didn’t belong to him, making him several times stronger than at his peak.

The Heartless Creed elder was completely caught off guard by this turn of events. He tried to create distance and employ [Rules] to heal his wounds, but Lu Yang had witnessed countless battles among high-level cultivators and immortals. He understood all too well what the elder intended. freewebnovel.com
