How could he possibly give him that chance?!

Lu Yang closed the distance with lightning speed and delivered another identical sword strike, startling the Heartless Creed elder so much that he had no time to invoke rules and hastily activated his power to block.

Yet this sword strike was unexpectedly ordinary.

Just as he thought it was over, Lu Yang spat forth Three Flavor True Fire directly into his face.

“Ah!” The Three Flavor True Fire seared the elder’s face relentlessly, the agony ripping a scream from his throat. He was forced to divert power to suppress the true fire.

Lu Yang struck repeatedly, concealing Ten Thousand Swords Return to One within his deceptively plain sword moves, catching the Heartless Creed elder off guard at every turn.

“Blood Sea Vengeful Sky!” the Heartless Creed intoned in a low voice. Behind him, a vast sea of blood surged into existence, within which countless ghosts and living beings thrashed and wailed in supplication. They extended innumerable arms, wanting to drag Lu Yang into that crimson sea!

Lu Yang pointed his sword at the Heartless Creed elder and yelled sternly, “Kneel!”

The Heartless Creed elder found himself utterly unable to resist, dropping to his knees with a thud. His technique was interrupted, and the surging sea of blood behind him disappeared.

An incredibly swift sword light flashed, and an exceedingly fine line of blood appeared on the elder’s neck.

Blood sprayed forth, and his head tumbled through the air. Upon landing on the ground, it rolled until it stopped at Lu Yang’s feet.

Lu Yang sheathed his sword and gazed at Man Gu and Lan Ting. “So, can someone explain to me just what in the world happened?”

Chapter 931: Lu Yang’s Seniority

Man Gu and Lan Ting were about to rush to Lu Yang’s aid, but before they could even move, they witnessed him decapitate the Heartless Creed elder with a series of sword moves as fluid as flowing water.

Even when they saw the Heartless Creed elder’s wide eyes staring at them with nothing but a head, they still felt a sense of surreal disorientation.

The two of them took turns explaining the sequence of events, and Lu Yang finally grasped roughly what had transpired.

“In other words, you two ran into a Heartless Creed elder you couldn’t defeat, so you summoned me?”

“I summoned our Barbarian Tribe’s ancestor with the highest combat prowess,” Man Gu said, correcting him.

Lu Yang could only press his hand to his forehead in resignation. He recalled how he had gone so far as to acknowledge the Everlasting Immortal Fairy as his shifu for the sake of learning the Play-Dead Technique.

She had claimed that becoming her disciple would elevate his seniority, placing him on the same generational level as those in the Ancient Barbarian Tribe.

Now it seems like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy really didn’t deceive me.

What is the trait of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe? They were a special branch of humanity upon whom the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had planted her Tame Head Curse. From this perspective, I’m a bona fide member of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe.

In fact, I may be the most ancient and purest among them all.

Man Gu’s primordial soul could invoke the power left behind in the world by the Barbarian ancestors. Since those ancestors had long since become a part of history, only a fraction of their power lingered between heaven and earth. Man Gu’s primordial soul could summon only that remnant of power.

Now that I, a bona fide Barbarian Tribe ancestor, am still alive and kicking, I was summoned directly.

“I had no idea, Brother Lu. So you are an ancestor of our Barbarian Tribe?” Man Gu asked cautiously, regarding Lu Yang with reverence.

Lan Ting also gazed at Lu Yang in astonishment. No wonder they say that hanging out with Dao-Seeking Sect disciples can broaden one’s horizons.

Lu Yang. “...”

I also just found out myself.

“Junior Sister Lan Ting, long time no see,” Lu Yang greeted with a smile. The last time he saw her was when the Vast Sea Daoist Lord had emerged after dealing with the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord. A crowd of cultivation experts had come to pay their respects then.

Lan Ting smiled. Clad in a cyan top and a gauze skirt, with strands of hair clinging to her face after the battle, she possessed a unique charm. “Although we haven’t met for a while, Senior Brother Lu Yang, your reputation has certainly reached my ears.

"Rescuing the Dragon Ancient Ancestor at the East Sea and leaving her indebted to you, composing the timeless ci poem for Ye Mengmeng, reporting the Fourth Imperial Prince’s rebellion, saving the Sword Tower Supreme Lord and Senior Sister Yun Zhi at the Sword Tower, holding off the Heaven Mandate Immortal...”

Lu Yang broke out in a cold sweat upon hearing the last line. How did that rumor spread?

Ah, right. Back then, Yun Mengmeng had fought the Heaven Mandate corpse while borrowing Big Senior Sister’s name. Given Yun Mengmeng’s and Big Senior Sister’s temperaments, they likely couldn’t be bothered to clarify matters afterward. In the eyes of the world, it would naturally appear as though I had spoken up to save Big Senior Sister!

“They’re all rumors.” Lu Yang laughed dryly, not daring to acknowledge these matters, especially since some had been the work of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy while she took over his body.

However, to Lan Ting and Man Gu, it seemed like Lu Yang was simply modest, and their admiration for him only deepened.

“By the way, ever since I arrived here, I’ve sensed an additional power within that doesn’t belong to me. Do you know what’s going on?” Without that power bolstering him, even though his techniques were swift and ingenious, and the Heartless Creed elder had already been worn down by Man Gu and Lan Ting, he wouldn’t have finished the elder off so quickly.

Man Gu was taken aback. “What a coincidence. I sense that my primordial soul is within you, Brother Lu.”

“Junior Brother Man...perhaps you could try ending your invocation to the ancestors?”

“Oh, oh, of course.” Man Gu terminated the ancestral invocation.

Man Gu’s primordial soul drifted out of Lu Yang’s body and returned to him, while Lu Yang’s power also reverted to its original state.

“Why is your summoning one-way?” Lu Yang was still thinking about returning to continue bamboozling Meng Jingzhou.

Noticing that Lu Yang wasn’t in a rush to leave, Lan Ting’s eyes lit up. “Senior Brother Lu Yang, if you have no urgent matters, why don’t you visit our Moon Laurel Immortal Palace as a guest? We could spar a little and improve together.”

Lu Yang indeed had no pressing matters at the moment. “But isn’t your Moon Laurel Immortal Palace off-limits to males?”

“There’s no such strict rule.” Lan Ting chuckled.

Lu Yang mulled over it. Since she has extended an invitation, wouldn’t it be ungracious to refuse her kindness? freewebnovel.com

Besides, I do want to see what the legendary Moon Laurel Immortal Palace looks like.

“Then I’ll have to trouble you, Junior Sister Lan Ting.”

As Man Gu watched the two chat amiably, he couldn’t help but feel he was unnecessary.

“To whom should the soul of this Heartless Creed elder belong?” Lan Ting and I had accepted the mission, so which sect should we bring this elder back to?

“That’s easily settled.” From observing how Jiang Ping’an had divided Guan Shanhai’s soul, Lu Yang had more or less grasped the method.

He evenly smeared a few drops of his blood onto the blade of his sword, affixed several incantations, and then extracted the soul hidden in the Heartless Creed elder’s head.

He ignored the elder’s blood-curdling screams and brought down his sword, neatly splitting the three ethereal souls and seven corporeal souls. Lan Ting took the three ethereal souls, while Man Gu took the seven corporeal souls.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, do you not want a share?” Lan Ting asked. He clearly contributed the most.

Lu Yang waved his hand dismissively. He was wealthy with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s contribution points at his disposal. A mere Fusion cultivator is hardly worth anything.

A thought seemed to have struck Lu Yang, and he instructed Man Gu seriously, “By the way, Junior Brother Man, when you return, make sure to emphasize to Senior Brother Dai how much I contributed. It’ll be a great chance to improve my image in his eyes.”

“Alright.”

“Junior Sister Lan Ting, let’s go.”

~~~

Dai Bufan was quite surprised to see Man Gu bringing back the three ethereal souls of a Heartless Creed elder. The mission had been for Man Gu to investigate leads on the Heartless Creed.

I didn’t expect him to track down a high-ranking member right away. It’s truly an unexpected delight. With the elder’s three ethereal souls, we’ll definitely be able to capture more Heartless Creed higher-ups after performing a soul search!

“Junior Brother Man, I never expected you to slay a Basic Fusion cultivator at the Divine Transfiguration Stage. Impressive.”

Man Gu chuckled sheepishly, not taking credit. “All the credit goes to Senior Sister Lan Ting and Senior Brother Lu Yang. I didn’t contribute much.”

“How so? Tell me about it.”

Man Gu recounted in detail how he and Lan Ting had met, found the clues, and run into the Heartless Creed elder. Following Lu Yang’s wishes, Man Gu emphasized Lu Yang’s timely appearance, his rescue of Lan Ting at the critical juncture, and his decapitation of the Heartless Creed elder to demonstrate his paramount contribution.

Dai Bufan found this amusing. How did Lu Yang become a Barbarian Tribe ancestor?

“It seems Junior Brother Lu isn’t only capable of giving me scares; he can do many good deeds, too. I never imagined him to play such a pivotal role in this matter,” Dai Bufan remarked with a smile.

In the past, it wasn’t that Lu Yang didn’t do good deeds. It was that while doing good deeds, he also managed to give me tremendous scares, like when he suddenly established the Heavenly Court Creed to infiltrate the diabolic creeds, discovered Founding Ancestor Innate, and so on.

It’s different this time. Lu Yang has only done good deeds and has not given me any scares.

“Is everything you’ve said true?” Dai Bufan asked, verifying it once more.

Man Gu honestly replied, “Yes, it’s true. It’s exactly what Senior Brother Lu Yang had told me to say.”

A question mark popped into Dai Bufan’s head.

Chapter 932: Visiting the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace

Stretching across the expanse between the Central Continent and the Extreme North lay an unbroken chain of snow-capped mountains. Snow fell throughout the year there, and clear skies were rare.

“So this is the legendary Great Snow Mountain.” Lu Yang stood at the mountain’s base. Shielding his eyes, he gazed upward. Beyond the swirling, feathery snowflakes, a majestic, pure-white mountain lay quietly before him.

“It’s hardly legendary.” Lan Ting chuckled from beside him. “It’s merely because the place is too remote, and few are willing to come here.”

This was spoken out of modesty. The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace was considered a semi-reclusive immortal sect, rarely engaging with the outside world. Any external communication, such as seeking their aid, issuing missions, convening meetings for the righteous path, and arranging immortal sect gatherings, passed through the Great Communications Hall at the mountain’s foot.

However, there were exceptions in which outsiders could proceed directly to the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace without these procedures. For instance, when Lan Ting escorted Lu Yang up the mountain, it was what the common folk typically referred to as “using connections to enter through the back door.”

Along the small winding path leading up the mountain, small trees resembling translucent jade frequently appeared on both sides. Taller than a man, they were as exquisite as works of art.

“Are these moon laurel trees?” Lu Yang asked. It was his first time encountering a living one; previously, he had only seen their branches in the outside world.

Moon laurel trees grew only on the Great Snow Mountain. Removed from this environment, no divine method could sustain their lives.

“Mmm. The entire Great Snow Mountain is covered with them. Legend has it that during a war among ancient immortals three hundred thousand years ago, the stars were remolded into continents, and the moon was transformed into what is now the Great Snow Mountain.”

“Immortal Fairy, is that true?” Lu Yang sought confirmation from the intermittently effective Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Probably. Analyzing the soil composition beneath our feet, it is indeed the moon. In our era, moon laurel trees did grow on the moon. The jade rabbits often dug burrows beneath them. The Nine-Layers Immortal frequently visited the moon to catch jade rabbits for breeding, and the Heaven Mandate Immortal regularly took his Heaven-Splitting Axe to chop down moon laurel trees on the moon and bring them back for me to use as firewood.

“Let me tell you, food cooked over moon laurel wood carries a unique fragrance; no other type of wood can produce a similar aroma.”

The two climbed the Great Snow Mountain at a leisurely pace. Towering thirty thousand meters high, it was the tallest peak in the cultivation world, and ordinary cultivators found it difficult to scale. However, Lu Yang and Lan Ting were already at the Divine Transfiguration Stage, so climbing the mountain was as effortless as walking on level ground.

The closer they drew to the summit, the more frequently moon laurel trees appeared, and the taller they became, all exceeding ten meters.

When Lu Yang climbed onto a massive rocky platform, he beheld a pristine white palace nestled among the mountain peaks, magnificent and ethereal, resembling an immortal realm. It was the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, known to many through hearsay, but a place few had set foot in.

Lan Ting led Lu Yang to the entrance. Spotting a man approaching, the two female disciples on guard duty instinctively grew vigilant, raising their spears to bar the way.

Just as Lan Ting was about to explain, the two disciples recognized Lu Yang. Their hesitant voices were tinged with delight as they asked, “Could you be Senior Brother Lu Yang from the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

Lu Yang nodded, though he couldn’t help but feel that the gazes of these two female disciples were somewhat unusual.

Lan Ting inwardly exclaimed, Oh dear! I had only thought of inviting Lu Yang to the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace to bring us closer, but I had forgotten just how popular he is here!

“Did Young Master Meng, the Imperial City’s Buddha Scion, not come?” The two female disciples peered about, eager to catch a glimpse of the legendary, aloof Buddha Scion, who was renowned for his unsmiling demeanor, his distance from women, and his wholehearted devotion to the Dao.

“He’s at a critical stage in his cultivation, so it’s not convenient for him to come here,” Lu Yang replied. This was the truth. Given Meng Jingzhou’s current situation, the most important thing was to distance himself from female allure. A place like the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, which is teeming with beauties, is a forbidden zone for him.

“So that’s how it is. Senior Brother, please enter.” Without needing any explanation from Lan Ting, the two female disciples directly permitted his passage.

Just as Lan Ting had said earlier, the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace’s rules were not actually so strict.

Of course, whether the rules were strict mainly depended on who the visitor was. If it were the Taciturn Daoist Priest, the treatment wouldn’t have been so favorable.

Lan Ting was already beginning to regret bringing Lu Yang here. It would have been better to simply host him at my own home.

But I’ve already brought him to the entrance. It’s too late for regrets.

Within the immortal palace, everything was adorned with silver. In the vast expanse of white, a thick layer of snow blanketed the eaves and gathered on the treetops.

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace naturally possessed the ability to clear the snow, but its founder, the Moonchaser True Person, believed this environment to be conducive to cultivating luna power and that there was no need to erect a barrier to keep the heavy snow outside.

“I’ll take you to see my shifu first,” Lan Ting said.

Lu Yang’s expression shifted subtly.

Lan Ting’s shifu, Luo Hongxia, also the palace leader of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, was from the same era as the Taciturn Daoist Priest. She was a highly respected elder, but Lu Yang had defeated her when her cultivation had been suppressed to the same level as his.

Perhaps one couldn’t exactly say that Lu Yang had defeated her. To be more accurate, it was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy who took over Lu Yang’s body who defeated her, leaving her mouth stuffed with leaves.

Fearing that other disciples would discover Lu Yang’s presence, Lan Ting hurriedly tugged him along to find her shifu.

Unfortunately, no matter their speed, they couldn’t run within the immortal palace. Along the way, they encountered several disciples, all of whom recognized the renowned Lu Yang.

Before they could even open their mouths to inquire, Lan Ting had already pulled Lu Yang away and run into the distance.

~~~

“Shifu, look who I’ve brought!” Lan Ting announced excitedly upon arriving at the palace leader’s cave abode.

“Lu Yang?” A flicker of discomfort crossed Luo Hongxia’s face as memories of being beaten by him surfaced.

“Junior Lu Yang pays respects to Palace Leader Luo.” Lu Yang was always well-behaved before elders; the only times he wasn’t obedient were when the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had taken over his body.

“Shifu, while I was out on a mission, I ran into a Heartless Creed elder. It was Senior Brother Lu Yang who appeared and saved me. I thought I should invite him to our immortal palace as a guest. May I?”

As the palace leader’s disciple, Lan Ting possessed life-preserving techniques. Even without Lu Yang’s intervention, her life wouldn’t have been in danger. However, this didn’t prevent her from framing the events in a different way.

Luo Hongxia’s eye twitched almost imperceptibly. You’ve already brought him before me, yet you’re still asking if you may? Can I really say no?

Seeing Lan Ting’s rare display of delight, Luo Hongxia sighed inwardly. I’ve long advised keeping a distance from Dao-Seeking Sect disciples, lest they influence one’s thinking. My good disciple has clearly paid no heed to my words.

A daughter grown is a daughter lost; you can’t restrain a girl once she’s grown up.

She sighed again in her heart, though her countenance remained composed. “Since you’re indebted to him for saving your life, inviting him to our immortal palace as a guest doesn’t count as violating the rules.”

Having obtained her shifu’s approval, Lan Ting gleefully led Lu Yang out of the cave abode.

As soon as they pushed open the door, they found it crowded by numerous disciples, a flurry of beauties that left Lu Yang dazzled and disoriented. freewebnovel.com

“We finally get to meet the legendary Senior Brother Lu Yang?”

“Don’t push, don’t push.”

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, how long will you be staying at the immortal palace?”

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, can you tell us what the Dragon Ancient Ancestor is like?”

The immortal palace disciples were immensely curious about this Senior Brother Lu Yang, who was surrounded by numerous legends. News of his arrival had spread swiftly, and everyone flocked to the door, eager to see how the real Lu Yang compared to his portraits.

When had Lu Yang encountered so many beautiful female cultivators? He was momentarily at a loss, a rare expression of embarrassment creeping onto his visage.

Chapter 933: Earth Core’s Fire

Lu Yang had weathered countless storms, surviving immortal battles more than once or twice. Yet, he had never encountered a situation where he was surrounded by a throng of female cultivators.

Half of Lu Yang’s popularity could be attributed to the genuinely legendary nature of his experiences. Accomplishing even one of his feats in most cultivators’ lifetime would already be rare, let alone the multitude he had accumulated.

The other half was attributed to the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s tireless promotion. Employing the Spring and Autumn Brushwork with selective embellishment and fabricated details, he had portrayed Lu Yang as an image of perfection.

Although everyone knew the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s words couldn’t be trusted, the constant recitation of Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Lu Yang had caused them to subconsciously associate the Lu Yang of the tales with the Lu Yang of reality.

“You don’t know what to do? Let me handle it!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy declared, taking charge with the air of a female boss.

Lu Yang was naturally not deceived by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s facade, instead asking calmly, “Immortal Fairy, have you ever encountered such a situation?”

“Of course I have! What situation have I not seen? Back when I created the Mother-Child River, many female cultivators came to pay homage, seeking the river’s water and praying to me for children. The situation then wasn’t too different from now.”

It’s far different! Lu Yang felt relieved that he hadn’t rashly handed over control of his body to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Otherwise, who knows what chaos she would stir up?

Since he was at a loss for what to do, he considered taking out a recording orb to capture the scene. It’s a pity that Old Meng can’t visit the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace. Showing him the recording after I return should somewhat make up for it.

Lu Yang felt that he was truly a good brother, taking care of everything so thoroughly.

Although Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy were unreliable, at least Lan Ting was reliable.

“Alright, that’s enough, calm down, everyone. Senior Brother Lu Yang will be staying at the immortal palace for an extended period. You will have plenty of time to interact with him next time. There’s no need to crowd around and make things difficult for him!” Lan Ting persuaded them loudly a few more times, and only then did the immortal palace disciples gradually disperse.

Lu Yang was bewildered. Wasn’t it said that I would stay for just a few days? How had it suddenly become an extended stay?

Lan Ting quickly pressed her palms together in apology. “I’m sorry. With how urgent the situation was, I had no choice but to say that. Otherwise, they wouldn’t have left.”

She lifted her head, sneakily peeking at Lu Yang’s expression, and spoke abashedly. “Senior Brother Lu Yang, could I trouble you to stay at the immortal palace a while longer? Now that I’ve said it, if you leave after just two days, my credibility will be...

“But don’t worry, Senior Brother. Our immortal palace doesn’t lack cultivation resources. Whatever you need for your cultivation, I...we will provide.”

With the matter put this way, Lu Yang could only agree. After all, he could cultivate anywhere; he wasn’t picky about the location.

“Let me take you to your lodgings first,” Lan Ting said hastily upon seeing her ploy had succeeded.

Soon, Lan Ting led Lu Yang to a row of connected courtyards. These were the guest quarters of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace. Each courtyard housed a moon laurel tree. When guests opened their doors or windows, they could behold these trees, which were as precious as immortal treasures.

There were no other guests at the moment, so Lan Ting arranged for Lu Yang to stay in the first courtyard.

The courtyard exuded an antique charm, with thick layers of snow blanketing the ground and roof tiles, painting a uniquely beautiful scene. The room contained a Spirit-Energy Gathering Array, sufficient even for a Fusion cultivator’s cultivation.

The only flaw was the presence of a bronze mirror, rouge, and other such items in the room, which were incongruous with Lu Yang’s gender... This was a guest room intended for female cultivators.

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace had never considered the matter of hosting male cultivators.

“I’ll tidy it up right away!” Lan Ting said, flustered. She had only thought of inviting Lu Yang to the immortal palace, not considering that there would be no suitable room for him.

“It’s fine, it’s fine. Just leave them here.” Lu Yang was embarrassed to trouble Lan Ting further. Let’s just leave the bronze mirror, rouge, and other items on the dressing table. I won’t have a use for them anyway, and their presence won’t hinder anything. There’s no need to go through the trouble of moving them.

It’s not as if this is my first time staying in a place that resembles a maiden’s boudoir. Back when the Everlasting Immortal Fairy occupied my mental space, she had decorated it in a pink, girly style. Compared to her boudoir, this immortal palace’s guest room is actually quite decent.

If not for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s current ambition to establish the Great Dou Dynasty, which prompted her to transform the mental space into a palace, my mental space would still be all soft pink.

As they spoke, Lu Yang noticed that within his mental space, heavy feather-like snow had begun to fall, soon covering the ground and even the imperial throne.

“Woohoo, it’s snowing!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy leaped from the throne and threw herself onto the snowy ground, rolling back and forth, her laughter echoing unceasingly.

There’s no need to ask—it’s obviously the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s doing again, wanting a change of environment.

“Xiao Yangzi, come play with me!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy lay prone on the ground, legs kicking in the air. She tilted her head back to look at Lu Yang as she invited him.

Without a moment’s hesitation, Lu Yang declined. “No, I still need to tour the immortal palace.”

~~~

“This is the pill concoction chamber.” Lan Ting led Lu Yang to an adjacent building.

Lu Yang could sense heatwaves radiating endlessly from within, and their stability was astonishing.

Lan Ting added, “Beneath this place lies a fire from the earth’s core. The pill concoction chamber channels this fire upward to serve as the fire focal point. Supplementing it with various true fires will elevate the temperature and impart diverse properties for pill concoction.

“Legend has it that this is no natural fire, but a mouthful of immortal fire passed down from the ancient era, burning continuously until now!” Lan Ting’s expression revealed her admiration. An immortal fire that has been burning for three hundred thousand years, just how powerful must those ancient immortals have been?

Within the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was scooping up piles of snow and tossing them skyward when she suddenly sensed something. She exclaimed in delight, “Eh, isn’t this the fire I left behind when we were barbecuing on the moon back then?

“At the time, the Heaven Mandate Immortal got tired of hauling moon laurel trees back and forth, so he suggested we just set up a campfire and eat on the moon. We ate with such relish that the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others all passed out from being too full. I had to send them back one by one.

“Could it be that I was so focused on transporting them that I forgot to put out the fire?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was one to correct her mistakes. She prepared to extinguish the immortal fire, but Lu Yang quickly stopped her.

“Your Exalted Majesty’s willingness to correct your mistakes is truly gratifying. You are a rare, wise ruler in history. However, the common people still rely on this immortal fire for their livelihoods. There’s no need to extinguish it.”

“Oh, alright then.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was indeed a wise ruler. Despite being stopped from an absurd act by a trusted aide, she was not angry—a rare occurrence for rulers in history.

“To the right is a restricted zone. Senior Brother Lu Yang, you must absolutely not approach it, lest you put your life in danger.” Lan Ting pointed to the right of the pill concoction chamber, where a luxuriously decorated palace hall stood. Even the pillars supporting its entrance were over ten meters high.

“What is that place?”

“The hot spring pool. The earth's core fire is still abundant, so when our predecessors constructed the immortal palace, they also built this hot spring.”

Lan Ting then pointed to the left. “The artifact refinement chamber on the left operates on a similar principle to the pill concoction chamber, also harnessing the earth’s core fire.”

Helping the immortal palace retain the earth’s core fire, thereby enabling the continued existence of the pill concoction chamber, hot spring pool, and artifact refinement chamber, was a great meritorious deed. Lu Yang mused, If one could cultivate through the power of merit, I would have long since reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage with just my meritorious achievements.

Chapter 934: The Thorough Founding Ancestor Moonchaser

Lu Yang was somewhat surprised. He had not expected that a place inhabited solely by female cultivators, like the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, would have an artifact refinement chamber. Typically, few female cultivators were willing to engage in forging artifacts.

After all, while pursuing cultivation, female cultivators also valued elegance and aesthetics. For instance, Lu Yang had never seen a female cultivator swinging a huge hammer like Man Gu, nor a female cultivator whose body would split apart like Li Haoran’s.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, do you find it strange that we female cultivators engage in artifact refinement?” Lan Ting noticed the peculiar look in Lu Yang’s eyes, roughly guessing what was on his mind.

“No, not at all,” Lu Yang replied with an awkward laugh.

“It’s not strange to think that way. Indeed, there are very few female artifact refiners in the outside world. It’s our immortal palace that has some unique aspects.”

“Unique aspects?”

“We have moon laurel trees.”

Seeing Lu Yang’s still perplexed expression, Lan Ting led him to a small grove filled with moon laurel trees. If these were to be sold in the outside world, they would fetch an astronomical price. freewebnovel.com

Before even entering the moon laurel grove, Lu Yang heard a continuous, muffled thumping sound, like the collision of two heavy objects.

Then he saw numerous immortal palace disciples taking turns swinging axes at the moon laurel trees. They were all panting from exhaustion, drenched in sweat. It was difficult to imagine that these were the same women with the ethereal image of immortal fairies who abstained from ordinary grains in public.

Lu Yang noticed that whenever a disciple struck a moon laurel tree, a gash would appear, only to mend itself rapidly, as though it had never been there. The disciples then had to continue chopping, repeating the cycle endlessly without pause.

“What is this?”

“This is a tradition passed down from our founding ancestor, the Moonchaser True Person. Legend has it that the Heaven Mandate Immortal frequently chopped down moon laurel trees with an axe in the ancient era, for reasons unknown. The Moonchaser True Person believed that every action of ancient immortals carried profound meaning and that this must be some form of cultivation method. Hence, she advocated using axes to chop moon laurel trees as a means of training.

“These moon laurel trees are indeed remarkably resistant to chopping. If a single swing from the axe fails to sever them, the gash will simply heal.”

Lan Ting smiled sheepishly. “Since we’re already swinging axes at moon laurel trees, wielding hammers for artifact refinement no longer seems like a crude activity in our eyes.

“As for the great strength required to swing hammers for artifact forging, we’ve already developed that through chopping moon laurel trees.”

Lu Yang was about to nod when an idea suddenly struck him. Since chopping moon laurel trees is a tradition of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, doesn’t that mean Lan Ting has also done it? If Lan Ting also chops trees, does it make sense for her to fight using those light, fluttery ribbons all day?

“Senior Sister Lan Ting! Senior Brother Lu Yang!”

The immortal palace disciples were diligently chopping trees when they spotted Lan Ting and Lu Yang walking together, their eyes lighting up. They all placed down their axes and approached Lu Yang.

But as they drew near Lu Yang, they hesitated and dared not go closer.

We’ve been chopping moon laurel trees for so long and are covered in sweat stains. If we approach Lu Yang in this state, won’t that be improper?

By the time they realized they could use a Body-Cleansing Incantation, Lan Ting had already pulled Lu Yang away. The two walked deep into the moon laurel grove, not stopping until they reached a tree that towered into the clouds.

Lu Yang gazed upward, unable to see the top of this moon laurel tree. He felt as infinitesimal as a speck of dust standing at its base.

“This is the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor. It existed before our immortal palace was constructed. All the moon laurel trees on this Great Snow Mountain are its descendants. According to research by our predecessors, the Tree Ancestor is most likely a moon laurel tree from the ancient era, far distant in the past.”

“Immortal Fairy, can you determine the age of this tree?”

Within the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was focused on building snowmen. Two snowmen stood side by side, with carrots for noses and branches for arms. Names were written on their bodies—the left one was called Huang Doudou, and the right one was called Lu Yang.

Hearing Lu Yang call her, she diverted her attention to the outside world.

“What a tall moon laurel tree!” Even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hadn’t seen such a massive moon laurel tree before.

“I had seen a moon laurel tree on the moon that was two hundred thousand years old, and it wasn’t this tall. This one must be over two hundred thousand years old. As for its exact age, you either have to cut it down and count the rings or have the Epoch Immortal come and ask him.”

Obviously, neither method was feasible.

“But it very well could be a moon laurel tree from the ancient era,” she added.

“How so?”

“Didn’t I need the Heaven Mandate Immortal to chop firewood for my cooking back then? I instructed him that we must take responsibility for our actions. If he cut down a moon laurel tree, he must remember to plant another one.

“Perhaps this is one among the many moon laurel trees that the Heaven Mandate Immortal planted back then. It’s probably with the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s blessings that it survived until now.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s advanced concept of environmental protection left Lu Yang in awe.

As far as Lu Yang knew, no tree had ever lived for two hundred thousand years. Even if the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor before him wasn’t planted in the ancient era, it must still be the oldest tree in existence, truly worthy of its name.

Exiting the moon laurel grove, they headed to the other end, where a large courtyard stood. Lu Yang saw numerous immortal palace disciples assiduously training within—repeatedly inserting their hands into scorching hot iron sand, shattering boulders of unknown material with a single elbow strike, running while carrying small mountains on their backs...

Lu Yang found this scene strangely familiar. That is exactly how Old Meng tempers his body.

“What are they doing?”

“Body tempering,” Lan Ting replied earnestly.

“Ah?” Lu Yang felt that the cultivation methods of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace were truly distinct from those of female cultivators elsewhere. Even disciples of the Allure Sect, an S-class sect, wouldn’t both swing axes and temper their bodies.

“This also has historical origins. A thousand years after the immortal palace was established, Great Xia had recovered from the chaos of war. The nation was at peace, and the people lived happily. Founding Ancestor Moonchaser descended the mountain to travel.

“Later, she stumbled upon a bookstall and found several improper books. Though the stories differed, they shared a common thread. In each book, an immortal fairy descends the mountain to cultivate and accidentally falls victim to an aphrodisiac poison, and the male protagonist is forced to help her detoxify.

"From there on, the immortal fairy becomes one of the story’s female leads, beginning a complicated entanglement of love and hate with the male protagonist.

“At the start, the male protagonist is an insignificant figure, but as the story progresses, he grows stronger step by step, eventually becoming worthy of the immortal fairy.

“Founding Ancestor Moonchaser felt that although these were mere stories, the content wasn’t without reason; such things could happen in reality.

“Upon her return, she added another element to training—body tempering. All disciples were required to temper their bodies.

“After body tempering, one’s constitution strengthens, greatly weakening the effects of any aphrodisiac poison. This buys time to find an antidote, preventing one from recklessly giving themselves away.

“Time proved that Founding Ancestor Moonchaser’s decision was correct. Over the past one hundred thousand years, many seniors descending the mountain have fallen victim to aphrodisiac poisons. Had they not tempered their bodies, they might have ended up in bed with some random man.

“Furthermore, Founding Ancestor Moonchaser also considered that in these stories, the male and female leads often fell in love, but the female lead’s sect will disapprove, creating obstacles. Eventually, the male lead will achieve fame and success, then return to the female lead’s sect to slap their face and humble them. Therefore, she decreed that if a disciple of our sect fell in love with a man, the sect would not interfere.”

Lu Yang. “...”

Your founding ancestor really thought of everything.

Chapter 935: I Rested Quite Well

Lu Yang felt that this trip to the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace had not been in vain. He had never imagined that every disciple was adept at swinging axes and tempering their bodies. What terrifying strength must lie beneath those delicate figures?!

He had only sparred with Lan Ting a few times, and those were only friendly contests. He never realized that she also possessed immense strength and excelled in body arts.

Even more unexpected were the immortal palace’s liberal rules, which did not interfere in the romantic affairs of their disciples.

This Moonchaser True Person must have been a far-sighted and open-minded senior.

Respect.

“Come to think of it, I’ve never really learned body-tempering techniques.” Lu Yang reflected on his cultivation journey. His focus had primarily been on sword techniques and spells; he hadn’t delved into body tempering.

“What need does our Everlasting Lineage have for body-tempering techniques?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy interjected. “Once you possess the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit, your body will be far sturdier than any physique cultivator’s. Besides, even if you become a physique cultivator, the power of your self-detonation would still be no different from that of an ordinary cultivator, right?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy laid out the pros and cons for Lu Yang with clear logic.

“Well? If you feel your body isn’t sturdy enough, I can give you an Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit now.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was raring to go. As long as Lu Yang nodded and uttered “yes,” she would stuff the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit into his body.

“No,” Lu Yang declined. My goal is to become an immortal and stand alongside Big Senior Sister and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. How could I accept an Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit now? Wouldn’t that make me a disgraceful half-immortal like Li Haoran?

Seeing Lu Yang refuse, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked somewhat disappointed and muttered under her breath, “What’s the big deal if I give you an Incipient Dao Fruit? Why be so standoffish?”

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace was so vast that even after touring for a full day, Lan Ting and Lu Yang had only covered a small part.

“We’ll meet again tomorrow then, Senior Brother.” Lan Ting escorted Lu Yang back to the entrance of the guest courtyard and offered him a sweet smile.

“See you tomorrow.”

By now, night had fallen. The sun above had been replaced by the moon, and the luna power was far denser than before. Night was the most crucial time for the immortal palace disciples’ cultivation. This was why Lan Ting had taken her leave.

“Luna power, huh...” Lu Yang gazed at the moon. His cultivation didn’t rely on solar or luna power, so he couldn’t really distinguish the shifts in these two powers.

Just as Lu Yang was contemplating whether to recite Prelude to Water Melody[1], a petite immortal palace disciple approached coyly, looking somewhat embarrassed.

The disciple greeted politely. “Hello, Senior Brother Lu Yang.”

“You are?”

“I’m Bai Ye, a disciple of the immortal palace.” Bai Ye was rather bashful. Keeping her head lowered, she glanced upward, stealing a glance at Lu Yang. “Senior Brother Lu Yang, could you tell me about your experiences? Like going to the Demon Region and the East Sea?”

She had never ventured to such distant places. When watching storytelling performances, she had always found Lu Yang impressive. He has been everywhere and experienced everything. Now that I’ve finally encountered the real person, I’m determined to hear his tales.

“Don’t you need to cultivate?” Lu Yang had assumed that all immortal palace disciples were like Lan Ting, seizing every moment to cultivate.

“Skipping one day of cultivation won’t hurt,” Bai Ye replied with a grin. Perhaps sensing Lu Yang’s gentle demeanor, she gradually relaxed.

Lu Yang mulled over it. Since I have nothing to do at the moment, there’s no harm in telling stories. At worst, I can omit the parts that shouldn’t be shared, such as resurrecting Jiang Lianyi in the Demon Region.

“Sure.” Lu Yang gestured for her to sit.

“Let me think where to begin... Oh, yes, I’ll start from the second time I went to the Great Mission Hall to accept a mission. The objective was to eliminate a tiger demon...”

With Lu Yang’s rich experiences, even with the secrets omitted, one night was far from enough to recount them all.

Bai Ye listened with rapt attention, her eyes sparkling. Her gaze toward Lu Yang was increasingly filled with admiration. It was hard for her to imagine that these were the experiences of one cultivator. I’m afraid even all the immortal palace disciples combined hadn’t experienced as much as Senior Brother Lu Yang.

“Alright, we’ll stop here for today. The sky is about to turn bright,” Lu Yang said with a smile. He had been talking all night, and it was nearly daybreak now. I can’t possibly continue nonstop; when would it ever end?

“Okay then.” Bai Ye looked as if she hadn’t had her fill. She wanted to hear more, but it was truly too late to continue. “In that case, will you tell stories again tomorrow night, Senior Brother Lu Yang?”

“If you come to listen, I’ll tell them,” Lu Yang replied with a chuckle. He had rather taken a liking to this little immortal palace disciple.

Bai Ye was overjoyed. As she walked away, she waved goodbye to Lu Yang. “Then see you tomorrow night, Senior Brother Lu Yang!”

While the sky hadn’t turned completely bright, Lu Yang returned to his room. He sat down on the Spirit-Energy Gathering Array and opened his mouth wide to devour spirit qi for cultivation.

His entire cultivation had been achieved through such efforts that wasted no seconds. It was exceedingly arduous.

He also took the chance to let his consciousness return to the mental space to find the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, multitasking without delaying anything.

“Immortal Fairy, come play with the snow.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted, quite displeased that Lu Yang had only come to play with her now. She picked up the snowman inscribed with the name “Lu Yang” and hurled it at him. “Hmph! You’re only showing up now.”

Before Lu Yang could even make out the characters on the snowman, he saw it flying straight toward him. He shifted his stance, moving his body with such speed that an afterimage lingered where he had stood.

And then, he failed to dodge.

Wiping the snow from his face, Lu Yang grinned awkwardly. “Unlike you, Immortal Fairy, I haven’t seen much of the world. This is my first time at the immortal palace. Of course, I have to take a good look around.”

Hearing Lu Yang praise her wealth of knowledge and experience, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t prevent the corners of her mouth from twitching upward. “What’s a mere immortal palace? And it’s even an immortal palace without an immortal! Follow me faithfully, and I guarantee I’ll show you genuine immortal creations far superior to this place!”

“Of course, of course. I trust in your abilities, Immortal Fairy.

“What shall we play?” Lu Yang asked next.

In truth, Lu Yang wasn’t simply humoring the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. He hadn’t played with snow for a long time, especially snow this thick. The last time he had seen such snow was in his previous life, and back then, he was in no mood to play.

“Let’s build a snowman. Having only one right now isn’t fun.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pointed at the lonely snowman.

“Then who should we build?”

“There are only the two of us in the mental space, so of course we’ll build you!” With that, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy began rolling a snowball.

Lu Yang joined her in rolling a snowball.

~~~

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, how was your rest last night?” Early the next morning, Lan Ting came looking for Lu Yang.

Lu Yang replied inwardly, When did I rest last night? First, it was storytelling, then it was building a snowman. I had a fun time, but it had nothing to do with the word “rest.”

The snowman named “Lu Yang” residing in his mental space now was the joint masterpiece of him and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“I rested quite well.”

“That's great then.” Lan Ting breathed a sigh of relief. She had been worried about other disciples looking for Lu Yang and bonding with him behind her back. But now, it seems my concern was unnecessary.

1. A poem by Song Dynasty poet Song Shi, also known as Su Dongpo. It has also been adapted to a song. ☜

Chapter 936: Does Your Immortal Palace Need the Twins River?

Lu Yang was quite popular in the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace. As Lan Ting escorted him on his tour of the immortal palace, the disciples also conducted their own “tour” of Lu Yang. Wherever he went, crowds of disciples would surround him, peppering him with all sorts of questions, making him feel like some rare and exotic specimen.

Though male cultivators were indeed a rare and exotic species in the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

“Alright, that’s enough. Don’t forget it’s cultivation time now. Do not let yourselves be distracted.” A steady voice rang out, instantly silencing the chattering disciples. They quickly returned to their places and resumed their cultivation obediently. freewebnovel.com

A cold and aloof female cultivator with a jet-black ring on her middle finger approached.

“Senior Sister Jinghong.” Lan Ting greeted with a bow.

Lu Yang followed suit, mimicking her gesture. “Greetings, Senior Sister Jinghong.”

Jinghong returned the courtesy. “You must be the Junior Brother Lu Yang in the rumors.

“Junior Sister Lan Ting, if you are going to show Junior Brother Lu Yang around our immortal palace, you should keep a low profile. Our junior sisters’ Dao hearts are not steadfast enough. When they see such an outstanding talent like Junior Brother Lu Yang, they will inevitably get excited, rendering their cultivation efforts today wasted.”

“Yes,” Lan Ting acknowledged.

There were also immortal palace disciples like Jinghong, who wasn’t interested in Lu Yang.

Once they were out of Jinghong’s line of sight, Lu Yang whispered, “Why does it feel like Senior Sister Jinghong doesn’t really welcome me?”

Lan Ting tittered. “Senior Brother, don’t find Senior Sister Jinghong cold; she’s like this with everyone.

“She is Third Elder’s disciple and skilled in artifact refinement. She entered the sect before I did and is at the Intermediate Divine Transfiguration Stage. Although her cultivation isn’t top-tier, she’s thorough in her work and steady in character, thus deeply favored by the elders.”

Lu Yang nodded. He thought he had done something wrong to displease her. It’s good to know that wasn’t the case.

~~~

Elsewhere, after Jinghong confirmed no one was nearby, she surreptitiously rubbed her ring and split off a wisp of spiritual consciousness to enter the ring.

“Shifu, is that sufficient?”

An old yet authoritative voice reverberated within the ring’s space. “This will suffice.”

“One senses that this person called Lu Yang is far from simple. He likely harbors a great secret. You should keep your distance from him. Be sure not to become entangled, lest karmic ties form. I am worried that if you become overly involved with him, it may cause him to detect my existence, causing me to emerge prematurely and triggering an upheaval of the ages.”

“Yes.”

~~~

“This is the scripture library. Senior Brother, would you like to take a look inside?” Lan Ting led Lu Yang to a wooden building almost completely buried under snow, as if it could collapse under the weight at any moment.

This was the scripture library, which had stood firm for a hundred thousand years. It naturally wouldn’t be brought down by mere snow.

“Let’s go in to have a look.” As long as he wasn’t asked to write cultivation techniques, Lu Yang enjoyed wandering around places like the scripture library.

The layout of the immortal palace’s scripture library was largely similar to that of the Dao-Seeking Sect. The difference was in the collection of texts.

Most of the texts housed here were female-oriented cultivation techniques. Male-oriented ones were rare, and those that existed generally pertained to gathering luna power.

“What is this? Immortal Fairy’s Tribulation?” Lu Yang randomly pulled out an ancient text and flipped through a couple of pages, his expression turning peculiar.

The content of this book doesn’t seem improper. Is it really displayed so openly in the scripture library?

Our Dao-Seeking Sect was very secretive about the Dragon Phoenix Transformation.

And judging by the book’s condition, it appears to have been browsed quite frequently.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scanned it with her immortal consciousness, and her face instantly flushed. She stammered, unable to construct a sentence.

Finally, she managed to spit out a word furiously. “Vulgar!”

Lan Ting’s cheeks blushed slightly. She coughed twice to ease the awkwardness. “This is an ancient text brought back by Founding Ancestor Moonchaser a hundred thousand years ago. The stories within are highly instructive. The purpose of placing it here in the scripture library is to caution later generations, so that such fates do not befall them.”

Aside from Immortal Fairy’s Tribulation, Lu Yang noticed many other bizarre titles. He surmised they were all brought back by the Moonchaser True Person, their contents likely similar.

Many spots where books should have been were empty, presumably borrowed by the immortal palace disciples.

Regardless, the Moonchaser True Person’s various actions had indeed heightened the disciples’ vigilance, preserving their chastity. Lu Yang had never heard of any immortal palace disciple descending the mountain and hooking up with some random man.

“There are so many ancient texts here,” Lu Yang commented with a smile. He was most familiar with ancient texts, more so than with sword techniques.

“The immortal palace didn’t use to have so many ancient texts. It was due to recent demand that we purchased many from the Taixue Imperial Academy.”

“Demand?”

“Mmm. Senior Brother, you should know that the ancient Heaven Mandate Immortal created the Mother-Child River, right?”

Lu Yang’s expression grew odd. Should I say that I know or that I don’t know?

“Some immortal palace disciples aren’t interested in romantic love, yet they desire a child. Previously, there was no way. Now that they’ve learned of the Mother-Child River’s existence, they’ve begun devising all kinds of methods to locate it. Searching for clues in ancient texts is one such method.”

“Have they found anything?” Lu Yang inquired on behalf of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

Lan Ting shook her head regretfully. “Not a single thing. Senior Brother, you’re well-versed in ancient knowledge. Do you know where the Mother-Child River might be?”

“I have no idea.”

Suddenly, Lu Yang remembered something. Although I don’t know where the Mother-Child River is, I know where the Twins River is—right atop Heaven’s Gate Peak.

“Hmm? So they need the Twins River? Why not just move it over for them?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suggested magnanimously. Since it’s just sitting unused on Heaven’s Gate Peak without anyone drinking from it, we might as well give it to somewhere like the immortal palace that needs it.

Lu Yang contemplated seriously. It does seem possible to gift the Twins River to the immortal palace; this won’t expose anything either.

“Actually, although I don’t know where the Mother-Child River is, I do know the location of the Twins River.”

“Twins River?” Lan Ting had never heard of it.

Lu Yang pondered over how he should explain. The Twins River’s origins were somewhat complicated. “The Twins River, like the Mother-Child River, was created by the Heaven Mandate Immortal. The difference is that a woman drinking from the Mother-Child River can only bear one child, while drinking from the Twins River can produce twins.

“The exceedingly rare Twin Lotus Flower growing from a single stalk is a product of the Twins River.”

Lan Ting hadn’t imagined such an immortal item existed. The abilities of immortals are truly mysterious and inscrutable.

But why did the Heaven Mandate Immortal create the Twins River?

“And where is this Twins River?” she asked.

“It was recently discovered in an ancient secret domain. It’s currently at our Dao-Seeking Sect. If your immortal palace requires it, I could request some river water from our sect.”

Lan Ting’s face lit up with joy at this unexpected gain. If the immortal palace obtains water from the Twins River, who knows how many senior sisters and elders might bear children?

“Then I’ll thank you in advance, Senior Brother. May I report this matter to my shifu?” The matter of the Twins River was of great significance; Lan Ting couldn’t handle it alone.

“Of course, you can.”

~~~

Upon learning of the wondrous Twins River, Luo Hongxia was equally overjoyed. Our immortal palace needs something like this the most.

The way she looked at Lu Yang changed entirely. Everything about him seemed pleasing to the eye now.

“Lu Yang, if our immortal palace disciples become pregnant, you’ll be the greatest contributor!”

“...” Lu Yang. Why does that sound so strange?

Chapter 937: The Mysterious Bai Ye

“Our immortal palace cannot accept benefits without offering something in return. Lu Yang, tell me, what does your Dao-Seeking Sect need?!” Luo Hongxia asked. Right now, she felt that Lu Yang was the best kid under heaven.

If the Twins River really proves effective, it could make up for the regrets of many in the immortal palace.

Even if Lu Yang wants Lan Ting, I would consent right away.

“Uh, perhaps you would like to ask my Big Senior Sister?” Lu Yang had no idea what the Dao-Seeking Sect needed. This was something only Yun Zhi would know.

“Right, right, right. I was being foolish.” Luo Hongxia quickly realized her oversight. Although Lu Yang is world-famous, he is not yet a decision-maker for the Dao-Seeking Sect. This matter should be discussed with Yun Zhi.

Luo Hongxia calmed down. This matter is of great significance; it mustn’t be rushed. To exchange for such an immortal item from the Dao-Seeking Sect, I have to carefully take stock of what our immortal palace possesses that is of equal value.

As the palace leader, Luo Hongxia had far more considerations than the average person. Until the Twins River’s efficacy could be verified, she had to keep the matter under wraps, lest it raise false hopes.

After seeing Lu Yang off, Luo Hongxia paced within her cave abode, hands clasped behind her back. It had been a long time since she experienced such fluctuations in her emotions.

The last time she experienced such emotional fluctuations was when she learned of Lan Ting’s interest in Lu Yang.

“To ascertain the Twins River’s efficacy, we must find someone to test it. It would be best to choose someone with higher cultivation so that if something happens, they can still be saved.”

Suddenly, Luo Hongxia thought of someone. Leaving her cave abode, she quietly made her way to the artifact refinement chamber to find the Third Elder, Zhu Hong.

Zhu Hong was a beauty with bronze skin. She was from a branch of the Barbarian Tribe and disliked elaborate formalities. While forging artifacts, she often wore only a few strips of cloth to cover the key areas.

With her hammer paused mid-air, she asked in confusion, “Senior Sister, why did you come in such a hurry? Do you urgently require me to forge some magical treasure?”

“Old Three, haven’t you always wanted a child? I can make you pregnant. Would you like to come with me to the Dao-Seeking Sect to give it a try?”

Zhu Hong’s mouth fell open, and she stood frozen in place. At some point, the hammer slipped from her grasp, crashing to the ground and creating a sizable pit.

Senior Sister, do you want to hear what you’re saying?

~~~

Heaven’s Gate Peak welcomed visitors from the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

“Palace Leader Luo, so you’re hoping to taste the water of the Twins River?” Yun Zhi asked.

Initially, when she learned that Luo Hongxia intended to pay her a visit, she found it strange. Little Junior Brother has only been at the immortal palace for two days. Could he have stirred up so much trouble that Luo Hongxia is demanding that I bring him back?

This troublemaking speed is a bit too fast; it’s breaking records.

Only after Luo Hongxia explained her purpose did Yun Zhi understand the situation.

So it’s because of the Twins River.

“Is that possible?” Luo Hongxia inquired.

“Of course, it is,” Yun Zhi replied.

Since Little Junior Brother could divulge information about the Twins River to Luo Hongxia, it implies that this matter has the Immortal Fairy’s approval. The Twins River belongs to the Immortal Fairy. She is free to do as she pleases with it.

Luo Hongxia and Elder Zhu Hong exchanged a glance, both elated.

“It is possible, but we are still figuring out how the Twins River water should be consumed and if there are any contraindications. I ask that you give us some time. Once we have worked it out, we will invite Elder Zhu Hong to partake.”

Yun Zhi genuinely did not know how the Twins River water should be consumed, what quantity was appropriate, or what contraindications existed. These were known only to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Only when Lu Yang returned with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could they seek clarification.

However, Yun Zhi couldn’t mention such matters openly, lest she inadvertently reveal the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence or risk others misunderstanding that the Heaven Mandate Immortal resided within Lu Yang.

“I see.” Luo Hongxia and Elder Zhu Hong couldn’t help but show traces of disappointment.

Yun Zhi could only add. “Although the method of consumption remains unclear, please rest assured that the Twins River can certainly induce pregnancy. This I can guarantee.”

Even though there was no evidence, Yun Zhi’s assurance seemed to carry a mystical power that compelled one to believe her. The two women’s spirits were visibly lifted.

It’s just waiting for a few days. As two Fusion cultivators, we don’t lack time.

Watching their retreating figures, Yun Zhi couldn’t shake the feeling that Luo Hongxia and Zhu Hong resembled a long-time infertile couple, while she played the role of an old physician capable of miraculous cures.

If Elder Zhu Hong does become pregnant, her presenting me with a brocade banner that reads “Miraculous Cure” wouldn’t seem entirely out of place.

Yun Zhi shook her head, tossing out these peculiar thoughts. She felt that frequent contact with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was causing her own thinking to become peculiar.

After the two departed, Yun Mengmeng stealthily emerged and pounced onto Yun Zhi.

“There’s such a fun thing as the Twins River?” Yun Mengmeng’s eyes sparkled with curiosity about the Twins River.

It inevitably reminded her of the Mother-Child River in her hometown. freewebnovel.com

Yun Zhi shot Yun Mengmeng a sidelong glance. She pried the arms wrapped around her neck loose and warned, “You are not allowed to research anything regarding the Twins River.”

Yun Mengmeng stuck out her tongue in defiance.

~~~

Lan Ting increasingly felt that Lu Yang was truly amazing. He has just arrived at the immortal palace, yet he has already resolved a problem that has plagued us for a hundred thousand years.

If I get together with Lu Yang, I’m sure Shifu won’t oppose it; in fact, she’ll even offer us her blessings.

When night fell, Lan Ting bid Lu Yang goodbye and went to cultivate. Bai Ye came looking for Lu Yang again, carrying a small stool in her hand.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, I’ve come to hear more stories.”

Lu Yang chuckled. “Skipping cultivation again to sneak out? Where did we leave off yesterday?”

“We were at the part where the three of you infiltrated the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters and reported its location, prompting the Dao-Seeking Sect and the imperial court to join forces to wipe out the Everlasting Creed.” Bai Ye sat on her small stool, her eyes gleaming with anticipation for more stories.

The two sat beneath the moon laurel tree in the courtyard, one narrating and one listening. Just like that, another night passed.

Before parting, they agreed to meet again tomorrow, and Bai Ye cheerfully handed Lu Yang a paper bag.

At Bai Ye’s gesture, Lu Yang opened the bag and discovered it contained numerous petals. “What are these?”

“These are moon laurel petals. They’re delicious. Senior Brother Lu Yang, you can snack on them when you have nothing to do.”

Moon laurel trees have petals? This was news to Lu Yang.

He pinched one and placed it in his mouth. The sweet fragrance of osmanthus blossomed on his tongue, intertwined with a tinge of spirit qi that transformed directly into his own spirit energy without any need for refinement.

“No wonder you dare sneak out and skip cultivation.” Eating moon laurel petals counts as cultivation. That’s so convenient.

Seeing that Lu Yang enjoyed them, Bai Ye grinned widely. “I don’t have many moon laurel petals myself, but if you like them, I’ll set some aside for you next time, Senior Brother.”

“It’s settled then.”

Lu Yang had never eaten moon laurel petals before and didn’t expect them to be so delectable. The more he ate, the more addictive they became.

Judging by Bai Ye’s tone, these shouldn’t be anything precious. If they’re too valuable, I would feel embarrassed to accept them.

Within the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had sculpted a throne from snow. Seated upon it, she stared intently at Bai Ye’s figure, murmuring to herself.

“Is this lass a tree? Somehow, it doesn’t feel like it.

“Silly Xiao Yangzi can’t tell a thing. I suppose this is what they mean by ‘fortune favors fools.’”

Chapter 938: Sinner Hall

Having observed Bai Ye for two nights now, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could say with certainty that she was related to the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor. She surmised that Bai Ye was probably some manifestation of the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor’s consciousness or something similar.

As a tree that was suspected to have been planted by the Heaven Mandate Immortal, four hundred thousand years was enough time for it to develop spirit intelligence. For example, before the Epoch Immortal became an immortal, he often split off a clone to act on his behalf. The principle was roughly the same.

But Bai Ye is definitely more than just the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor. However, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had yet to work out the full picture.

“Xiao Yangzi isn’t clever enough. He still needs me to worry about him.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head happily. Lu Yang truly can’t do without me as his strategist.

“But then again, this little lass means no harm to Xiao Yangzi, so it’s nothing for me to worry about. Should I even bother figuring out what’s going on with Bai Ye?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy leaned back on her ice-carved throne and ruminated for a moment, but soon drifted into sleep, exhausted from the mental strain.

~~~

Lu Yang felt that he had toured most of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, but he couldn’t shake the feeling that one place had been missed, leaving his heart feeling empty.

“By the way, Junior Sister Lan, do you have a place similar to Incarceration Peak here?”

It dawned on him. I haven’t visited the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace’s equivalent of Incarceration Peak yet.

“Ah? Senior Brother, you want to visit Sinner Hall?”

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace wielded enforcement authority, so naturally, it had a facility akin to Incarceration Peak. It was called Sinner Hall.

Lan Ting hadn’t expected Lu Yang to be so interested in Sinner Hall. She had deliberately avoided taking him there, thinking it was unsuitable for him.

“I want to broaden my horizons,” Lu Yang said with a chuckle. He was curious to see what other immortal sects’ “Incarceration Peak" looked like.

Sinner Hall wasn’t a restricted area; immortal palace disciples could enter and exit freely.

Lan Ting led Lu Yang to a relatively low-rise palace hall, so small that it hardly seemed like a place for detaining prisoners.

As they entered, candles lining the walls sensed their presence and flared to life with a whoosh, illuminating the passage ahead.

“The prisoners are all down below,” Lan Ting said, pointing at the passage leading underground.

The passageway was silent, with only the echoes of their footsteps. As they walked, candles on either side of the underground passage ignited in response.

Noticing Lu Yang’s interest in the candles, Lan Ting explained with a smile, “You see, the candles in Sinner Hall used to burn constantly. I thought it was rather wasteful, so I designed an array. Normally, the candles are extinguished, but when they detect sound, the array activates and lights them. It’s very convenient.

“I even received a thousand contribution points for helping the sect save on candles.”

“It’s indeed an excellent design.” Lu Yang nodded. He hadn’t expected the array to be Lan Ting’s creation. I should have realized she has a talent for such things.

After all, she was the one who first proposed the concept of an automatic skewering array.

“Have you applied for a patent?”

“No, it seems rather troublesome.” Unlike the Dao-Seeking Sect with its established patent application process, the semi-reclusive Moon Laurel Immortal Palace had no interest in patents.

Lu Yang advised, “It’s best to apply for one. If I’ve calculated the timing correctly, solar lamps should be appearing now as replacements for candles. Voice-controlled solar lamps probably haven’t emerged yet. If you secure the patent for this array, you can likely earn a considerable amount of spirit stones.”

“Senior Brother, are you referring to the solar lamps promoted by the Solar Energy Technology Development Merchant Guild?” Lan Ting had heard a little about this up-and-coming merchant guild while out on a mission recently. They often advertised through Dreamlike Bubble Mirages.

“They’ve got the production line sorted? It seems they move quite quickly,” Lu Yang mumbled to himself, then said, “Yes, those solar lamps. Emerging industries offer many business opportunities; you can seize this chance to profit. Though we cultivators shouldn’t let spirit stones cloud our minds, our cultivation still has to rely on them. With a patent in hand, spirit stones will flow in continuously, making future cultivation much easier.”

“Alright.” Although Lan Ting’s attitude toward patents was different, since Lu Yang suggested it, she would certainly go along with it.

Junior Sister Tao, you don’t get to enjoy such treatment, do you?

As they conversed, they reached the end of the passage and encountered a gatekeeper draped in black robes.

The gatekeeper kept her head lowered, scribbling something.

“This is Elder Mo Ran.”

“Junior Lu Yang pays respects to Elder Mo Ran.” Lu Yang greeted her with a bow.

Seeing someone approach, Elder Mo Ran hastily covered what she was writing. “So it’s the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s little disciple. What offense did you commit to land yourself here?”

“Ah?”

Noticing Lu Yang’s bewilderment, Elder Mo Ran grew puzzled. “Aren’t you following your shifu’s example, getting caught for committing some offense in the outside world and sent to our immortal palace?”

Lan Ting hurriedly explained that Lu Yang was visiting the immortal palace, unlike the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“It was my mistake. I thought it was some master-disciple tradition.” Bound by her duty, Elder Mo Ran rarely left Sinner Hall and was hardly aware of recent developments.

“Has my shifu visited Sinner Hall before?” Lu Yang asked cautiously. Shifu is even more well-traveled than I’d thought. He has even been to such a remote place as the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

Elder Mo Ran snorted coldly. “Which immortal sect’s Sinner Hall hasn’t he visited?

“If you wish to look around inside, have Junior Niece Lan take you. It’s not her first time here, and she’s quite familiar with the place. I won’t go in.” Elder Mo Ran disliked chatting and moving about. The quiet environment of Sinner Hall suited her best.

Watching their retreating figures, Elder Mo Ran’s gaze turned cold. “They probably didn’t see what I was writing. If they did, they cannot be allowed to leave!”

Elder Mo Ran lowered her head and continued writing: The Morning Light Divine Lord wrapped his arm around Chu Xian’er’s slender waist. Facing the besiegement of countless gods and Buddhas, he stood unwavering, as steadfast as a statue...

~~~

With Elder Mo Ran’s token in hand, they passed through the great array and entered the true Sinner Hall.

“Our Sinner Hall serves the same purpose as your Incarceration Peak. It detains criminals apprehended during external missions. The prisoners here range from the Foundation Establishment Stage to the Fusion Stage.”

Speaking of Fusion criminals in Sinner Hall, Lan Ting couldn’t hide a hint of pride. The highest cultivation among immortal palace disciples was the Fusion Stage. The difficulty of capturing a Fusion criminal alive during a mission was unimaginable.

Just like the recently captured Heartless Creed elder, if not for Lu Yang, Man Gu, and herself working together, capturing him alive would have been nearly impossible.

Lu Yang pondered. It seems the lowest cultivation among prisoners in our Incarceration Peak is the Fusion Stage, and the one with the highest cultivation is Guan Shanhai.

Dao-Seeking Sect disciples also captured criminals when out on missions, but those below the Fusion Stage were sent directly to local authorities. There was no need to bring them back to Incarceration Peak.

Prison cells in Incarceration Peak were limited and had to be used sparingly.

Lu Yang noticed that each prisoner’s name, crime, and remaining sentence were inscribed before their cell. The shortest term was for theft, with the prisoner to be released in a few days.

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace did not segregate prisoners by gender; otherwise, the Taciturn Daoist Priest wouldn’t have gotten in.

Incarceration Peak had similar plaques bearing the prisoners’ names and crimes. The only difference was that no sentence length was recorded.

The prisoners in Incarceration Peak were either murderers or would-be rebels. What remaining sentence could they have? They had to obediently spend the rest of their lives locked up in there.

Chapter 939: Unexpected Acquaintances

Lu Yang scanned the prisoners’ crimes in Sinner Hall one by one. Soon, a particular crime caught his attention. “Attempted body takeover?”

This was a rather uncommon offense. Typically, body takeover was a completed crime. After all, when a high-level cultivator attempted to take over the body of a low-level cultivator, the latter had no power to resist. How could it fail?

Lu Yang noted that the prisoner charged with attempted body takeover was at the Advanced Divine Transfiguration Stage, which wasn’t low.

Lan Ting explained, “This person was simply unlucky. He tried to take over the body of a cultivator named Kong Hao.”

A strange expression crept onto Lu Yang’s face. Of course, he knew Kong Hao. During the Dao-Seeking Sect’s 120,000th anniversary celebration, he had exchanged blows with Kong Hao under the identity of Young Creed Leader Lu.

I had also reported Kong Hao for borrowing the power of the ferocious beast within him during the match...

“Kong Hao’s cultivation was supposed to be inferior to his, so no accidents should have occurred. But to his surprise, Kong Hao’s mental space was inhabited by two Transcendent Tribulation taowu.”

“Two?” Lu Yang was befuddled. I remember Kong Hao having only one taowu. Did that taowu become pregnant?

That’s not right either. The other couldn’t possibly have been born at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

“Mmm. With two Transcendent Tribulation taowu residing within Kong Hao, the body takeover naturally failed.”

Lu Yang noticed that the adjacent cell also detained someone for attempted body takeover. “What about this one?”

“This person attempted to take over the body of a fellow Daoist named Long Huo. There was a gap in their cultivation realms, so the attempt should have succeeded. According to this prisoner, just as the body takeover was about to succeed, Long Huo began shouting incomprehensible phrases like ‘I cannot lose’ and broke through on the spot. This triggered a spike in his mental power, causing the prisoner’s body takeover attempt to fail.

“A senior sister happened to pass by and brought the prisoner back. According to his confession, he had prepared numerous natural treasures to nourish his new body after his body takeover plan succeeded. These would have been classified as stolen goods to corroborate his crime. Strangely, when that senior sister went to the location as indicated by the prisoner to retrieve the booty, she found nothing. It remains unknown as to who took them.”

Lu Yang also had some recollection of Long Huo. During the Dao-Seeking Sect’s 120,000th anniversary celebration, Long Huo was Meng Jingzhou’s opponent and was beaten so badly by him that he saw his life flash before his eyes.

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, I never expected us to meet here,” a prisoner in one of the cells called out to Lu Yang.

“Xue Shilou, what are you doing here?” Lu Yang exclaimed, not expecting to encounter an acquaintance in Sinner Hall.

Xue Shilou hailed from the Extreme North and was rumored to possess some Snow Emperor Bloodline. After being defeated by Lu Yang, he had let his second personality take over, then fused his first and second personalities, rising again several times.

Lu Yang glanced at the crime pasted on his cell door—Crime of Illegal Crossing.

There’s no need to ask. He had obviously come to Great Xia without going through the proper exit and entry procedures.

Thinking about it, it makes sense. The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace is located at the northernmost edge of Great Xia; further north lies the Extreme North. Illegal border crossings would be common. Before encountering Xue Shilou, Lu Yang had already seen several prisoners charged with the same crime.

Aside from them, there were also those locked up for stealing moon laurel trees.

Xue Shilou spoke indignantly, regretting his actions from back then. “I never imagined the security levels at Great Xia’s various checkpoints would differ so greatly. I was careless!”

The Great Xia’s northern border was long; the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace couldn’t possibly cover every inch.

Presumably, when Xue Shilou entered Great Xia, he had passed through an area not under the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace’s jurisdiction. But when he tried to leave, he happened to step right into their territory.

Cultivators from the Extreme North were always solitary, seldom mingling with others. News traveled slowly there, so naturally, no one had informed Xue Shilou that entering and exiting Great Xia required proper procedures.

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, and me too,” the occupant of the adjacent cell called out.

Lu Yang turned his head and stared blankly for two seconds, but he still failed to recall their identity. “Who are you?”

“I’m Xuanyuan Tianhen!”

Lu Yang mulled over it carefully. I would surely remember if I’d heard such a distinctive name before. This means I really don’t know him.

To avoid awkwardness, Lu Yang specifically asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “Immortal Fairy, do you know them?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pondered seriously for a while. “That name sounds like something the Heaven Mandate Immortal would come up with.”

Lu Yang confirmed that he indeed didn’t know this person.

“I’m Xue Shilou’s senior brother! We participated in the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony together!” Xuanyuan Tianhen hastily added.

This time, Lu Yang finally had a faint recollection. When I was sparring with Xue Shilou, someone did claim to be his senior brother and kept shouting from below the platform, yelling things like “Junior Xue has fainted, this is terrible!” and “His combat power will skyrocket!”

Realization dawned upon Lu Yang. It seems both senior and junior brothers have been caught for illegal border crossing. Good for them—they have company.

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, since you’re an immortal sect disciple, could you put in a word with the immortal palace and have us senior and junior brothers released? We guarantee we won’t commit the same crime again!”Xuanyuan Tianhen implored.

Seeing Lu Yang’s hesitant expression, Xuanyuan Tianhen quickly added, “Rest assured, Fellow Daoist Lu Yang! If we two can leave the immortal palace, we will surely present you with generous gifts!”

Hearing this, Lu Yang finally made up his mind. Turning to Lan Ting, he said, “You heard that, right? They’re trying to bribe their way out. Your immortal palace should increase their punishments accordingly.”

Originally, he had been contemplating whether Xuanyuan Tianhen’s actions constituted bribery. Now he was certain. It’s definitely bribery.

“Rest assured, Senior Brother. Our immortal palace always acts fairly.”

As they spoke, Xue Shilou suddenly became feverish all over, rolling on the ground repeatedly. Lu Yang was startled and wanted to go over to help, but Lan Ting held him back.

“This is his bloodline gradually awakening. Don’t disturb him.”

Watching Xue Shilou writhing on the ground in pain, Lan Ting sighed and explained the situation. “Less than half a day after Xue Shilou was imprisoned here, he suddenly fell unconscious and wouldn’t wake. He vomited blood from time to time and grew terribly weak, looking like he could die at any moment. Elder Mo Ran thought he was trying to swindle our immortal palace.

“To be safe, Elder Mo Ran invited Elder Zhou Yulu, who excels in medical skills, to examine him. The inspection revealed that he possessed the Snow Emperor Bloodline, but he was too frail to withstand its gradual awakening. If he were to be left untreated, he would surely die.
