“Our immortal palace’s Sinner Hall is a proper official prison, not some private dungeon. If someone were to die inside, it would reflect poorly on us and easily lead to misunderstandings. We had no choice but to suppress the gradually awakening Snow Emperor Bloodline while tempering his body, allowing the bloodline to awaken step by step.”

The thought of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace wasting natural treasures to help Xue Shilou awaken his bloodline made Lan Ting’s heart ache.

“His current state is a normal reaction to the bloodline awakening. There’s no need to intervene. He’ll be fine after shouting a few times.”

Lu Yang’s eyelid twitched. Compared to our Incarceration Peak, Sinner Hall seems far more legitimate.

Our Incarceration Peak either subjects prisoners to torture or refines their bodies and souls. freewebnovel.com

Help with healing their wounds and treating their illnesses? Nothing of the sort.

Chapter 940: The Pill Concoction Chamber’s New Product

Just as Lu Yang was pondering what fortuitous encounters a Fusion cultivator might stumble upon, a cold, sinister voice sounded.

“Heh, since when has the immortal palace fallen so far that men can come and go as they please?”

Qu Ling: Crime of Corruption, Life Imprisonment.

The corners of Qu Ling’s mouth curled up into a mysterious smile.

Lu Yang figured it out. “I get it! It’s because you think this looks cool, right?”

Qu Ling continued smiling, uncertain what to do next.

Isn’t this the kind of scene that often appears in the books brought back by Founding Ancestor Moonchaser?

A mysterious figure is imprisoned and calls out to the protagonist, mocking or sneering at them, and uttering cryptic words no one can understand. The protagonist leaves with questions, and the mysterious figure shrouded in the darkness of their cell reveals an inscrutable smile.

But the books never explain why the mysterious figure had called out to the protagonist in the first place.

Crunch. Crunch. The sound was grating to the ear.

The demon rabbit appeared fierce, but was only at the Golden Core Stage. It didn't pose a threat at all.

Crunch, crunch, crunch.

To test medicinal properties, the immortal palace raised many demon beasts. Unlike the demon race, these demon beasts had no spirit intelligence, making them ideal for testing pills.

Hearing the commotion, the immortal palace disciples rushed over, concerned for Qin Nan.

“I suspect the ratios were not quite right, triggering the demon rabbit’s bloodline and causing it to grow larger and uncontrollable.”

“What did you feed it?”

“A derivative of the Beautifying Pill—the Beautifying Mooncake. It has osmanthus filling.” Qin Nan took out a mooncake from the front of her robes. It was printed with “Moon Laurel Immortal Palace” on the front, and the back was printed with “beautifying.”

Lan Ting murmured a soft affirmative. “The Mid-Autumn Festival is approaching. Our immortal palace has a tradition of making mooncakes every year. New innovations emerge from the pill concoction chamber, which attempts to combine pills and mooncakes.

“Judging by the current situation, the research isn't going smoothly.”

The Mid-Autumn Festival was a tradition passed down from ancient times, when the moon waxed and waned. The full moon on the fifteenth day of the eighth month marked the festival.

Ever since the Nine-Layers Immortal created the sun-moon entity, there was no longer any “waxing and waning” of the moon; every night was a full moon. Nevertheless, the custom endured.

The Dao-Seeking Sect didn’t really celebrate the Mid-Autumn Festival. It was presumably due to the moon’s special significance for the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace that they treated the Mid-Autumn Festival seriously.

“What do we do with this rabbit?” Lu Yang asked. The rabbit appeared to be six meters long and wouldn’t stay still, twisting and turning on the ground.

“Let’s dissect it and find out what caused it to lose control,” one of the immortal palace disciples suggested loudly.

“Look, this rabbit’s eyes are all red; it’s definitely gone berserk. There’s no saving it.”

“But aren’t rabbits’ eyes naturally red?” a young disciple asked, puzzled.

“Shut up. Do you want to eat rabbit meat or not?”

The young disciple felt conflicted. Telling the truth may save the rabbit, but I won’t get to eat any delicious rabbit. Lying won’t save the rabbit, but I will get to eat a delicious rabbit. Is this the adult world—full of lies and choices?

She racked her brains, vacillating between ideals and reality. Finally, she settled on how to cook the rabbit.

“Let’s just roast it, then.”

Chapter 941: The Tree Ancestor’s Care

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace acted with caution. They wouldn’t eat the demon rabbit under the pretext of dissection.

At the very least, they had to ascertain whether the demon rabbit’s meat was poisonous before consuming it.

“Do you need a chef?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt it was time to showcase her skills. She volunteered enthusiastically, ready to demonstrate the culinary skills of an immortal.

Having the Everlasting Immortal Fairy cook was out of the question. Back in ancient times, when she tried to barbecue on the moon, the four immortals were poisoned unconscious, and she had to carry them home, leaving the immortal fire behind on the moon. The immortal palace disciples, being mere mortals, would certainly be unable to withstand such an immortal-grade poison.

Directly refusing wouldn’t do. With his meticulous mind and quick thinking, Lu Yang soon came up with an appropriate response. As the saying goes, it’s better to redirect than to resist. Rejecting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s proposal outright may trigger her rebellious nature. The best method is to find a chef who would satisfy her.

And this chef will have to be none other than myself.

“Your Exalted Majesty is noble like golden branches and jade leaves. How could you do such things? Allow your concu—subject to handle it.” Lately, with time on his hands, Lu Yang had been reading novels from the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace’s scripture library, especially those about palace intrigue.[1] For a moment, his tongue betrayed him, and he nearly misspoke.

Lan Ting had witnessed Lu Yang’s culinary skills back in Yanjiang Commandery. There’s no doubt about it; the taste was superb.

Now that Lu Yang has advanced to the Divine Transfiguration Stage, his control over heat and the meat quality must have reached the “subtlety” realm. The flavor would definitely be even better than before.

And it has also been a long time since I’ve had Lu Yang’s barbeque.

“I’ll speak with the senior sister in charge of cooking.”

~~~

“It’s more or less something along those lines.”

“That’s good then.” Lu Yang was worried that his actions could have displeased the head cook.

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace was remarkably efficient. In the time it took to wash the pots, they had already figured out why the demon rabbit had suddenly grown so large.

“It’s the reaction between the Beautifying Pill and the osmanthus flowers,” Qin Nan concluded. “Beautifying pills inherently have an enlarging effect. For some reason, the freshly picked osmanthus flowers also possessed this property. The combination of these two factors caused a sharp increase in the demon rabbit’s size.”

“And also caused the demon rabbit to go berserk,” a junior female disciple added. This was a crucial point.

“Ah, right, and it also caused the demon rabbit to go berserk.”

“But the good news is that the demon rabbit has fully metabolized the medicinal properties. It’s edible, non-toxic, and harmless, with healthy meat quality."

It is good news that the demon rabbit is edible; it means I can showcase my skills. But Lu Yang still had one question. “Why do Beautifying Pills have an enlarging effect?” freewebnovel.com

Don’t female cultivators consume Beautifying Pills to make themselves more attractive?

Asking such a question revealed that Lu Yang was an outsider in the field. All Moon Laurel Immortal Palace disciples knew the answer.

Qin Nan explained, “It’s like this. Female cultivators commonly consume two types of pills. Youth-Preservation Pill locks in one’s appearance, while Beautifying Pills alter it.

“Altering appearances generally falls into two categories: enlarging or reducing.

“Some female cultivators are talented and able to cultivate rapidly, reaching the Youth-Preservation realm while still young, after which their appearance no longer changes.

Lu Yang was enlightened. This is a domain I’ve never ventured into; there are indeed many intricacies.

As the number one of the Top Ten Ancient Beauties, I’m qualified to say such things.

Although I may not have use for this knowledge, learning a bit more can’t hurt.

“By the way, have you ever tried using moon laurel wood as fuel for barbecue?” Lu Yang asked while grinding the marinade ingredients. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s barbecue method does have its merits.

“Use moon laurel trees as firewood?” Lan Ting was stunned. This was something she had never considered.

“Wait a moment. I’ll go ask the Tree Ancestor. If it agrees, then it’s fine.”

“The Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor has consciousness?” Lu Yang was astonished. He had assumed the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor was simply tall.

Noticing Lu Yang’s interest, Lan Ting led him deep into the moon laurel grove once again, where they saw the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor that reached the sky.

Lan Ting bowed three times to the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor and performed an entire complex ritual before respectfully asking, “Your disciple wishes to fell a moon laurel tree for firewood. I humbly seek your consent, Tree Ancestor.”

Rustle, rustle, rustle. The massive branches swayed without any wind.

Lan Ting looked up excitedly. “The Tree Ancestor has agreed!”

Lu Yang hadn’t expected the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor to be so amicable. He also bowed three times to it.

Having obtained the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor’s approval, the two began searching for a suitable moon laurel tree. Since the tree needed to be felled with a single strike, choosing an overly thick one would inevitably lead to embarrassment, while an overly thin one wouldn’t provide enough firewood.

“This one should do.” Lu Yang patted a nearby moon laurel tree that was about an arm's span in girth.

“Isn’t it too thick?” Lan Ting doubted she could chop down such a thick moon laurel tree.

“We’ll find out when we try.” Lu Yang drew his Qingfeng Sword and tapped the moon laurel tree. He had never chopped one down before; this would be a novel experience.

Within the Qingfeng Sword, Ten Thousand Swords Return to One was activated. Lu Yang’s gaze sharpened as he unified his waist and stance, pushed off with his right foot, twisted his torso, channeled all his strength into the Qingfeng Sword, and bellowed, “Slash!”

Crack!

As the strike fell, the Qingfeng Sword embedded itself halfway into the trunk. It wasn’t severed. Lu Yang scratched his head. He had wanted to show off before Lan Ting, but his attempt had failed.

Just as he was about to say something to diffuse the awkwardness, Lan Ting pointed at the partially severed moon laurel tree in surprise. “The moon laurel tree isn’t healing!”

This has never happened before! Lu Yang swung his sword again.

Crack. Crash.

The moon laurel tree toppled down.

“Strange. Did I chop it too fast for the moon laurel tree to heal?” Lu Yang hoisted the tree onto his shoulder, puzzled.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rolled her eyes. Too fast for the tree to heal? It’s clearly the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor deliberately controlling this moon laurel tree, preventing it from healing.

“Takes quite good care of Xiao Yangzi, huh.”

Chapter 942: Rabbit May Be Good, but Don’t Eat Too Much

Barbecuing was a meticulous task. By the time all preparations were complete, and Lu Yang and Lan Ting had hauled the moon laurel tree back, it was already night.

Lu Yang weaved through the crowd with the moon laurel tree on his shoulder, like a triumphant great general returning from a campaign. He earned waves of exclamations and admiration.

“Why are they carrying a whole moon laurel tree back?”

“I heard it’s to be used as firewood.”

“Ah? Moon laurel trees can be used like that?”

“Probably. Since they could cut it down, it means the Tree Ancestor consented.”

Lu Yang split the moon laurel tree in the middle, then chopped it into smaller segments. He roasted them over a fire to dry out the moisture.

Next, he tossed these moon laurel trees into a large pit dug in advance, placed a grill over the pit, and laid the marinated demon rabbit upon it.

With a flick of his finger, Lu Yang sent a spark of Three Flavor True Fire into the pit, and the moon laurel wood segments burned instantly. Based on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s experience, moon laurel wood logs of this age would burn through the night, more than enough to roast the demon rabbit thoroughly.

As the moon laurel wood burned, it released an intoxicating fragrance that suffused the air. Everyone in the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace felt as though they had been transported back to the season when the moon laurel trees bloomed. freewebnovel.com

As one of the founders of One More Time Barbeque Shop, Lu Yang's barbecue skill needed no elaboration; it was unparalleled in the current age, with only Man Gu, who grasped Corpse-Driving Techniques, capable of contending with him. The competition was for the title of number one after the Everlasting Immortal Fairy!

Lu Yang enveloped every inch of the demon rabbit’s flesh with his spiritual consciousness, managing the Three Flavor True Fire with precise control. Every now and then, he would toss two chunks of moon laurel wood logs into the fire pit, causing it to crackle endlessly.

He continuously brushed oil onto the meat and turned it, letting the skin, flesh, sinew, and bones achieve a balance of flavor and texture. The faint scent of garlic and fresh kick of chilli permeated deep into the meat.

Even the Automatic Barbecue Array had its limitations. Such a massive demon rabbit far exceeded its capacity. At times like this, the value of an old hand like Lu Yang became all the more apparent.

Amidst the warmth radiating from the fire pit, mingled with the fragrance of osmanthus flowers and roasted meat, the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace disciples chatted merrily, their laughter unceasing.

Lan Ting sat beside Lu Yang, neither of them speaking. It was unclear how much time had passed before Lu Yang roused the sleepy Lan Ting.

“Junior Sister Lan, want to have a taste?”

Lan Ting opened her eyes and saw that the demon rabbit had been roasted to a golden brown. She tore off a piece of flesh and skin. The juices beneath the skin, seeming to have found an outlet, dripped and pattered onto the fire pit, sizzling and crackling.

Having been smoked by the moon laurel wood, the demon rabbit's gamey odor had been completely removed.

The outer layer was crispy and fragrant, providing a delightful crunch with each bite. The generous chunks of lean meat were chewy, their meaty flavor intensifying with every chew. The osmanthus flower fragrance tantalized her taste buds, and combined with Lu Yang's dipping sauce mixed with sesame oil, soybeans, and ground sesame seeds, the aroma jolted Lan Ting fully awake.

Lan Ting sucked her fingertips, looking like she hadn't had her fill.

Seeing Lan Ting’s expression, Lu Yang knew that the demon rabbit was perfectly done, even without her saying anything.

“Everyone, it’s ready to eat!

“The left side is not spicy, and the right side is spicy! The jars by the fire pit contain the dipping sauce!”

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace disciples had been waiting for this moment. Since everyone here was one of their own, there was no need to maintain the ethereal image of an immortal fairy like they did in the outside world. In a flurry, they crowded around to sample the demon rabbit they had long coveted.

The cultivation world’s principle of “the strong reigns supreme” was vividly demonstrated at this moment. Those with higher cultivation charged to the front, while those with lower cultivation could only queue behind.

“So delicious!”

“I’ve never eaten such tasty barbeque!”

“I’ve visited the headquarters of One More Time Barbeque Shop, and even their barbeque isn’t as good as Senior Brother Lu Yang’s!”

Even the senior female disciple serving as head chef, with her discerning palate, had to admit that Lu Yang’s barbecue skills surpassed her own, perhaps by a wide margin.

I’ve lost. Completely and utterly.

When ordinary people barbecue, roasting such a massive ingredient would inevitably leave the exterior charred while the inside remained uncooked. Yet under Lu Yang’s control, tendrils of Three Flavor True Fire had penetrated every inch of the demon rabbit, searing the meat to perfection.

Even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy heaped praise upon Lu Yang’s barbeque demon rabbit. “Xiao Yangzi does have some skill. He made the Three Flavor True Fire burrow into the demon rabbit’s body like maggots clinging to bones, roasting even the bones to a fragrant crispness. He has already learned three-tenths of my ability.”

Although it was meant as praise, Lu Yang couldn’t shake the feeling that something about her words was off.

No one noticed the petite Bai Ye weaving through the crowd, tearing off a piece of rabbit meat before stealthily slipping away. She sat upon a branch of the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor, eating with satisfaction until her whole mouth was greasy.

“Hmm? Barbecuing with our moon laurel tree makes it this fragrant?”

~~~

This night, not a single Moon Laurel Immortal Palace disciple cultivated; they ate to their hearts’ content. Anyone witnessing this scene would never associate these reveling disciples with the image of ethereal, otherworldly immortal fairies displayed to the outside world.

Lu Yang was also elated. As a chef, nothing pleased him more than diners praising the food. In fact, he didn’t need their praise. Watching the junior female disciples contentedly suck on the bones, he confirmed that his barbecue was a success this time.

“So sleepy...” Lu Yang let out a huge yawn. He also felt like slacking off today, not cultivating and heading straight to sleep.

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace Disciples also yawned endlessly. Shedding all concerns for appearances, they simply lay down and slept. At their cultivation levels, even falling snow wouldn’t freeze them; they could sleep anywhere.

If someone were to look down from the sky, they would see an enormous pit at the center of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, surrounded by countless sleeping disciples.

~~~

The moon ignited, turning into the sun. Lu Yang felt the morning light on his face and struggled to open his eyes. He hadn’t slept so comfortably in a long time.

“Who covered me with a blanket?”

Lu Yang felt like a blanket was weighing on him. He wondered which kind soul had done this.

Was it Junior Sister Lan?

Lu Yang groggily opened his eyes, laboriously crawled out from under the blanket, and looked at the senior and junior disciples filling the entire place. His mind still felt somewhat foggy.

“Why do I keep feeling like something is off?” Lu Yang mumbled to himself.

Suddenly, realization dawned upon him.

“Why am I naked?!”

Lu Yang raised his hand, his pupils constricting sharply. “No...I have shrunk!”

This isn’t a blanket at all; it’s clearly my own clothing. It’s just that after I’ve shrunk, my clothes have become as loose as a blanket.

Lu Yang snapped fully awake and gazed at Lan Ting sleeping beside him. In her place, a little girl of about eight to nine years old had taken Lan Ting’s place.

Lan Ting has shrunk too!

Lu Yang surveyed their surroundings. It isn’t just Lan Ting; everyone present has shrunk.

Meanwhile, Luo Hongxia and Elder Zhu returned from the Dao-Seeking Sect. Luo Hongxia kindly counseled Elder Zhu Hong.

“Junior Sister, don’t be disappointed. Didn’t Yun Zhi say she would let you consume the water of the Twins River once the research is completed?

“You’ve wanted children for more than just a day or two. Surely you won’t mind waiting a little longer?"

Elder Zhu Hong nodded perfunctorily, saying nothing.

Seeing that, Luo Hongxia knew that all her persuasion had been in vain.

When the two alighted and landed, they saw Lu Yang standing in the cold wind with his buttocks bare, surrounded by little girls all over the place.

Eyes wide; mouth agape.

Chapter 943: You Have Really Become Xiao Yangzi

Luo Hongxia and Elder Zhu Hong stood frozen, utterly at a loss.

Elder Zhu Hong admitted she did like children, but she had never imagined the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace would one day be filled with so many of them.

“Did someone cast a time-reversal spell, sending the immortal palace back to the past?"

“No, that’s not right either. Even going back in time wouldn’t result in this.”

The disciples range widely in age, yet all of them have taken on the appearance of children. This can’t be explained by time reversal.

What exactly happened?

Weren’t we only gone for three days? How did the immortal palace become so unrecognizable?

“You...you’re Lu Yang, right?” Luo Hongxia asked hesitantly. Even with his miniature size, one could still discern his original features.

“Not now,” Lu Yang firmly denied, then hastily retrieved his clothes from the ground and wrapped himself up.

“Now I am Lu Yang.”

That person standing with his buttocks bare in the snow a moment ago has nothing to do with me.

“What happened here?”

“I have no idea either! We just ate a roasted rabbit, slept, and woke up like this.” Lu Yang was innocent and just as flummoxed. Why have I suddenly turned into a child for no reason?

“Immortal Fairy, stop sleeping! Wake up!” Lu Yang shook the Everlasting Immortal Fairy awake from her snow bed, where she lay with her fingers crossed over her chest.

When the Everlasting Immortal Fairy slept, she was exceedingly beautiful, so much so that Lu Yang could momentarily forget all her antics and acknowledge her as the foremost of the Ten Ancient Beauties.

But now is not the time to admire her beauty!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy slept even more soundly than Lu Yang was reluctant to wake up.

Upon rousing from her dreams, she caught sight of the childlike Lu Yang and instantly perked up.

“Ah! How did you become so small?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shot upright in bed and repeatedly gestured, comparing Lu Yang’s height to hers. He now only reached her waist.

“You’ve really become Xiao Yangzi.”[1]

“Isn’t that why I came to ask you for a diagnosis?” Lu Yang implored her to help.

“Aiya, it’s pretty nice having you this small.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy giggled as she crouched down and patted Lu Yang’s head, showing no inclination whatsoever to take charge of matters.

~~~

Outside, the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace disciples woke up one after another. Shrill cries pierced the air in succession, but their voices were so childish that it sounded like babies bawling. Lu Yang wondered if he had stumbled into some kindergarten, where he was the little grown-up, neither crying nor fussing.

Luo Hongxia and Zhu Hong had barely finished consoling one child before they had to turn and pacify another. They weren’t physically tired, but mentally exhausted.

Elder Zhu Hong began to feel that perhaps she didn’t need the Twins River’s water that much after all.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, we...” Lan Ting bashfully wrapped herself in her clothes, covering even her head, leaving only half her face exposed.

Lu Yang pressed his hand to his forehead. Junior Sister Lan, don’t look at me like that. You’re making it seem as though something happened between us last night.

In our current state, both of us combined would barely be considered adults. What could possibly have happened?

Fortunately, the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace disciples weren’t truly children. They frequently went out on missions and handled major situations. After shouting a few times upon waking, they calmed down.

Though this was indeed a situation they had never encountered.

When the other elders heard that something had happened, they rushed over. Only the disciples had eaten the rabbit last night. The elders were mindful of their status and hadn’t participated in this grand gathering.

“Junior Sister Yulu, could you take a look and see what’s going on here?” Luo Hongxia summoned Elder Zhou Yulu, their most skilled medical expert. It was Elder Zhou Yulu who had successfully treated Xue Shilou’s bloodline issues.

Elder Zhou Yulu’s eyelid twitched at the sight of children everywhere. Her professionalism as a physician allowed her to maintain her composure, suppressing the urge to capture this scene with a recording orb. She proceeded to diagnose their pulses one by one.

“Poison? Doesn’t seem like it? A tonic effect?”

“Was there a problem with what they ate yesterday?” Luo Hongxia pointed to the rack where only the demon rabbit’s skeleton remained.

“That shouldn’t be. I examined this demon rabbit before consumption; it was fine.”

Nevertheless, Elder Zhou Yulu scraped a small piece of meat from the skeleton and let her spiritual consciousness seep into it, analyzing it repeatedly. “There’s indeed no problem with the meat.”

Lu Yang exhaled a sigh of relief. At least I wasn’t the one who caused the problem.

Suddenly, Elder Zhou Yulu noticed that the charred wood in the large pit looked somewhat strange.

“Is this moon laurel tree cleaved and used as firewood?”

She drew a piece of charred wood toward her, letting her spiritual consciousness seep into it, analyzing its composition. Finally, she pinpointed the issue.

“There’s a problem with the moon laurel wood. This particular tree was tampered with. Several substances were added, giving it a shrinking effect.

“When burned, the moon laurel tree’s fragrance masked the other scents. Anyone who inhaled them would be unknowingly affected.”

In fact, after the demon rabbit was smoked with the moon laurel wood, these substances also remained on the meat, but only on the surface layers, not permeating the meat closest to the bone.

Lu Yang re-inhaled the breath of relief he exhaled. So it’s connected to me after all.

“But are Little Lan and the others alright?” This was Luo Hongxia’s primary concern.

“It’s nothing serious. They have merely shrunk in size. Left alone, they should return to normal in a few days. By the time I even develop an antidote, they’ll likely have already recovered on their own.”

“As long as it’s nothing serious.”

“Palace Leader, the problem now isn’t with Junior Niece Lan and the others but with the moon laurel trees.”

Elder Zhou Yulu pointed at the skeletal remains of the demon rabbit and said gravely, “This demon rabbit grew large because it ate the mooncake with osmanthus filling. Subsequent investigations revealed that the moon laurel tree from which the osmanthus was harvested had been tampered with, containing enlarging effects.

“Now we’ve discovered another moon laurel with shrinking effects.

“Who exactly tampered with these moon laurel trees, and how many have been affected?”

Luo Hongxia’s expression grew solemn. This is indeed a major problem.

The immortal palace is protected by arrays, so outsiders can’t get in. This must be an inside job!

“Immortal Fairy, do you know who did this?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “No idea.”

I’m not the type of person with no sense of propriety, using my immortal consciousness to observe everything happening in the immortal palace all day long. freewebnovel.com

The matter of the moon laurel trees was important, but not the most pressing issue. The most urgent matter at hand was these “children.”

“Lu Yang, would you like to return to your guest room first?” Luo Hongxia suggested.

Lu Yang was the only male cultivator at the scene. The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace disciples who had transformed into children couldn’t wear proper clothing. With Lu Yang present, they were too shy to move, fearing he might see things he shouldn’t.

“Alright.” Lu Yang understood the boundaries between men and women.

However, some individuals were apparently oblivious to such concepts; the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was one example.

Inside the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy scooped up little Lu Yang under his arms and spun him around, cooing “ooh-ooh” in rhythm. Her joyful laughter echoed throughout the space.

Lu Yang’s expression was blank, his eyes like those of a lifeless fish, toyed with at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s whim.

“Immortal Fairy, there should be boundaries between men and women,” Lu Yang kindly reminded her, attempting to improve the way she treated him.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy crouched down and poked Lu Yang’s forehead, finding his current form fun to play with. With a wide grin, she said, “What is there to distinguish between men and women when you’re such a little tyke?”

1. This was probably mentioned in an earlier chapter, but the “xiao” here means small. ☜

Chapter 944: Kept A Secret, But Not Entirely

After Lu Yang transformed into a child, it wasn’t merely his stature that had shrunk; even his cultivation had been sealed away, rendering him no different from an ordinary child.

“There are no suitable clothes,” Lu Yang lamented, his brow furrowed in distress. Wrapped in his oversized garment, he paced around the room, the hem dragging along the floor. In this state, he dared not even venture into the courtyard.

His attire now enveloped him like a blanket, and since he hadn’t brought any children’s clothing, he found himself without anything wearable for now.

It wasn’t important whether he had cultivation. According to Elder Zhou Yulu, his power would return in time. For the time being, finding something he could wear was paramount.

“Where can I find a set of clothes? Ouch...” freewebnovel.com

Lu Yang continued circling the room, but when he turned back, he accidentally tripped over the trailing hem of his garment, tumbling and rolling together with the fabric in a tangle.

He struggled to push his head out from the bundle of cloth, his eyes glazed and vacant.

Fine, cultivation is also important after all.

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace disciples shared similar woes. Who in their right mind would keep a stock of children’s clothing?

As for making clothes... regrettably, not a single soul skilled with needle and thread could be found in the vast immortal palace.

There were, however, plenty adept at swinging axes and chopping trees.

In theory, the Dao-Seeking Sect had its elders, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, and Yun Zhi. Pooling their collective wisdom, they would definitely have a way to restore him to his original form.

But that was contingent on his daring to return to the sect.

This will be a dark stain on my past; Old Meng would laugh at me over this incident for a lifetime.

Fortunately, all the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace disciples had also shrunk. Everyone would tacitly keep such an embarrassing affair to themselves, so there was no need to worry about the matter leaking.

For reasons such as saving face, the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace's higher-ups would also refrain from divulging anything.

Lu Yang’s gaze fell upon the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. His initially gentle look gradually grew fearsome.

In that case, only one person remains who may spill the beans.

To deal with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, I will have to resort to some unpresentable methods!

“Immortal Fairy, you absolutely must not speak of this to anyone, alright?” With his stature shrunk, Lu Yang’s voice had also become childish. His servile pleading entreaty came out in a babyish tone.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy giggled as she tugged at Lu Yang’s chubby little cheeks, which were plump and pleasant to the touch. Then she scooped him up and plopped him onto her lap, tousling his hair. “Come, say a few more nice things.”

Lu Yang leaned back and gazed up at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s pretty face, finding it utterly terrifying.

He had no choice but to endure humiliation and flatter the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with honeyed words. “Immortal Fairy, you are kind and beautiful. Surely you wouldn’t speak of my situation to outsiders and let them laugh at me.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy tried her best to maintain a straight face. “How could anyone laugh at you? Everyone sympathizes with you, Xiao Yangzi. Your heart is too dark. You must believe that everyone is a good person.”

“Immortal Fairy, I’m a minister of the Great Dou Dynasty. If outsiders learn of my current state, wouldn’t it damage our dynasty’s reputation?”

“Then I’ll only tell Little Ling, Lianyi, and the others. They’re all members of our Great Dou Dynasty; they won’t harm the dynasty’s image.”

“Immortal Fairy~~pretty please~~” Lu Yang nuzzled affectionately against the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s arm, enduring the utter humiliation.

Seeing Lu Yang so obedient, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy beamed with delight. “Very well then, I’ll help you keep this matter secret.”

Lu Yang hurriedly expressed his gratitude, fearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would change her mind. “Your Exalted Majesty, many thanks for your great kindness and favor! Your subject, Lu Yang, shall never forget it!”

He breathed a sigh of relief. Although the Everlasting Immortal Fairy isn’t reliable, she won’t break a promise. If she says she won’t leak the secret, she certainly won’t.

I’m safe now.

After being tormented by her for half the day, I’ve finally had things sorted with her.

Lu Yang felt somewhat tired, probably from all that pacing earlier. Without his cultivation, many tasks had indeed become inconvenient.

He gripped the edge of a stool, kicked his legs, and hoisted himself onto it. With much effort, he reached for the spirit fruits placed on the table. The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace had prepared these for guests. They were so precious that even a fortune couldn’t trade for them in the outside world.

If Lu Yang ate spirit fruits in his original state, it would have been just for novelty; his cultivation had reached a level where spirit fruits could hardly aid him. However, consuming them now could restore his stamina.

Out of habit, he rubbed the fruit’s skin with his hand, then took a small bite. Tasting such spiritual items in a shrunk state indeed felt different. The energy expended from wandering around the room was soon replenished.

“Being small isn’t so bad.” Lu Yang chuckled, hugging the fruit. This is a rare experience and feels quite novel.

In the past, I could devour a spirit fruit in a few bites. Now, I can’t even finish one with me hugging it.

~~~

A mysterious figure streaked through the air and appeared above the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

The immortal palace’s Great Sect Defense Array might as well be nonexistent before this enigmatic figure. She passed straight through it without triggering any alarm.

Her goal was clear; she dashed straight for the first guest room where Lu Yang resided, unnoticed by anyone.

Employing some unknown divine ability or immortal art, the mysterious figure caused the door to become as insubstantial as a phantom image before her, allowing her to enter the room without needing to push the door open.

Lu Yang finally detected the unexpected guest. He jerked his head up, his eyes full of wariness.

“Who goes there!”

“Little Junior Brother, Senior Immortal Fairy, about the Twins River...”

Lu Yang and the mysterious figure locked eyes. Senior sister and junior brother stood in silence; at that moment, time itself seemed to stand still.

Yun Zhi blinked, staring at the child before her, who hugged a spirit fruit with two bites taken out of it, his tiny face full of vigilance. The corner of her eye twitched twice.

She had noticed Elder Zhu Hong’s eagerness to consume the Twins River’s water in hopes of bearing a child and found it unwise to keep waiting for Lu Yang’s return. Who knew how long he would linger at the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace?

Rather than wait, I figured it would be better to quietly visit the immortal palace and inquire with the Immortal Fairy about the Twins River.

I’ve entered the immortal palace, but what is this situation before my eyes?

“Little Junior Brother, you...” Yun Zhi’s expression turned peculiar. Is this immortal palace so nurturing? Before setting out, Little Junior Brother had been a full-grown man, but now, he has become this tiny tyke.

“I’m not Lu Yang!” Lu Yang hastily denied. Although denial is futile before Big Senior Sister, a token attempt at concealment is still necessary. This is a matter of principle.

“Nor am I Lu Yin!” Lu Yang blurted out before he could register the words.

At this critical juncture, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy recalled her promise to keep Lu Yang’s diminution a secret. I was so absorbed in contemplating how to play with Xiao Yangzi that I didn’t notice Lass Yun sneaking up on us.

Too careless of me.

No, this won’t do. Wouldn’t this mean I had failed to keep my word? This would tarnish my image!

I must help Xiao Yangzi keep this secret!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy flew out of the mental space to salvage the situation, like mending the pen after sheep are lost. Her mind raced as she frantically explained, “Lass Yun, don’t be mistaken! Xiao Yangzi hasn’t shrunk; this isn’t Xiao Yangzi! The reason he looks so much like him is, is...because this is Xiao Yangzi’s and my child!”

Yun Zhi. “...”

Chapter 945: Clothing

Yun Zhi had always considered herself someone who remained unruffled in all kinds of situations, capable of calmly analyzing any problem, such as the terrifying lightning she faced, her first battle with an immortal, the moment she discovered Lu Yang’s exceptional talent in spells...

Some issues remained unresolved, but she had at least maintained her composure throughout.

After hearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words, however, her mind genuinely struggled to process them.

Plop.

Lu Yang was so startled that he dropped the spirit fruit in his hand, and it rolled away to some unknown corner.

“I...I am Lu Yang,” he hastily announced his true identity.

If I allow the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to continue speaking, who knows what world-shocking things she may spout next?

At that time, Big Senior Sister may be reluctant to lay hands on the Immortal Fairy, which means the unlucky one will be me!

~~~

Within the guest room, Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy knelt side by side in silence, obediently listening to Yun Zhi’s lecture.

Yun Zhi paced before them with a ruler in hand. The two trembled like a leaf, not daring to move or even lift their heads, lest they suffer a beating from the ruler.

“Senior Immortal Fairy, there are things one must not utter carelessly. They can easily lead to great chaos. Do you know that?

“I can understand your desire to protect Little Junior Brother, but you must not go overboard. If outsiders were to hear this, they might think something happened between the two of you, affecting both your reputations.”

“I was wrong. I won’t ever lie again.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy bowed her head, acknowledging her mistake with a fairly sincere attitude. If not for her insufficient literary skills, she might even have felt the urge to write a formal letter of apology.

Given how rare it was for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to admit her faults, most of the alarm that had made Yun Zhi’s heart pound subsided.

Scaring them a little is enough. I can’t actually beat them with the ruler.

Unfortunately, the monarch chair had been left behind at Heaven’s Gate Peak. Yun Zhi fetched a random chair from the room and sat before the two, listening to Lu Yang recount the sequence of events.

“In other words, the moon laurel tree was the problem, causing you to shrink when you ignited it?”

“Not just me—all the immortal palace disciples have shrunk.”

Yun Zhi nodded. This matter was neither trivial nor serious. Just like Elder Zhou Yulu had said, the shrinking and loss of cultivation were temporary. As long as they didn’t venture out during this period, no major issues should arise.

Of course, it would also be best if no one else secretly infiltrates the immortal palace like me.

“Big Senior Sister, do you have a way to return me to normal?” Lu Yang looked hopefully at his seemingly omnipotent Big Senior Sister. This child’s body is terribly inconvenient. I have to jump on a stool and stretch hard to reach spirit fruits.

Yun Zhi didn’t answer directly, beckoning to him instead. “Come here, let me examine you.”

“Oh.”

Yun Zhi pinched Lu Yang’s cheek, then caressed his little head. She shook her head regretfully, dashing his hopes. “This won’t do. I’m not well-versed in pharmacology. In situations like yours, you will have to rely on time to recover.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked puzzled. Is this matter truly so difficult?

I’m not well-versed in pharmacology either, but returning Xiao Yangzi to normal would be quite easy. However, once he changes back, I’ll no longer get to knead and squeeze him as I please.

Lass Yun just taught me not to lie, so I presume she must be speaking the truth now. This proves that she genuinely lacks the ability.

Looking at it from this perspective, Lass Yun indeed can’t compare to me, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mused gleefully. Aside from wisdom, I’ve found yet another area where I’m better than Lass Yun.

“Don’t you have suitable clothing?” Yun Zhi noticed Lu Yang’s garments were abnormally loose.

“No.”

“How about this? Find a piece of clothing, and I’ll tailor it for you.”

Lu Yang’s face lit up with delight. “Big Senior Sister, you know how to tailor clothes?”

“I learned it as a child, but it’s been a long time since I’ve practiced. I hope I haven’t grown rusty.”

Just as Lu Yang was about to go and find some clothes, he realized that apart from the garment wrapped around him, his other clothes were all stored inside his identity jade tablet.

And without his magical power, he couldn’t access it now.

Yun Zhi reached out and retrieved a set of clothes from Lu Yang’s identity jade tablet. This had nothing to do with cultivation—it was her privilege as acting sect leader.

She carefully scrutinized Lu Yang, forming a design in her mind. With her finger as a blade, she cut the garment into a size suited for Lu Yang’s current form. Following that, she took out a needle and thread from her own identity jade tablet. Stitch by stitch, she crafted the clothing for Lu Yang—cutting, sewing, adding patterns, smoothing wrinkles...

Yun Zhi’s movements were fluid, nothing like the “rusty” skill from lack of practice as she had claimed. On the contrary, Lu Yang had never seen anyone surpass her craftsmanship in this regard.

“It’s done.”

Yun Zhi flicked the clothing. It was a white outfit with blue edging, the workmanship exquisite.

Lu Yang received it with care, as if acquiring a supreme treasure. Come to think of it, this is my first time receiving something handmade by Big Senior Sister. Setting aside its practical value, its commemorative significance alone is extraordinary.

“By the way, Senior Immortal Fairy, did you suggest letting the immortal palace people drink from the Twins River?” Yun Zhi finally recalled the main purpose of her visit.

“Yes. Didn’t they say they want children? Drinking from the Twins River would be perfect for that.”

“Are there any precautions to note when drinking the river water? For instance, is there a specific amount one should consume each time?”

“I’m not so particular about the things I create. One bowl is sufficient. Drinking more or even plunging headfirst into the river won’t matter; you won’t give birth to quadruplets just because you drank more.

“Also, a person can only drink from the Twins River once in their lifetime. The second time will have no effect; it becomes no different from ordinary river water.”

Yun Zhi nodded inwardly. It seems the Twins River and the Mother-Child River are used in the same manner, differing only slightly in their effects.

“In that case, Little Junior Brother, take care of yourself here at the immortal palace. Return to the Dao-Seeking Sect whenever you wish.” Yun Zhi rose to take her leave. Despite some twists and turns on this trip, her goal had ultimately been achieved.

After bidding goodbye to Yun Zhi, Lu Yang told the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to close her eyes and not look at him.

“I need to change.”

“Don’t worry, I won’t peek.”

Lu Yang slipped into his new clothes with a rustle. They fit perfectly, and he appeared renewed, brimming with energy. Previously, when he was wrapped in his clothes like a blanket, he resembled a patient.

Not long after Lu Yang had changed, he heard Lan Ting knock on the door. “Senior Brother Lu Yang, are you in?”

“Come in.”

Lan Ting was dressed in new clothes and carried another set in her arms. A mischievous smile tugged at the corner of her mouth.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, the elders just went down the mountain and bought clothes for everyone. However, they forgot about your situation and purchased only women’s garments. Would you like to make do with this... Eh? You already have clothes?”

She stared at the well-dressed Lu Yang in surprise. My plan has failed.

“Ah, yes. I happened to have brought a set of children’s clothes with me,” Lu Yang said with an awkward laugh. I can’t exactly say that Big Senior Sister had visited and made me a new outfit on the spot.

Lan Ting looked at Lu Yang with a peculiar expression. Why would Senior Brother Lu Yang carry children’s clothes with him?

Chapter 946: Three Suspects

Lan Ting had come to the guest room to deliver clothes. Although he had no use for them himself, Lu Yang couldn’t simply send her away now. That would be discourteous.

“Junior Sister Lan, would you like to come in and have a seat?”

“Sure.” Lan Ting entered and noticed a half-eaten spirit fruit by the doorway.

“I didn’t hold it steady earlier and accidentally dropped it on the floor,” Lu Yang explained sheepishly as he grabbed the spirit fruit, wiped it clean, and resumed eating.

Both of them struggled to hop onto their chairs. After that, Lu Yang initiated a conversation about their diminution.

“Has it been discovered who dosed the moon laurel trees?” This culprit caused me to turn small! Lu Yang swore to bring them to justice once they were caught!

“Not yet. Investigations revealed that a total of thirty-six moon laurel trees of various ages have been dosed, taking on enlarging and shrinking properties. The one used for the mooncake filling and the one you chopped down were two of them.”

Lu Yang helplessly pressed his hand to his forehead. With moon laurel trees covering the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace’s mountains, he had simply picked a thriving one at random, never expecting it to be among those dosed.

What luck.

The immortal palace also understood that this was a matter of luck, unrelated to Lu Yang.

If it were related to him, he might have ended up in a cell next to Xue Shilou for a while. But then again, the two could exchange insights on Sword Dao, so it wouldn’t necessarily be a disaster.

Lan Ting continued, “Also, when the pill concoction chamber took stock of its inventory, dozens of precious medicinal ingredients were found missing. Traces of these ingredients were discovered on the dosed moon laurel trees.

“The pill concoction chamber conducts an inventory check every two months before going down the mountain to purchase supplies. That’s why the theft has gone unnoticed until now.”

“So it was really the work of someone within the immortal palace?” Lu Yang asked.

The storage area for medicinal ingredients would certainly be protected by layers of arrays. To pass through these arrays and steal the ingredients, the culprit had to be either an immortal or someone from within the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

“My shifu is investigating each suspect one by one, but so far, there haven’t been any leads. Moreover, she can’t fathom why the thief would experiment on moon laurel trees. What could be their purpose?” Although Lan Ting really wanted to help her shifu resolve this intractable situation, she was, unfortunately, a child now and could not be of assistance.

“How many suspects are there?” Despite Lu Yang’s miniature size and his loss of magical powers, he trusted that his mind still functioned well. Perhaps I can uncover some clues.

Lan Ting saw no harm in sharing the details with Lu Yang and counted on her fingers. “There are three: Elder Miao, the former supervisor of the pill concoction chamber; Elder Mei, the current supervisor; and Senior Sister Bai, Elder Mei’s eldest disciple.

“Only the three of them know how to open the great array and can freely access the pill concoction chamber’s medicine repository.

“In fact, Junior Grand-Aunt Qu Ling, the previous palace leader, also knows how to open the great array. However, she’s currently imprisoned in Sinner Hall. It can’t be her.

“Although we can’t ascertain who stole the precious medicinal ingredients, the time of theft can be determined.”

“How so?”

“Every time the great array is opened to enter the medicine repository, a record is kept—what time it was, who opened it, and what medicinal ingredients were taken.

“According to the data, over the past two months, the great array was opened sixteen times: eight by Senior Sister Bai, six by Elder Mei, and two by Elder Miao.

“However, after an elder adept at arrays meticulously investigated the records, she discovered the great array had been opened seventeen times—one more time than recorded!

“This extra time must be when the thief opened it!

“My shifu has investigated in detail what each of the three was doing on that day.”

With much effort, Lan Ting grabbed two spirit fruits from the plate at the table’s center, one red and one blue, to represent the suspects.

Lu Yang tacitly handed her his half-eaten spirit fruit, saving her the effort of reaching for a third.

Lan Ting arranged the two whole spirit fruits and the half-eaten one in a row.

She pushed the red spirit fruit forward. “Elder Miao is skilled in clone-splitting techniques, so adept that those of the same level cannot distinguish her real self from her clones.

“After retiring, she traveled far and wide to seek breakthrough opportunities. Coincidentally, she returned to the sect a month and a half ago, allegedly due to owing a huge debt; she had come back to borrow spirit stones. As for exactly how much she owed and whether she borrowed enough, that remains unknown.

“On the day of the incident, Elder Miao was catching up with another retired elder and never left her cave abode.”

Lan Ting pushed the blue spirit fruit forward. “As the current supervisor of the pill concoction chamber, Elder Mei is always busy, and the day of the incident was no exception. She claims that she stayed in the room all day, contemplating new pill formulas and this year’s mooncake designs. She mentioned that she left the room only twice for a walk to find some inspiration, but no one saw her outside the pill concoction chamber.”

The remaining half of a spirit fruit naturally represented Senior Sister Bai. “That day, Senior Sister Bai was concocting pills. Three junior sisters passing by the pill concoction chamber saw her concocting pills through the paper window.

“The pill she was refining is called the Nine-Heart Lotus Seed Pill. It requires a full day of uninterrupted focus; leaving the pill furnace is utterly impossible. The Nine-Heart Lotus Seed Pill is exceedingly difficult to concoct. Even Senior Sister Bai has only a ten percent chance of success. She was in excellent form that day and succeeded. Afterward, she flaunted her achievement to several senior and junior sisters.

"During the investigation, another matter came to light. A week before the medicinal ingredients disappeared, Senior Sister Bai had a fierce argument with Elder Mei. Senior Sister Bai had requested three precious medicinal ingredients to refine a pill and improve her pill-concocting skills, but Elder Mei deemed her abilities insufficient and believed she would certainly fail, so she rejected the application.

“Coincidentally, these three medicinal ingredients were on the list of stolen items.”

After listening, Lu Yang had a pensive expression. Upon careful consideration, none of the three had alibis.

Elder Miao’s proficiency in clone-splitting techniques makes it difficult to distinguish real from fake. She could have used the other elder to fabricate an alibi.

Elder Mei claims to have left the room to seek inspiration, but there are no witnesses.

Senior Sister Bai’s pill concoction process required undivided attention, but the three witnesses had only seen her silhouette through the paper window. What they saw might not have been Senior Sister Bai at all.

Moreover, each of them has a motive.

Lu Yang lowered his head, an enigmatic smile playing at the corner of his lips.

This is what they mean by “it’s dark right under the lamp,” huh? People tend to overlook the things right under their noses.

“Senior Brother, have you thought of something?” Seeing Lu Yang’s expression, Lan Ting was certain he had uncovered a clue!

“Little Lan, I know who the thief is.”

“These three may appear suspicious, but that’s not the case. Since each of them has records of entering the medicine repository and taking medicinal ingredients, they could simply take what they wanted during those authorized visits. There would be no need for a seventeenth time to go through the great array unauthorized—an act that would leave traces behind!

“The only explanation is that the culprit is none of these three!"

“Junior Sister Lan, you mentioned earlier that Qu Ling, the previous palace leader, knows how to undo the medicine repository’s grand array. Doesn’t that imply the current palace leader also knows how to open it?”

Lu Yang’s visage flickered with pain. Though the answer will be hard for Junior Sister Lan to hear, it is the truth—a cruel truth she must confront!

“Therefore, the answer is obvious. The perpetrator is none other than Luo—”

Before Lu Yang could finish, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy witnessed a surprising scene with her immortal consciousness. “Eh? Why is that little lass Bai Ye dosing the moon laurel trees?”

Chapter 947: The Simplest Deductions Often Only Require Immortal Consciousness

Having learned from the experience of Lu Yang inquiring about the culprit’s identity while she herself remained ignorant, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy constantly scanned the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace with her immortal consciousness, vowing to find the culprit and salvage her dignity.

Fortunately, I’ve finally found a lead.

Just as I thought, as long as I, Huang Doudou, take charge, there’s no uncrackable case!

“Who? Bai Ye?”

Hearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s sudden injection, Lu Yang found himself unable to utter the words “Palace Leader Luo,” which had been on the tip of his tongue.

“Immortal Fairy, next time, could you please share what you saw earlier?!” Lu Yang refused to believe the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hadn’t noticed anything amiss before Bai Ye started dosing the moon laurel trees.

Besides, even if it was Bai Ye, how did she manage to break the medicine repository’s great array?

“Isn’t the principle to catch the culprit red-handed? I only suspected her before; what if I had wrongfully accused that lass?” Having studied law alongside Lu Yang for so long, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had developed quite a legal mindset.

“Senior Brother? Senior Brother Lu Yang?” Lan Ting noticed that Lu Yang had suddenly fallen silent in the middle of his analysis. Puzzled, she waved her small, fair hand before Lu Yang’s face, finally jolting him back to attention.

Lu Yang realized that he was in the middle of analyzing the case; it wasn’t the time for bickering with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Come, come, come, let me take charge of this!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that since she had uncovered the truth, she should be the one to reveal the answer! freewebnovel.com

How could Lu Yang be a match for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy? In an instant, his body was taken over.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy adopted an expression as if she had just woken from a dream. “Ah, I’m here, I’m here. Where did I stop just now?”

“You just said ‘The perpetrator is none other than Luo...’ and then you stopped talking.” Lan Ting looked at “Lu Yang” with a peculiar expression, though she concealed it well.

Why does it feel like Senior Brother has become a different person?

With her extensive experience taking over Lu Yang’s body and playing as him during their time in the imperial city, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy now mimicked him with remarkable accuracy; she didn’t even refer to herself as “this immortal” anymore.

“What I meant to say just now was ‘The perpetrator is none other than the delicate and fragile Bai Ye!”

“Lu Yang” declared with confidence, “Criminals often return to the scene of the crime. If I’m not mistaken, she is currently at the moon laurel grove—the thirtieth tree in the twelfth row!”

Lan Ting was befuddled. How did Senior Brother Lu Yang deduce such a precise location? Did I miss some steps in his reasoning just now?

Just as I thought, I can’t keep up with Senior Brother Lu Yang’s thought process.

And most importantly...

“Who is Bai Ye?” She had never heard of such a person in the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

“You don’t know her? She comes to me every night to listen to stories,” “Lu Yang” said with a hint of resentment in “his” tone.

If not for that little lass occupying Lu Yang’s nights, Lu Yang could have spent the whole night playing snowball fights with me.

“Goes to you every night to listen to stories?” Lan Ting grew increasingly alarmed. Who is this person, skipping cultivation to secretly visit Senior Brother and get a jump on me?

“Wait, wait,” Lu Yang couldn’t help but interject from the mental space. “How could Junior Sister Lan Ting not have heard of Junior Sister Bai Ye?”

This makes it seem like I’ve been telling stories every night to someone who doesn’t exist—it’s terrifying.

“She’s something like an incarnation of the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor, probably a secret within the immortal palace. It’s perfectly normal for Lass Lan not to have heard of her.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy revealed Bai Ye’s identity, as if the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor was some insignificant figure.

“Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor?!” Lu Yang was flabbergasted.

He suddenly recalled that Bai Ye had given him a pouch of moon laurel flowers to snack on. Could Bai Ye have plucked them from herself?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t care about Lu Yang’s reaction for now. As the only person in the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace who knew the truth, she felt that her intellect had reached a transcendent realm. She was determined to capture Bai Ye in one go.

“Let’s put this aside first. We’ll go after Bai Ye now!”

With a wave of her hand, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy led Lan Ting at a brisk trot all the way to Luo Hongxia’s cave abode.

Xiao Yangzi currently has no cultivation. Even if we find Bai Ye, he can’t catch her. We’ll need Luo Hongxia, this defeated opponent, to assist.

But then again, even if Xiao Yangzi still has his cultivation, he probably can’t catch Bai Ye either.

~~~

At the moment, Luo Hongxia also had three spirit fruits laid out before her as she pondered which one represented the thief who stole the medicinal ingredients.

Hearing a knock, she opened the door, but saw no one.

“Here, here.”

Luo Hongxia looked down and spotted two little tykes.

“Shifu, Senior Brother Lu Yang has deduced the culprit’s identity! It’s a little lass called Bai Ye. She is about my height and is in the moon laurel grove right now!”

“Who is Bai Ye?” Luo Hongxia had never heard of the name either.

But her expression quickly turned serious. Now is not the time to mull over Bai Ye’s identity. Since we have traces of the culprit’s whereabouts, the most important thing is to go to the moon laurel grove and catch her!

“Let’s go!”

After Luo Hongxia soared into the air, she noticed her two companions missing. Looking down, she saw the two little tykes frantically trotting toward the moon laurel grove.

She landed and tucked one under each arm before speeding toward the moon laurel grove again.

“Let’s go!”

Carrying the two burdens didn’t slow Luo Hongxia in the slightest. She even thoughtfully enveloped them in transparent shields to protect them from the biting wind.

Flying over the moon laurel grove, she indeed spotted a petite figure pouring something into a pit beside a moon laurel tree, muttering something under her breath.

“Thief, take this!”

Luo Hongxia dropped the two little tykes and attacked fiercely.

With the help of the shields, the two bounced a couple of times upon landing and came to a stop safely.

Seeing Luo Hongxia strike, the petite figure cursed inwardly, Oh dear! She was too engrossed in her experiments on the moon laurel trees and momentarily failed to detect Luo Hongxia’s arrival.

The petite figure seemed to have no intention of fighting. She turned and fled with such speed that only an afterimage remained, her true form having teleported to some unknown location.

Even with Luo Hongxia’s sharp vision, she couldn’t track the petite figure’s movements. She expanded her spiritual consciousness to search, but found nothing.

Recalling the petite figure’s face, she furrowed her brows. “An unfamiliar face. Could it be an outsider?”

~~~

“What a close shave. Little Luo almost caught up to me.” The petite figure leaned against the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor, panting from fright. She still couldn’t figure out how Luo Hongxia had discovered her.

It was as if she knew exactly where I would be; her targeting was remarkably accurate.

“Heh heh, trying to run? Do you think you can escape?” A childish laugh sounded from behind the petite figure, startling her into spinning around.

“Who’s there?!” She was certain that with her spiritual consciousness extended, she would have detected anyone approaching.

And how did this person know I’m here?

“Lu Yang?” the petite figure exclaimed in surprise. How could it be Lu Yang?

“Lass Bai Ye, come back with me obediently and admit your mistakes.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy smirked smugly. No matter how fast Bai Ye is, how could she outpace my immortal consciousness?

Caught red-handed—a meritorious achievement!

The petite figure snorted coldly. “I’m not Bai Ye. I’m Bai Ri.”[1]

Within the mental space, Lu Yang vaguely remembered hearing this name somewhere and started.

“Bai Ri... Why do I recall that the founder of the immortal palace, the Moonchaser True Person, was called Bai Ri?”

1. “Ye” means night, and “ri” means day. ☜

Chapter 948: Moonchaser True Person

The Moonchaser True Person, Bai Ri, was the founder of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, active during the late Great Yu to early Great Xia eras. Legend held that she was elegant and graceful like an immortal fairy, with a beauty that surpassed that of mortals, captivating countless heroes of her time.

Lu Yang pulled his attention back from his memories. From the mental space, he stared at the little girl named “Bai Ri.” She appeared around ten years old, only slightly taller than his shrunken form.

She’s cute indeed, but isn’t the gap between her and adjectives like “elegant and graceful” rather vast?

“Aren’t you the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor? How did you become the Moonchaser True Person?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked, perplexed. She had sensed earlier that Bai Ye was more than just the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor, and she now confirmed there was indeed something amiss.

Bai Ye was taken aback. “How do you know about the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor?” She was certain she had never told anyone about this.

“First, tell me about this body of yours.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy wasn’t so foolish as to answer every question thrown at her. This is called information exchange.

“If you can catch me, I’ll tell you.” Bai Ri’s mouth curved into a smirk. This kid called Lu Yang is truly interesting. No wonder Bai Ye sought him out every night to hear his stories.

As soon as the words fell, Bai Ri vanished into the vast expanse of snow, leaving no trace. Gazing around, one could only see the endless stretches of moon laurel trees.

Bai Ri’s cultivation was so high that even if Lu Yang was no longer a child and had regained his original strength, he would never be able to so much as touch the hem of her garment.

Unfortunately for her, the current Lu Yang was not Lu Yang.

“How dare you try to run right under my nose!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s fighting spirit ignited. Through my brilliant deductions, the true culprit has revealed herself. All that remains is the capture.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy swung her little arms and gave chase, her gaze resolute, her goal clear.

Huff, huff. Huff, huff.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s breathing followed a rhythm, as if imbued with some mystical power, piquing Lu Yang’s curiosity.

Legend had it that in the most ancient of eras, the earliest Qi Training cultivators were called Qi Refiners. The cultivation method they mastered was known as the Breathing Technique. By breathing in specific patterns, they could create all sorts of unimaginable wonders.

Lu Yang carefully sensed his physical state and was astonished to discover that after employing the Breathing Technique, he could prevent the cold wind from rushing into his mouth and nose.

What an impressive Breathing Technique!

“He won’t find me here, right?” Bai Ri had fled to a corner of the immortal palace. The place itself was already sparsely populated, and this particular corner hadn’t had anyone passing by in decades. It’s absolutely safe.

Bai Ri found dealing with Lu Yang somewhat intractable. There was no deep-seated enmity between them, so she didn’t have a reason to strike with lethal force. Since she couldn’t bring herself to deliver any fatal blows, her only option was to flee.

“How exactly did he find me just now?

“That’s right. When I hid near the Tree Ancestor earlier, he noticed my connection to the Tree Ancestor and went there to try his luck.

“Troublesome kid. No wonder he has experienced so much at such a young age.”

~~~

Six hours later, a familiar voice sounded.

“Found you! Don’t run!”

There stood the Everlasting Immortal Fairy on skis crafted from moon laurel wood, a basket of spirit fruits strapped to her back. Whenever she was tired from skiing, she would take a couple of bites to replenish her stamina.

From the moon laurel grove to this corner of the immortal palace, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had skied for six hours! Without the skis, it would have taken even longer!

Having schemed throughout the ages, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was even aware that the shortest distance between two points was a straight line. To take the shortest route to find Bai Ri, she skied all the way, overcoming obstacles along the path, passing through the pill concoction chamber, the artifact refinement chamber, the hot springs, and other locations.

Her skiing movements were graceful and practiced, clearly those of an old hand.

Along the way, she encountered numerous witnesses, but the immortal palace disciples simply assumed “Lu Yang” was skiing for fun, unaware that he was actually pursuing a criminal.

“Wait, Immortal Fairy, when did you learn to ski?”

“Hmph, didn’t expect that, did you? Back in the ancient era, I foresaw this day and practiced skiing techniques in advance with a mortal body,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy declared without any shame.

“How do you keep finding me?!” Bai Ri looked as though she had seen a ghost. Do I have some scent that allows Lu Yang to sniff out my location? Or did listening to his stories somehow get me marked by him?

Bai Ri was about to flee again when suddenly, her legs gave way, and she couldn’t muster a single ounce of strength.

Crap, it’s night. freewebnovel.com

“Yawn... Why am I here today?” “Bai Ri” sat on the ground with a blank expression, looking around in confusion. Isn’t this a corner of the immortal palace? There’s nothing fun here.

Then she spotted the Everlasting Immortal Fairy skiing toward her.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang!” “Bai Ri” waved excitedly at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy executed a beautiful turn, skidding to a halt before “Bai Ri” and sending up a spray of snow as tall as a person.

“Now you’re Bai Ye, right?”

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, you already know everything?” Bai Ye’s mouth opened in shock.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy smiled. Having witnessed firsthand the transformation of “Bai Ri” to “Bai Ye,” she finally made sense of what was going on.

“Two souls in one body, switching dominance at the transition between yin and yang. Am I correct?”

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, you know so much.” Bai Ye grew increasingly surprised, feeling that Lu Yang knew more than she did.

“Of course! Look who this...this person you’re talking to is!”

“Little Ye, wait a moment. Let me talk to Lu Yang for a bit.” Bai Ri temporarily took control of the body.

Bai Ri sighed. Now that things have come to this, there’s no longer any point in hiding. I might as well tell Lu Yang everything, lest this kid keep pursuing me.

“I don’t know what’s up with you, kid; you even know something like two souls in one body.

“You guessed correctly. I am me, and Little Ye is Little Ye. However, the two of us share this body. I use it during the day, and she uses it at night.

“Little Ye’s original form is the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor. Rooted in the Great Snow Mountain, she cannot leave her territory. Thus, she has always yearned for life in the outside world.

“She often eavesdrops on immortal palace disciples recounting their external missions. Ever since she saw your story in Lan Ting’s mission reports, she longed to meet you in person.

“When Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect spread to the immortal palace, Little Ye’s desire to meet you grew even stronger.

“Coincidentally, you came. She sought you out every night to listen to stories, and naturally, I listened along as well.

“Truth be told, I somewhat wish you hadn’t come to the immortal palace. Before Little Ye heard of you, she always listened to my stories—tales of how Jiang Ping’an, Meng Junzi, and the rest of us fought our way across the land and established Great Xia.

“After you appeared, Little Ye’s attention shifted entirely to you.”

Bai Ri sighed again, looking at Lu Yang with an indescribably strange expression. “Although I’m reluctant to admit it, I must say that your experiences over the past few years are far more absurd than mine.”

Chapter 949: Honest Confession

The Moonchaser True Person considered her life to have been fulfilling. She had lived through the warlords’ contention in the late Great Yu era, witnessed the fall of Great Yu in the battle for supremacy, endured the tumultuous age punctuated by battles of Transcendent Tribulation cultivators and half-immortals, exchanged blows with Meng Junzi, aided Jiang Ping’an in establishing Great Xia, and founded the Five Great Immortal Sects with several fellow Daoists.

Tales of these exploits were passed down through generations, reinterpreted and reenacted, becoming part of the widely beloved storytelling epic Heroes of Great Xia.

Yet, they truly pale in comparison to Lu Yang’s experiences.

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, This is just the tip of the iceberg. What I’ve been sharing is the abridged versions. I haven’t even mentioned resurrecting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the various inside stories of half-immortal and immortal battles, encountering Hui Doudou, and overthrowing Great Xia to establish the Great Dou Dynasty.

“Don't digress so far. Confess honestly: why did you dose the moon laurel trees?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was displeased with how the Moonchaser True Person had described Lu Yang's experiences over the past few years.

How could you call that absurd? This is clearly called "fulfilling." I greatly admire Xiao Yangzi’s life experiences—full of surprises and challenges.

The Moonchaser True Person intended to explain matters clearly from the moment she decided to show herself. “To explain this, I must first start from the day Little Ye gained spirit intelligence.

“Little Ye's true form is what the world calls the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor, a moon laurel tree that has existed since ancient times. It is at least three hundred thousand years old, and after weathering the ages, it developed consciousness, then spirit intelligence, becoming a true living being.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded. This was the standard process for spirit plants to develop spirit intelligence. There were no shortcuts to speak of; the patient waited through the passage of eons.

If it truly is a moon laurel tree that has survived from ancient times, it might really have been planted by the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

“I am Bai Ri. Little Ye took my surname, Bai. She is fond of luna power and enjoys being active at night, so she named herself Bai Ye.

“Little Ye didn’t really like using the Tree Ancestor’s body, finding standing still all day far too boring. Thus, I found a method from ancient texts for spirit plants to create clones, allowing her to separate a body from the Tree Ancestor, which is what you see now.

“After several hundred years, something went wrong with my cultivation. My physical body was incinerated, and my soul was damaged so severely that no miraculous pills were effective. The situation then was dire.

“Fortunately, moon laurel trees are inherently yin in nature and possess the ability to nourish souls, their capability even surpassing that of locust trees. As the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor, Little Ye’s soul-nourishing ability is unparalleled in the world.

“She noticed the problem with my cultivation and hastily transferred my soul into this clone. At the time, I was delirious and unaware of her actions. I only felt a comfortably warm energy nurturing my soul, and I instinctively accepted it.

“Normally, nourishing the soul is a slow process. But the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor’s soul-nourishing ability was too strong, and so was my will to survive. The combination of these two factors accelerated the process tremendously, ultimately causing my soul to become so entangled with this clone that they could no longer be separated.

“Although my soul had recovered fully, I could no longer leave this clone.

“Nevertheless, having survived such a life-and-death crisis, living in this clone isn’t so bad. I can guard the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, secretly watch the disciples grow, and visit the scripture library daily to read. Besides, I also quite like moon laurel trees.”

Had she not genuinely loved moon laurel trees, the Moonchaser True Person wouldn’t have chosen to establish the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace on the harsh, unforgiving Great Snow Mountain.

“Little Ye grew accustomed to this clone and eventually shared it with me, leaving only instinctual responses within the Tree Ancestor’s true form.

“Later, we discovered that whichever soul was stronger would forcibly seize control of this body. This was an involuntary process beyond either of our control.

“Little Ye’s soul strength fluctuates with day and night. Solar power weakens her soul, so control of the body is passed to me during the day, and she will either sleep in her true form or within this body. At night, when luna power peaks and her soul strengthens, she will use this body.

“This clone is sufficiently robust, and with the Tree Ancestor continuously transmitting spirit energy, it also has strong regenerative abilities. Only two problems remain unsolved. First, as mentioned, the clone cannot leave the Tree Ancestor’s territory; second, it doesn’t quite match my image.”

The Moonchaser True Person sighed, reminiscing about her glorious past. “I was once a peerless beauty in the mortal realm, my fame resounding across the world. Who could resist my charm?

“In contrast, Little Ye’s clone is too short and utterly lacking in charm. I’m embarrassed to be seen like this. Hence, I thought about whether I could make this clone taller—if not permanently, then at least during the day.

“Unfortunately, this clone’s form is difficult to alter. Changing it would require an alternative approach.

“Since this clone is essentially a moon laurel tree, I wondered if I could develop a formula to accelerate the growth of moon laurel trees. With that, I took several herbs from the medicine repository, decocted them into various proportions, and poured the concoctions onto moon laurel tree roots to see which ratios promoted growth.

“I figured that with moon laurel trees covering the Great Snow Mountain, picking a few for experiments wouldn’t matter. Who could have anticipated that someone would harvest petals for mooncake filling and chop down a tree for barbecue?”

The Moonchaser True Person was already embarrassed to face anyone. Naturally, she would hide these experiments on promoting moon laurel tree growth as much as possible.

But when it came to luck, there was really no telling.

Lu Yang listened quietly to the tale and could understand the Moonchaser True Person’s feelings. In the few days since I’ve shrunk, haven’t I kept wanting to grow back?

“Done with the confessions? Then come back with me and plead guilty.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy remained unmoved by the Moonchaser True Person’s smooth talk, ever mindful that her purpose here was to apprehend a criminal.

~~~

“Strange, where has that kid Lu Yang gone?” Luo Hongxia murmured to herself. The last to have seen Lu Yang were several immortal palace disciples soaking in the hot springs.

According to their accounts, Lu Yang had been on skis, carrying a basket of spirit fruits on his back, his face beaming with excitement. After that, no one had seen him again.

And that person called Bai Ye still can’t be tracked down either.

“Palace Leader Luo, open the door.”

Hearing Lu Yang’s voice, Luo Hongxia opened the door to find “Lu Yang” grinning as he held Bai Ye’s hand, as if he was afraid she would escape.

“Palace Leader Luo, I’ve caught the culprit!” “Lu Yang” raised their hands and handed Bai Ye over to Luo Hongxia.

“How did you catch her?” Luo Hongxia was floored. I couldn’t even catch up to Bai Ye. How did Lu Yang manage it?

“That’s nothing. She has also confessed honestly to her crimes.” At that moment, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt as though she had accomplished a great task and was ready to retire with glory.

“Tell me, what happened?” Luo Hongxia pressed.

“It’s like this...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy repeated the tale that the Moonchaser True Person had told, leaving Luo Hongxia dumbfounded.

“In summary, your founding ancestor, the Moonchaser True Person, stole medicinal ingredients in hopes of growing taller. I’m not too familiar with sentencing, but you people at the immortal palace are well-versed in criminal law. How many years should she get?”

Chapter 950: Ignorance of the Law is No Excuse for Breaking It

“Wait, wait, wait, wait, are you saying that she is our immortal palace’s founder, the Moonchaser True Person?” Luo Hongxia clutched her head, struggling to absorb the influx of information.

“Yes.”

“She’s the one who stole the herbs?”

“Yes.”

“And you spent an entire day before finally catching her?”

“Yes.”
