The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded vigorously, her limpid eyes gazing up at Luo Hongxia, shining as if they emitted light. “So how many years does your immortal palace intend to sentence her to?”

Luo Hongxia’s mind couldn’t process everything right away. The events have unfolded too fast. In the blink of an eye, how has the Moonchaser True Person, rumored to be in seclusion, become a criminal facing sentencing?

Conflict, confusion, and bewilderment...a myriad of emotions flickered across Luo Hongxia’s face.

Noticing Luo Hongxia’s perplexity, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy's perceptiveness allowed her to understand Luo Hongxia’s predicament immediately, and she kindly offered, “The principle of recusal, right? I understand. If you find it awkward, you can lock her up at our Dao-Seeking Sect!”

Within the mental space, Lu Yang was enjoying the spectacle when he burst into sudden coughing.

“Immortal Fairy, absolutely not!” Lu Yang hastily urged her against it.

“Is there a problem?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy thought her idea was perfectly sound.

“Immortal Fairy, have you forgotten? The Moonchaser True Person cannot leave this clone, and this clone cannot leave Bai Ye’s territory.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had evidently already considered this. “Aiya, is that all? Just move the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor to our Dao-Seeking Sect. Our sect has plenty of space.”

Seeing Lu Yang about to speak again, she anticipated his question. “Oh, did you want to say that the moon laurel tree would die if it leaves the Great Snow Mountain? That’s also a minor issue. Just move the Great Snow Mountain to our sect too. We have plenty of space.”

In the blink of an eye, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had already annexed the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace into the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“I think...the problem isn’t whether our sect has space.” Lu Yang was worried about Dai Bufan’s heart and whether he would get a beating upon his return.

By heaven and earth, my conscience is clear; this truly has nothing to do with him—it is all the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s doing.

“Are you going to arrest me?” Bai Ye asked.

As night fell, Bai Ye gained control of the body; the Moonchaser True Person could only appear during the day.

In fact, even when they came to Luo Hongxia’s cave abode, it was Bai Ye who had flown the Everlasting Immortal Fairy here.

From the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s account, Luo Hongxia had already learned of Bai Ye’s and the Moonchaser True Person’s identities. Only now did she realize her shock had momentarily made her forget propriety.

“Greetings, Tree Ancestor.”

“Just call me Bai Ye.”

“Greetings, Tree Ancestor Bai Ye.”

Bai Ye had never appeared in public precisely because people became too formal and reserved upon meeting her.

Senior Brother Lu Yang is wonderful. Even after learning my identity, he didn’t become formal or reserved.

“If you wish to see A’ri, you’ll have to wait until morning.”

Bai Ye’s arm transformed into wood, then grew and extended, shaping itself into a small stool. With a swift chop from her left hand, she severed the stool, and her arm reverted to its original form.

Lu Yang’s eye twitched. So the stool Bai Ye has been bringing to my place every night was conjured by herself.

Bai Ye sat on the small stool and turned excitedly to “Lu Yang.” “Senior Brother Lu Yang, continue the story! You were about to talk about entering the imperial city.”

Storytelling wasn’t the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s forte. She wisely returned the body to Lu Yang.

“After our journey to the East Sea concluded, Old Meng dragged me to the imperial city...”

Luo Hongxia was also intrigued by Lu Yang’s experiences. Rather than idly waiting until dawn, I might as well listen to his storytelling.

“Just like that, I reported the Fourth Imperial Prince’s rebellion, and he was thrown into prison...

“Afterward, the Fifth Imperial Prince was also thrown into prison...

“For stealing the imperial throne, the Xia Emperor and I nearly got thrown into prison as well...”

The more Luo Hongxia listened, the more her eyelids twitched.

With Lu Yang telling stories, the night passed swiftly.

As day and night traded places, the moon gradually ignited with flames, marking the arrival of morning.

“Little Ye, let me use the body.”

Their identities swapped. Although the appearance remained unchanged, the Moonchaser True Person’s gaze was noticeably sharper, lacking Bai Ye’s innocence and naivety.

“Greetings, Moonchaser True Lord.” Although Luo Hongxia already knew the person before her was the Moonchaser True Person, she still struggled to connect that legendary beauty from the portraits to this little one.

“Little Luo, is it? Bowing is a rule established by Jiang Ping’an and his court; our immortal palace need not observe such formalities.”

“Yes. And regarding your theft of herbs from the medicine repository...”

“How can you call it theft? I founded this immortal palace; the herbs are naturally mine as well.”

“The immortal palace was indeed founded by you. However, when you passed the position of palace leader to Jingchuan True Person, ownership of the immortal palace also transferred accordingly. Subsequently, Jingchuan True Person passed the position to the third Palace Leader, the fourth Palace Leader...and so on, down to my generation.

“Therefore, strictly speaking, ownership of all the immortal palace’s assets resides with me. Your unauthorized use of the herbs counts as transferring ownership without permission, which does constitute the crime of theft.”

“But...but I’m the founder of the immortal palace!” The Moonchaser True Person's defense was feeble.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy understood the Moonchaser True Person’s intentions and took over Lu Yang’s body again. “You’re trying to say that, according to criminal law, mortal elders over seventy-five need not serve prison time, and that cultivators can follow the same rule, right?”

“You don’t look like you’re a hundred thousand years old; you must have frozen yourself at some point, right? How old are you now? Are you at least seventy-five thousand years old?”

“Enough, enough. I’ll serve prison time.” The Moonchaser True Person gave in.

“Actually, your theft doesn’t necessarily require imprisonment,” Luo Hongxia kindly reminded her. “If you compensate the immortal palace and obtain its forgiveness, you can receive a suspended sentence or even be exempted from criminal punishment.”

The Moonchaser True Person was overjoyed. I knew you were on my side, Little Luo.

Compensating the immortal palace and obtaining its forgiveness are both easy matters.

“However, your act of dosing the moon laurel trees caused serious harm and consequences, thus constituting the crime of releasing hazardous substances.

“Given the combined punishment for multiple offenses, it will likely be difficult for you to receive a suspended sentence.”

“I...” This was the first time the Moonchaser True Person had suffered due to her ignorance of the law.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy kindly reminded her, “Ignorance of the law is no excuse for breaking it.”

Then Luo Hongxia turned to “Lu Yang.” “Lu Yang, though your intrusion into the hot springs doesn’t constitute a crime, it disrupted public order. It’s considered an administrative offense and requires a few days’ detention.” She had been searching for Lu Yang precisely because of this matter.

“I was pursuing someone at the time.”

“But the situation wasn’t so urgent that it prevented you from detouring around the hot springs.”

“I...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy realized that knowing the law was equally useless.

Lu Yang pressed his hand to his forehead. I knew things would develop to this point. I’ll just treat it as a life experience.

“Xiao Yangzi, don’t worry. How could I let you sit in prison? This has nothing to do with you,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy declared responsibly.

Lu Yang was astonished. “Immortal Fairy, are you planning to...”

“This immortal will take over your body for a few days and sit in prison for you.”

Chapter 951: A Second Visit to Sinner Hall

Lu Yang thought, Does it really make a difference which of us sits in prison? If you serve the sentence for me, Immortal Fairy, I’ll still be in the mental space. It’s not as if I won’t be in Sinner Hall once you’re locked up.

It’s rare to see the Everlasting Immortal Fairy willing to take responsibility for her own actions.

Though it’s useless.

Still, it is rare.

“Do I have to be locked up too?” Bai Ye replaced the Moonchaser True Person.

“When night falls, you can come out, Tree Ancestor,” Luo Hongxia said. Bai Ye has done nothing wrong. How could she be imprisoned?

“Oh, alright then.” Bai Ye retreated, handing over control of the body to the Moonchaser True Person.

“Tree Ancestor, please don’t leave just yet. There’s one more matter requiring your consent,” Luo Hongxia called out.

“What is it?”

“Previously, the immortal palace wasn’t aware that you possessed spirit intelligence, and we have been felling and selling moon laurel trees without seeking your opinion. We are deeply guilty. These moon laurel trees belong to you, so the spirit stones obtained from selling them should belong to you. Please inform us when you gain sentience to make it easier for us to calculate the spirit stones to return.”

Bai Ye found it difficult to grasp Luo Hongxia’s meaning, but she roughly understood that the latter wanted to give her spirit stones.

“I have no use for spirit stones. Just keep them. As for cutting and selling trees, continue as before.”

“Tree Ancestor, you are most benevolent and righteous.” Luo Hongxia bowed.

The moment the Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor gained spirit intelligence and became a “person,” the ownership of all moon laurel trees on the Great Snow Mountain had transferred from the immortal palace to Bai Ye. However, the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace was unaware of Bai Ye’s existence at that time. Therefore, felling and selling the moon laurel trees lacked criminal intent and did not constitute a crime.

Now that the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace knew of Bai Ye’s existence, they could no longer fell or sell moon laurel trees without Bai Ye’s consent.

~~~

Sinner Hall.

“Palace Leader, what brings you here?” Elder Mo Ran was surprised. She was clad in a black dress with lotus patterns.

What surprised her even more was that Luo Hongxia had brought two children with her.

“You have children now?”

As Elder Mo Ran was in charge of overseeing Sinner Hall, she rarely had the opportunity to leave and was unaware of recent events outside.

Her imagination instantly conjured a scenario:

Luo Hongxia and the Taciturn Daoist Priest secretly developed feelings for each other, but the Taciturn Daoist Priest had numerous enemies and dared not make their relationship public, forcing them to meet in secret, even bearing two children. Now that the Taciturn Daoist Priest has advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and no longer fears his enemies, Luo Hongxia finally dares to announce their relationship, bringing her children around to meet everyone...

Luo Hongxia’s eyelid twitched. I can’t help but find the way Junior Sister Mo Ran looks at me unsettling.

Junior Sister Mo Ran has always been imaginative. Who knows what she’s concocting in her mind now?

“Recently, an incident occurred in the immortal palace; all the disciples have shrunk, and Lu Yang is no exception. This little fellow is Lu Yang.”

“So mystical? And is Lu Yang here to visit Sinner Hall again?”

“He’ll be staying for five days.”

Elder Mo Ran was taken aback, but quickly understood Luo Hongxia’s meaning. “So you really intend to follow your shifu’s example and experience Sinner Hall, huh?”

Lu Yang. “...”

Elder Mo Ran, you must have some misunderstanding about me.

“And this is?”

“Her identity cannot be disclosed. You only need to know she has committed theft. Due to special circumstances, she will be confined here during the day but may move freely at night.”

The Moonchaser True Person was concerned about her image and did not wish outsiders to learn that she had transformed into a little girl, so she had requested that Luo Hongxia keep it a secret.

“Someone with connections?” In her thousand years of guarding Sinner Hall, Elder Mo Ran had never seen such a free prisoner.

Luo Hongxia. “...”

How am I supposed to explain this? In a sense, yes, she is someone with connections.

Normally, Elder Mo Ran would be responsible for locking people up, but since Luo Hongxia had come personally, Elder Mo Ran couldn’t be bothered to act. Such an important matter should be handled by the Palace Leader herself.

Just as they entered Sinner Hall, they heard Qu Ling’s resentful voice. “My good disciple, I never imagined you’d dare come here! How dare you imprison your shifu?! Such audacity and impiety!”

“Shut up,” the Moonchaser True Person rebuked her. “Even I must come here when I’ve erred. Who do you think you are?!”

Had anyone else dared speak to Qu Ling like that, she would have flown into a rage long ago. Yet, for some reason, an instinctive fear gripped Qu Ling when this tiny figure berated her, rendering her unable to retaliate.

“Who are you?” Qu Ling scrutinized the Moonchaser True Person with suspicion and uncertainty, not understanding why she feared this little girl.

“You’re not fit to know.”

“You!”

Luo Hongxia shot a sidelong glance at Qu Ling. “Since you are my shifu, I’ll offer you a piece of advice: show this person some respect, or you’ll regret it later.”

Qu Ling snorted coldly and said no more.

“Are you...Fellow Daoist Lu Yang?” Xue Shilou rubbed his eyes, wondering if his recent bloodline awakening had impaired his vision.

Just a few days ago, Fellow Daoist Lu Yang had stood over a meter tall; why is he barely a meter now?

Lu Yang inwardly groaned. I totally forgot about this. I had intended to keep my diminution a secret, but now, Xue Shilou, an outsider, has found out about it.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy tried her best to preserve Lu Yang’s dignity before outsiders. “Ahem, I’m currently cultivating the Eternal Life Immortal Art. Something went awry during my cultivation, so I’ll shrink for a few days each year. The outside world is too dangerous with too many enemies; I’ve come to Sinner Hall to seek refuge and some leisure.”

“So that’s how it is.” Xue Shilou was enlightened. “Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, you must be more careful with your cultivation. This cultivation technique sounds quite dangerous.”

“Is that for real?” Xuanyuan Tianhen didn’t buy it at all.

“Of course it’s true,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said nonchalantly, striving to project the image of an official from the Ministry of Justice inspecting the prison’s environment. However, with Lu Yang’s overly tiny form, no expression or posture he adopted could replicate that demeanor.

Previously, Lu Yang had seen a prisoner locked up for theft. The prisoner had completed his sentence and been released, vacating a spot for the Moonchaser True Person.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stayed next door to the Moonchaser True Person. She made her bed, then gleefully hopped onto it and lay down, feeling a familiar sensation.

“It feels like being in the mental space. It’s not entirely the same, though; the bed in the mental space is more comfortable.”

She closed her eyes, and her consciousness returned to the mental space.

“Xiao Yangzi, come have a snowball fight!”

Lu Yang sighed. “Immortal Fairy, it makes no difference whether you serve prison time.”

Previously, I had commented that the prisoners in Sinner Hall are too low-level. Now, they’re high-level enough—even an immortal has ended up here.

~~~

“Shifu, Lu Yang disappeared after passing by the hot springs? Could something have happened to him?” After not seeing Lu Yang for a full day and night, Lan Ting anxiously sought out Luo Hongxia.

“It’s not exactly that something happened... He’s currently staying in Sinner Hall.”

“Ah? Does that not count as something?” Then Lan Ting understood. It’s because he accidentally entered the hot springs.

I believe Senior Brother Lu Yang must have his reasons for this.

“If you wish to see him, you may visit him in Sinner Hall.” Luo Hongxia felt that this good disciple of hers was a lost cause. I might as well just give her to the Dao-Seeking Sect.
